# Welcome to Hivel | Hivel

![Page cover](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FluolO7UltYX0kNgpsuMe%252FSPEED%2520%281%29.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D743a7009-c92b-40ec-929d-74785603c7ff&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9740759e&sv=2)

Hivel is an intelligence platform providing Software Engineering Leaders with **actionable insights** from Dev Tools, empowering them to unlock their organization's full potential. These insights empower **hi**gh-**vel**ocity teams, and **boost business impact**.

[](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel)

# Welcome to Hivel | Welcome Packet | Hivel

![Page cover](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1678521024-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FxFR2Rv2DoZlYsSKT7aaT%252Fuploads%252FQ6FnCOkJ3NZBL0FQ8T3p%252Fhivel%2520rocket.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc7b2f98-3aa7-45ca-9dcc-371be57dbae1&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e8047fb&sv=2)

Hivel is an intelligence platform providing Software Engineering Leaders with **actionable insights** from Dev Tools, empowering them to unlock their organization's full potential. These insights empower **hi**gh-**vel**ocity teams, and **boost business impact**.

This packet contains the following topics:

1.  Signing up to Hivel
    
2.  Inviting team members to start using Hivel
    
3.  Integrating Hivel with all dev tools you use
    
4.  Best Practices for efficient Software Development
    
5.  Setting and monitoring KPIs in Hivel
    
6.  Case studies on the results customer's have seen with Hivel
    

[NextIntegrating Your Toolschevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/welcome-packet/quick-start-guide/integrating-your-tools)

Last updated 1 year ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Integrating Your Tools | Welcome Packet | Hivel

[](https://hivel.gitbook.io/knowlegebase/integrations/github)

Github

[](https://hivel.gitbook.io/knowlegebase/integrations/gitlab)

Gitlab

# Understanding and Selecting KPIs | Welcome Packet | Hivel

**Understanding KPIs** Key Performance Indicators (KPIs) in Hivel are specific metrics chosen to represent essential aspects of your team’s performance. These indicators provide data-driven insights into areas like speed, quality, and team efficiency.

Hivel categorises KPIs into Speed Metrics, Quality Metrics and Throughput Metrics to give teams a balanced view across these dimensions.

*   Speed Metrics: Cycle Time, Deployment Frequency.
    
*   Quality Metrics: Change Failure Rate, Mean Time to Repair (MTTR), Flashy Reviews, and Large PRs Reviewed
    
*   Throughput Metrics: Commits, PRs Opened, New Work, Active Days
    

**Selecting KPIs**

Start by defining what success looks like for your team. Are you looking to decrease development cycle time? Increase code quality? Identifying objectives helps choose KPIs that align with those goals.

Prioritize based on impact by choosing a manageable set of KPIs that directly impact your team’s objectives. For example:

*   If reducing bottlenecks is essential, Cycle Time and Review Time might be top priorities.
    
*   To improve stability, focus on Change Failure Rate (CFR) and Mean Time to Repair (MTTR).
    
*   To reduce Review Time, focus on Avg. Size of PRs and percentage of PRs over 400 LoC
    
*   To improve on code quality, focus on Flashy Reviews and Rework.
    

[PreviousKPIs in Hivelchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/welcome-packet/kpi-planning/kpis-in-hivel)
[NextConfiguring KPIs in Hivelchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/welcome-packet/kpi-planning/kpis-in-hivel/configuring-kpis-in-hivel)

# Reviewing and Adjusting KPIs | Welcome Packet | Hivel

**Monthly or Quarterly Reviews:**

*   Set up a regular cadence, such as monthly or quarterly reviews, to assess how each KPI aligns with the team’s evolving goals.
    

**Adjust Targets as Needed:**

*   If the team consistently meets a KPI target, consider adjusting the threshold to encourage continuous improvement. Conversely, if a KPI is challenging, adjust the baseline or provide additional resources to help the team meet expectations.
    

**Learning from Outliers:**

*   Use Hivel’s insights feature to investigate outliers and spikes in KPI data. Outliers often reveal bottlenecks or issues that, when addressed, lead to significant performance gains.

# Configuring KPIs in Hivel | Welcome Packet | Hivel

The Goals page allows you to set targets for metrics in Speed, Quality, and Throughput, enabling you to track and assess your team's progress. This guide will help you understand how to view and modify these goals and interpret the progress indicators.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1678521024-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FxFR2Rv2DoZlYsSKT7aaT%252Fuploads%252FZBnemCgXE7ihd5KkSwGi%252FSet%2520goals.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb88b6ee-5114-476e-9108-344e79968afd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a14cfda9&sv=2)

To view the goals against each metric, you can click on "View Goals".

The current value displayed for each metric represents the average value over the last 60 days. This historical data can be helpful when setting new goals.

**Setting or Modifying Goals:**

You can set or modify goals at both the organizational and team levels. Here’s how:

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1678521024-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FxFR2Rv2DoZlYsSKT7aaT%252Fuploads%252FoyHZvqmedXZTt1rivmzu%252FSet%2520Goals.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc780eab5-9807-49a5-a37a-a6a87223d075&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2b4c86d&sv=2)

1.  Click on "Modify" to go ahead and edit the set goals.
    
2.  You can edit the org-level goals from the "Organization" tab. To edit the goals at a team level, switch to "Team" tab and select any particular team.
    
3.  Once done, click on Publish to track your progress against the new goals.
    

**Understanding progress against goals:**

Click on any of the Red/Yellow/Green indicators at the top of the dashboard to highlight the R/Y/G status for all metrics, allowing you to quickly identify areas that need attention.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1678521024-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FxFR2Rv2DoZlYsSKT7aaT%252Fuploads%252FYpn94riXHJqdvfw8YFAR%252FUnderstanding%2520progress%2520to%2520goals.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D732f6b5c-15cb-46ff-b997-bdee45a45d59&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=18aff3c2&sv=2)

The logic behind the R/Y/G is below:

1.  Green = if the current value is 90% or above the goal
    
2.  Yellow = if the current value is between 70% and 90% of the goal
    
3.  Red = if the current value is below 70% of the goal
    

You can also download a CSV report of the Goals and their progress. [Click herearrow-up-right](https://hivel.gitbook.io/knowlegebase/using-hivel/faqs/how-to-download-reports)
 to see how.

If you have any questions or need any more help, please don't hesitate to contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#b9caccc9c9d6cbcdf9d1d0cfdcd597d8d0)
.

[PreviousUnderstanding and Selecting KPIschevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/welcome-packet/kpi-planning/kpis-in-hivel/understanding-and-selecting-kpis)
[NextMonitoring and Tracking KPIschevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/welcome-packet/kpi-planning/kpis-in-hivel/monitoring-and-tracking-kpis)

# Best Practices for Effective KPI Management | Welcome Packet | Hivel

Create a streamlined KPI setup that aligns with your team’s goals and drives performance in meaningful and measurable ways. Regularly reviewing and adjusting these KPIs will help keep your team on track and focused on achieving continuous improvement with Hivel.

*   **Focus on Actionable KPIs:** Only track KPIs that the team can influence directly. This approach keeps the team motivated and engaged.
    
*   **Communicate the importance of KPIs:** Make sure each team member understands why KPIs matter and how their contributions help improve overall performance.
    
*   **Appreciate Progress:** Recognize when the team meets or exceeds KPI targets. Positive reinforcement encourages continued success.
    

[PreviousReviewing and Adjusting KPIschevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/welcome-packet/kpi-planning/kpis-in-hivel/reviewing-and-adjusting-kpis)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1678521024-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FxFR2Rv2DoZlYsSKT7aaT%252Fuploads%252FiwipgLbgynF2cKWt4TkT%252FUnderstanding%2520progress%2520to%2520goals.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D564573f7-3cc9-4246-b580-34d913d413e8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1d3f4f&sv=2)

2.  Yellow = if the current value is between 70% and 90% of the goal
    
3.  Red = if the current value is below 70% of the goal

# Issue Age | Hivel

**Issue Age** is a key metric that provides insight into how long it takes for a team to resolve a ticket or issue, from its creation to its completion. Understanding and optimizing Issue Age is crucial for maintaining a high level of productivity and ensuring customer satisfaction.

circle-info

**Formula:**

Issue Age = Completion Date - Creation Date

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F26TpaG3A28JGzusr7JGE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fcdc105-d627-4405-afd7-c6abe29f1cc2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13a6addb&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/issue-age#example)

**Example**:

*   **Creation Date**: August 1, 2024
    
*   **Completion Date**: August 5, 2024
    
*   **Issue Age**: 4 days
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/issue-age#why-is-issue-age-important)

Why Is Issue Age Important?

Issue Age is a critical metric for several reasons:

*   **Team Efficiency**: A lower Issue Age indicates that your team is resolving issues quickly, which is a sign of efficiency. A higher Issue Age might suggest bottlenecks or delays in the workflow that need to be addressed.
    
*   **Customer Satisfaction**: For customer-facing teams, reducing Issue Age is essential. Faster resolution times lead to higher customer satisfaction and a better overall experience.
    

[PreviousInvestmentchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment)
[NextHow to set up Products & Allocation tabs in the Investment Screen?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/how-to-set-up-products-and-allocation-tabs-in-the-investment-screen)

# How to download reports | Hivel

Downloading reports in CSV format is a convenient way to analyze your data offline. In Hivel, you can download reports from the **Cockpit Pro, Pull Request, and Settings** screens. Below are step-by-step instructions for each type of report.

**Cockpit Pro reports:**

Cockpit Pro reports can be downloaded for data in the Speed, Quality, or Throughput buckets. To pull data from all buckets simultaneously, switch to tabular view and select "All." Here’s how to download a Cockpit report:

1.  Navigate to Cockpit Pro screen.
    
2.  Choose the relevant date range.
    
3.  Apply filters for the desired team, repository, or projects.
    
4.  Switch to tabular view.
    
5.  Under the graphical/tabular option, click on the "Export to CSV" option. The file will be downloaded instantly with the columns and fields as visible in the platform.
    

**Pull Request reports:**

The Pull Request report includes all data available for each PR in the Pull Request screen. Here’s how to download a Pull Request report:

1.  Navigate to Pull Request screen.
    
2.  Apply filters to narrow down the relevant PRs.
    
3.  Click on the "Export CSV" button.
    
4.  The report will be sent to your mail.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit/how-to-download-reports#other-reports)

**Other reports:**

**Settings -> Download Reports:**

You can download 4 kind of reports for the date range and teams that you select:

1.  **Activity** - Number of Active days where the engineers had some Git activity for the selected time period.
    
2.  **Activity (Raw)** - Detailed information on commits and PRs in various stages (merged, reviewed, opened, declined).
    
3.  **Code Base Changes (Raw)** - Summary of codebase changes (across New Work, Rework, and Maintenance) for the selected time period for the selected teams.
    
4.  **Commits part of PR Merged** - Details on commits that are part of PRs merged into the destination branch, including Lines of Changes, Rework, Maintenance, New Work, and other important information.
    
5.  **Goals** - Targets and the values of the metrics based on the frequency.
    

These reports will be sent to your mail, please check your spam folder in case you do not receive it within a few minutes.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FlLOUxm2gvHCtwZRO8YW3%252FScreenshot%25202024-09-10%2520at%25203.17.14%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D714118cb-6c8f-47ae-865e-70ed74e730fb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d3b71da&sv=2)

If you encounter any issues or have further questions, feel free to contact us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#ff8c8a8f8f908d8bbf9796899a93d19e96)
.

[NextMeetings Breakdownchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit/meetings-breakdown)

# How to add Custom fields for Product and Allocation Label in Jira | Hivel

Here are the steps to add custom fields in Jira to map Product and Allocation Label in Hivel:-

1.  **Access Jira Administration**: Log in to Jira as an administrator.
    
2.  After successful login, go to the **Settings** (gear) icon in the top right corner near the profile and click on it. Then, select "Issues" from the dropdown.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhivel.zendesk.com%2Fhc%2Farticle_attachments%2F17619139344669&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fc0db06&sv=2)
    
3.  **Navigate to Custom Fields**: After clicking on "**Issues**" on the left the side panel, under the fields there is "**Custom fields"**, click on it.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhivel.zendesk.com%2Fhc%2Farticle_attachments%2F17619139345949&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e47e51cc&sv=2)
    
4.  **Select Field Type:** Now you will be redirected to select field type; you can select any of the following field types "Select List(single choice)" or "Short Text(plain text only)." Jira offers various types such as text field, select list, date picker, etc.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhivel.zendesk.com%2Fhc%2Farticle_attachments%2F17619139349405&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a2ec45d1&sv=2)
    
5.  **Configure the Field:** Provide a name for the custom field and configure any additional options based on the field type you selected. For example, if you're creating a dropdown select list, you'll need to define the list of options.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fhivel.zendesk.com%2Fhc%2Farticle_attachments%2F17619125679389&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b4133fd&sv=2)
    
6.  **Associate with Screens:** Choose the screens where you want the custom field to appear, preferably all screens, so select all. Screens determine where the field will be displayed when users create or edit issues and update.
    
7.  **Add to Projects:** Now, in the left panel, Click on "Project Settings" and drag and drop all the projects that need those custom fields.
    

**Note:** Repeat the above steps to create additional custom fields if needed. After creating the custom fields, you can add them to the details of the Jira ticket to capture relevant information.

[PreviousHow to set up Products & Allocation tabs in the Investment Screen?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/how-to-set-up-products-and-allocation-tabs-in-the-investment-screen)

# Meetings Breakdown | Hivel

The Meetings Breakdown feature provides an overview of your team's meeting schedules, helping you identify if they're overwhelmed by excessive long meetings.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fn4e1ueeMat8FGsLXkCH2%252FScreenshot%25202024-09-10%2520at%25203.22.19%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8344f5f8-6fa7-4400-87bd-20154f4bcebc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fef782b&sv=2)

This feature can be accessed while creating a new custom dashboard or by navigating to the custom dashboards page -> selecting any metric -> "Meetings Breakdown" from the dropdown.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FqSA7Yv2bp2Y2OGx1oJy6%252FGIF%2520Recording%2520Sept%252010%2520%281%29.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dacbecfd9-e765-4edb-bf8b-08bbbbf7280a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8eb7c760&sv=2)

_Accessing from within a metric_

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FPYl1pD1wKXetqlUHDfqB%252FGIF%2520Recording%2520Sept%252010%2520from%2520Jumpshare.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1700354c-091b-4b82-bd1b-5d110b6fb49f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf9a3a0f&sv=2)

_Adding the metric as part of new dashboard creation_

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit/meetings-breakdown#the-total-time-spent-is-broken-down-into-the-following-categories-of-meetings)

The total time spent is broken down into the following categories of meetings:

1. **Deep** \- If the gap between two meetings is more than 2 hours, it's considered Deep work. This allows developers to focus on their tasks without interruption. _Ideally majority of the developers' time should be in this category._

2. **Shallow** - When the gap between two meetings is less than 2 hours, it's classified as Shallow work, as frequent meetings require context switching.

3. **Private** - All meetings marked as Private in Google Calendar or personal time blocks fall under this category.

4. **Team** - These are meetings with three or more people from the same organization.

5. **External** - Meetings that include at least one person from outside the organization.

6. **One\_On\_One** - Meetings involving just two people from the same organization.

You can filter this data based on specific teams and dates to gain the insights you need.

If google calendar is not integrated with Hivel yet, please follow the steps mentioned [herearrow-up-right](https://hivel.zendesk.com/hc/en-in/articles/19341040186909-How-to-integrate-Google-Calendar-in-Hivel)
.

If you encounter any issues or have further questions, feel free to contact us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a9dadcd9d9c6dbdde9c1c0dfccc587c8c0)
.

[PreviousHow to download reportschevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit/how-to-download-reports)
[NextInvestmentchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Pull Request | Hivel

Pull Requests are the holy grail of any software development process, and getting a 360-degree view into them, and the ability to filter to see the PRs that may require your attention is necessary.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request#you-can-use-data-on-this-screen-to)

You can use data on this screen to:

*   Consistently get a view of the process, proactively coach the team and remind them of your best practices or SLA.
    
*   Show the reviewer reviewing most PRs and schedule a knowledge-sharing session.
    
*   Look at the PRs that are open for longer, and clear roadblocks to push them to production.
    
*   If your average cycle time is higher than expected, you can look at the PRs or engineers swinging the most toward this number.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request#major-metrics-and-what-they-mean)

Major metrics and what they mean

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F3vMk2TJKmkc5fOMpNi0m%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D20431abf-bf69-4eef-a6b2-06e99395d81e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8d1267c3&sv=2)

1.  **Release Merge Frequency** is the total number of PRs merged to release branch in that selected time period/total number of days in the selected time period.
    
2.  **Hotfix Rate** is the number of hotfix PRs merged to release branch over the total number of PRs merged to release branch.
    
3.  **Hotfix Resolution Rate** shows the average cycle time of the hotfix PRs.
    
4.  **Unreviewed PRs** gives the number of PRs that were merged without any approval.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request#other-metrics-and-filters)

**Other metrics and filters:**

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FSerHpsr8pY9649PHoCqN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e4f7e4e-f605-4fb3-b329-372594871bd3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a7e628fb&sv=2)

*   **Unaccounted Work** includes all PRs that are not linked to Jira or any other project management tool's tickets.
    
*   **Ready to Review** shows all PRs that are open and are pending a review or approval.
    
*   **Ready to Merge** shows all PRs that have been approved and are awaiting merge.
    
*   **PRs > 400 LoC** helps you track larger PRs over a certain number of lines of code in the selected time period. The larger the PR, the slower it moves through the review cycle and the higher the probability of bugs.
    
    *   The threshold of 400 LoC is modifiable from Configurations screen.
        
    
*   **Cycle time > 5 days** shows all PRs merged in that time period with cycle time greater than 5 days.
    
    *   The threshold of 5 days is modifiable from Configurations screen.
        
    
*   **Flashy Review** is used to identify PRs which were reviewed very fast and indicate ineffective review. By default PRs > 200 LoC with a review time < 5minutes, are considered flashy, [but this is configurable](https://docs.hivel.ai/configurations/branch-configurations#flashy-review)
    .
    

[PreviousHow to add Custom fields for Product and Allocation Label in Jirachevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/how-to-add-custom-fields-for-product-and-allocation-label-in-jira)
[NextComments Categorizationchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/comments-categorization)

Last updated 3 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# How to set up Products & Allocation tabs in the Investment Screen? | Hivel

Hivel's Products and Allocation feature helps you see where your team's efforts are going. It shows how resources are split across your products through Jira tickets. By mapping your custom Jira labels in Hivel, you can get a clear picture of this distribution and make smarter investment decisions. Let’s walk through how to set this up.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FIkIXrQmFkVaU2RwTkLbm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3fb0d152-dc8d-4c14-8db6-84a7af3e61cf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9192080e&sv=2)

_Product section_

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FneVqqtokkWRyXYL6mBiI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2ba85a82-7f3a-4cde-acec-2f071d887c3c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a74e6716&sv=2)

_Allocation section_

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/how-to-set-up-products-and-allocation-tabs-in-the-investment-screen#to-populate-the-graphs-hivel-requires-information-about-two-custom-fields)

**To populate the graphs**, Hivel requires information about two custom fields:

*   **Product/Projects:** This field categorizes work into distinct product lines or projects in ways you may want to monitor effort spread across projects. Examples include Payments, Data Engineering, Checkout, AI, and Compliance.
    
*   **Work Type:** This field categorizes tasks based on their nature or purpose such as OKRs, initiatives and more. Examples include Roadmap, Tech Debt, R&D, Customer Success, KTLO (Keep the Lights On), etc.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F3ErkhMLLGcubbilIKePn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44b067fa-6f80-4ce5-8971-94fe19e73655&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2caafab6&sv=2)

These custom fields enable better organization and tracking of tasks within the Hivel platform, allowing teams to effectively manage their work and visualize progress across different product lines and types of work.

Please note that we can use any name for the above that you may be or prefer using internally.

circle-info

If you don't have the custom fields set up on Jira yet, you can [**follow the instructions here**](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/how-to-add-custom-fields-for-product-and-allocation-label-in-jira)
 to create them.

**Once you have custom fields**, follow these steps:

1.  **Go to Settings screen**
    
2.  Under Investment Configuration, set the 2 custom fields for Product and Allocation.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FlFiMh4Iwk1cbTdCpcXRz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9031cd92-bbb1-492b-9474-72b8e108ed15&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2ff0ad84&sv=2)
    

That's it, all done!

The new data will be within 24 hours.

In case the data does not show up, please reach out to [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#c6b5b3b6b6a9b4b286aeafb0a3aae8a7af)
.

[PreviousIssue Agechevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/issue-age)
[NextHow to add Custom fields for Product and Allocation Label in Jirachevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/how-to-add-custom-fields-for-product-and-allocation-label-in-jira)

# Cockpit | Hivel

Cockpit is your centralized command center for engineering insights. It brings together all your boards and templates into a streamlined view, making it easy to track key engineering metrics, explore trends, and derive insights without jumping across multiple screens.

With quick access to favorites, flexible filtering, drilldowns across time and teams, Cockpit helps you move from high-level visibility to actionable understanding in just a few clicks.

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit#key-features)

Key features


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit#unified-view-of-boards-and-templates)

Unified View of Boards & Templates

*   Access **all created boards** and **Hivel-provided templates** in a single place.
    
*   Easily differentiate between **private boards**, **public boards**, and **templates** with clear visual indicators.
    

**Favorites & Quick Access**

**Pin frequently used boards** to the side menu for instant access.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fhpgkf8phOMBxbNOC0Kz1%252FGoogle%2520Keep%2520Note.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb45b456-29a5-4c9f-8639-e368d2324594&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=88c0bc4d&sv=2)

**Metrics list**

**Hover over any template card** to quickly view a list of all metrics included in the board.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FYjlEwMLJQCNz84ZreN0K%252FGoogle%2520Keep%2520Note%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f929609-4857-4f5a-ba08-5a4bde3287c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1dd70b3d&sv=2)

**Board Ownership**

See **who created a board and when it was created** for better tracking and collaboration.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FDNdmeuYlPDyJTUUFKSv3%252FGoogle%2520Keep%2520Note%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f70008b-c5f8-4d88-91d9-c28fdde704e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ca232b9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit#features-available-for-the-boards)

Features available for the boards


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit#create-your-own-board-for-set-of-metrics-and-save-filters)

Create your own board for set of metrics and save filters

*   Navigate to '**All Boards**', Click the '**Create dashboard**' button, and create your customized board by giving the board name, description, and type of board.
    
*   Select the metrics and click on '**Apply Changes**.'
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FdoayQXbCMt7GDH3YFqU8%252FScreen%2520Cast%25202026-01-30%2520at%252012.15.16%2520PM.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a72ba7f-35d3-46e8-8923-17d18d1d8e7b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e33519c&sv=2)

*   You can tailor the dashboard to your liking and select a single team, multiple teams, one repository, or a group of repositories.
    
*   Choose a specific date range to focus on the period that is most relevant to your analysis.
    
*   Click on the '**Save Filter**' button, give the filter name, and save it for future reference.
    
*   Upon saving, the filter's unique URL is automatically updated in the browser’s address bar.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FcxtgkXa9jQHrTBxqHVp9%252FScreen%2520Cast%25202026-01-30%2520at%252012.19.39%2520PM.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2b24845-29cf-45c6-93a5-77678b32a966&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=75138dc7&sv=2)

*   Remember to copy the URL from the address bar for future use or to share it with your team.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit#drilldown-from-quarterly-to-daily-levels)

**Drilldown from Quarterly to Daily Levels**

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FSdKHX7t1R9CxqrLNRbFM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c13d75e-c832-4458-95b5-0061e43157b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6632fbf&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FNmxEQu72JRlCfFXrQmyP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e334dac-fd8a-46e8-a870-8cfce453b0f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7770d1ea&sv=2)

*   Start at a quarterly overview and **drill down into monthly, weekly, or daily trends** for deeper insights.
    
*   View pull requests (PRs) related to specific time periods for better traceability and exclude outliers.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F9UQY6RkxfIubnTcEneT5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D912e3a12-2123-4c02-93ca-2df9df750967&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70fb460f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit#dashboard-access-and-permissions)

Dashboard Access & Permissions

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FUYkv0DVDLiozImUOehUJ%252FGoogle%2520Keep%2520Note%2520%284%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78d887dc-a0c3-4f75-a503-6c8ed3203def&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f01a0ef6&sv=2)

*   **Public Dashboards:** Visible to everyone in the organization, but only the owner can modify them.
    
*   **Private Dashboards:** Only the owner can view, edit, and delete them.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit#workspaces-and-team-views)

Workspaces & Team Views

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F5SHIbRB8FP7x89XoeEgE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D676e0c85-e076-4d4d-a31b-484cc470976e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94c69fb9&sv=2)

*   If [Workspaces are enabled from the configuration](https://docs.hivel.ai/configurations/general-configurations)
    , users can view the combination of both Teams and Workspaces for a more structured and categorized view of performance metrics.
    
*   This allows for **cross-team and cross-workspace comparisons**, helping organizations track performance across different projects and initiatives.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit#side-by-side-team-comparison)

Side-by-Side Team Comparison

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F1XNOM6sAQLVZe1foQhi6%252FGoogle%2520Keep%2520Note%2520%283%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da794c86a-ff87-4ee5-9cb2-5045e012e3d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f49461fe&sv=2)

*   Compare **selected teams side by side** to **analyze performance trends over time**.
    
*   Easily track progress across multiple teams and benchmark their efficiency, cycle time, and other critical metrics.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit#tv-mode)

**TV Mode:**

You can select the TV icon at the top right corner to switch the dashboard display to TV mode, optimizing it for larger screens.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FG43HPH2A1XGSfFECqeje%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00b1ad57-06e5-435f-bee6-42042bcc661e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21e9a4b9&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit#download-report)

**Download Report:**

Next to the TV view icons, find the ‘**Download** ’icons. Click on this to download an image of the currently displayed graph or chart for offline reference.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F5QqemVYdIzifxdDQsY7f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6915abe4-c994-4da9-a1b5-25f4b64bfff8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2be8c5d0&sv=2)

For further guidance or support with Custom Dashboards, feel free to reach out to our support team at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#84f7f1f4f4ebf6f0c4ecedf2e1e8aae5ed)
.

# How to exclude outlier commits and PRs? | Hivel

Are some known outliers (like extra large commits) skewing your average metrics? Fear not, you can exclude them from your reports easily. Here's how -

Click the **Exclude button**![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FJ5lakWkMXjiOlGRcs7Ri%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8e11539a-0882-4cb6-84ed-a3091a546111&width=38&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a53ebc9&sv=2) on the

*   right panel in Process screen to exclude a PR.
    
*   right panel in Coding screen to exclude a Commit.
    
*   "PR size" column in Pull Request screen to exclude a PR.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FtjAaC7CfM2sijBCenz49%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34940921-d0d7-48c8-83db-3894a2d71f14&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48d1b894&sv=2)

*   All screens will be **updated instantly**. Only Cockpit will take 24 hours to reflect the change.
    
*   You can also **include** a PR/commit after it's been excluded by clicking on the![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FBVcSARjzqdOF7kRfhWAh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da224fa32-c99e-4eb9-ac78-35eab2057dee&width=40&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d89d945d&sv=2)icon in the **Excluded Items** section in Settings page.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FedYaiJgnxjv2AifGzByU%252FScreenshot%25202024-09-10%2520at%25204.06.03%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6b4d205-6caf-4eb2-9858-b4b41e7faf6b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=373f3a9a&sv=2)

# Process | Hivel

The Process Screen in Hivel gives you a visual breakdown of your cycle time—from writing code to merging it into production. This view is designed to help you identify bottlenecks, track engineering efficiency, and make data-driven improvements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/process#view-the-prs-behind-any-metric)

🔍 View the PRs Behind Any Metric

Click on any metric to instantly see the pull requests contributing to it. Noticed a spike? Just click on that time frame to view the PRs involved.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/process#dive-into-pr-details)

**Dive Into PR Details**

Drill down into you version control and see the tickets associated with the PR. This gives you a clear picture of where time is being spent and who’s involved.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/process#identify-bottlenecks)

⚠️ Identify Bottlenecks

See how long each stage took for a specific PR. This helps you pinpoint where delays occur—whether it's extended coding time, slow reviews, or lag in merging.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/process#clean-up-outliers)

🧹 Clean Up Outliers

If a spike is expected or due to a known outlier, you can **exclude specific PRs** from the board. This ensures your averages stay accurate and meaningful.

**You can use data on this screen to:**

*   See the stage at which your team is spending most of their time - coding, review, or release process.
    
*   Averages could sometimes be deceiving, so check the right panel for all the PRs and their respective breakdown into various stages.
    
*   You can look at your current sprints or past sprints and use this data during retrospectives.
    

circle-info

Refer [here](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/how-to-exclude-outlier-commits-and-prs)
 to know how to exclude certain PRs and commits from the calculation.

[PreviousHow to exclude outlier commits and PRs?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/how-to-exclude-outlier-commits-and-prs)
[NextGoalschevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/goals)

Last updated 11 months ago

*   [🔍 View the PRs Behind Any Metric](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/process#view-the-prs-behind-any-metric)
    
*   [Dive Into PR Details](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/process#dive-into-pr-details)
    
*   [⚠️ Identify Bottlenecks](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/process#identify-bottlenecks)
    
*   [🧹 Clean Up Outliers](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/process#clean-up-outliers)

# Review Cycles | Hivel

A review cycle is defined as the sequence of comments and commits within a PR. Each cycle is counted when a comment or request for change is followed by a commit or approved by someone. This cycle can repeat multiple times, indicating multiple review cycles within the same PR.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F6mcADUvBpZMFeIXPiZze%252FScreenshot%25202024-09-10%2520at%25203.59.35%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28c7ba24-4238-468a-98ca-5a12ae52ea76&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=589ec9be&sv=2)

circle-info

_This field can be found in the PR screen as a column._

Understanding the review cycle count helps in assessing the thoroughness and efficiency of the review process. High review cycle counts might indicate thorough reviews or potential issues in the code requiring multiple revisions, whereas low counts might suggest either fewer issues or potentially less thorough reviews.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/review-cycles#below-is-the-explanation-on-how-it-gets-calculated)

Below is the explanation on how it gets calculated:

1. **Review Cycle = 0** - If a pull request has neither comments nor approval, the review cycle count is 0.

2. **Review Cycle = 1** - If a pull request has been approved with or without comments, the review cycle count is 1. This accounts for the fact that some form of review has taken place (the approval), even if no comments were left.

`_**Example**_` A PR is created and a reviewer approves it without leaving any comments. Then review cycle count is 1 because the PR was reviewed (approved) even though no comments were made.

3. **Review Cycle is more than 1** - For pull requests with both comments and commits, the review cycle count is calculated based on the number of comment-commit pairs. Each sequence where a comment is followed by a commit is counted as one review cycle. This means that for each set of comments followed by a commit, the review cycle count increases.

`_**Example**_` A PR is created, and a reviewer leaves comments. The developer makes changes and commits those changes. This sequence repeats. - _**Result**_: The review cycle count is incremented for each comment-commit pair. - 1st Cycle: Reviewer comments -> Developer commits changes (Cycle 1) - 2nd Cycle: Reviewer comments again -> Developer commits changes again (Cycle 2) - The review cycle count is the number of these comment-commit sequences.

If you encounter any issues or have further questions, feel free to contact us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9deee8ededf2efe9ddf5f4ebf8f1b3fcf4)
.

[PreviousComments Categorizationchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/comments-categorization)
[NextHow to exclude outlier commits and PRs?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/how-to-exclude-outlier-commits-and-prs)

Last updated 1 year ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Investment | Hivel

The Investment Screen provides a detailed view of your team's efforts as tracked in Jira issues. It is divided into four sections, each offering specific insights into different aspects of your team's work:

[**Issue**](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#h_01hywypcmca37vt49c4764ms90)
 | [**Epic**](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#id-01hywzfvmctbkdjc1x2wn46w6h)
 | [**Product and Allocation**](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#id-01hywzmp6s17w4s3z0h4ks82cj)
 | [**Delivery**](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#id-01hyx089atjhwfc8anp8q73ajw)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#h_01hyx2e4t4s1edt663bwbjq25b)

**Sections:**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#h_01hywypcmca37vt49c4764ms90)

**Issue**

*   Gain visibility into the volume of issues or story points per sprint and issue type. This helps you assess whether your team is working within capacity or if there is room for improvement
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FfFtuqhi7tvNCJHKvIHnp%252FInvst%25201.1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6eb58269-1ddc-48b2-8c3b-cb3e6d4f763b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6546418b&sv=2)

1.  **Filter on issuetypes:** Click on any issue type to filter the graph data to only that issue type. The available issue types will be based on the issues created in your Jira project and board.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FCpDXU3G0EH2vj0z9yNgN%252FInvst%25202.1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d296732-a162-48ae-89b2-e2df809c68c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7964a354&sv=2)

1.  **Filter to identify missing hygiene:** You can apply additional filters such as "Missing Epics," "Missing Assignee," and "Missing Story Points" to identify issues with missing hygiene and ensure they are updated for proper tracking.
    

circle-info

All the sections in Investment follow a similar above behaviour of filtering on issuetype, sprints and arriving at the drilldown.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#id-01hywzfvmctbkdjc1x2wn46w6h)

**Epic**

*   This section provides visibility into the volume of tickets and story points at both the Epic and sprint levels. It helps you understand the efforts spent on specific Epics within each sprint.
    
*   Similar to the Issue section, you can drill down into issues by clicking on a sprint and filter by selecting a particular Epic from the available options.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FE3M9Be8rSGEJmv5rRY2G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41b032b4-93c3-4ad7-9adc-d6c9a1c0ae4a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28bb0297&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#id-01hywzmp6s17w4s3z0h4ks82cj)

**Product and Allocation**

Hivel's Products and Allocation sections helps you see where your team's efforts are going. It shows how resources are split across your products through Jira tickets. By mapping your custom Jira labels in Hivel, you can get a clear picture of this distribution and make smarter investment decisions.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FlhdtXMWaM0JtSq7l9qRP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d74882b-cdc1-4d58-ace8-6b8a377f1f3a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ae81e7a3&sv=2)

_Products section_

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FYcKm3w7flqxzhOG21pwJ%252FScreenshot%25202024-09-10%2520at%25203.43.25%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3524d6d8-152d-428d-8c13-cd748629ef6c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5d6c37e&sv=2)

_Allocation section_

For more information on how to set up this functionality, please refer to [this article](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/how-to-set-up-products-and-allocation-tabs-in-the-investment-screen)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#id-01hyx089atjhwfc8anp8q73ajw)

**Delivery**

The **Delivery Accuracy** graphs offer insights into the completion rate of planned efforts within a sprint and highlight any unplanned items that were addressed, as well as any delays encountered.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FexE5QPFZ2d80eofUDdSY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D296c4aae-e06c-434b-be26-2e739480142a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=978e04aa&sv=2)

The delivery bar chart data is categorized into two main sections: Completed and Spillover. Each section is further divided into Planned and Unplanned.

*   **Completed** : Issues/Story Points completed before the sprint closes.
    
*   **Spillover** : Issues/Story Points not completed by the time the sprint closes.
    
*   **Planned** : Issues/Story Points created before the sprint starts.
    
*   **Unplanned** : Issues/Story Points created after the sprint starts.
    

**Delivery Trend**

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FRcZ2imf7mh9THfJpOkYG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D434ced4e-3f3a-4ead-84ae-eca12a9c439e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=32de8b7d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#delivery-trend)

Delivery Trend

The **Delivery Trend** chart helps you track and evaluate your team’s sprint execution by combining two key metrics:

1\. **Say-Do Ratio**

This measures the accuracy of sprint planning by comparing what was **committed at the start of the sprint** to what was **actually delivered**.

*   **Formula:** `(Work Delivered from Sprint Start / Work Committed at Sprint Start) × 100`
    
*   **What it means:**
    
    *   A **high Say-Do Ratio** (>100%) could indicate **significant ad-hoc work** is being added and completed, possibly reducing focus on planned items.
        
    *   A **low Say-Do Ratio** (<100%) suggests that the team is **overcommitting** or **facing blockers**, pointing to potential areas where expectations or planning should be adjusted.
        
    

* * *

2\. **Delivery Rate**

This measures how much of the **total work taken up during the sprint -** both planned and ad-hoc - was actually delivered.

*   **Formula:** `(Total Work Delivered / Total Work Taken Up in Sprint) × 100`
    
*   **What it means:**
    
    *   Always shown as a percentage out of 100%.
        
    *   A **high Delivery Rate** indicates effective throughput, regardless of how work entered the sprint.
        
    *   A **low Delivery Rate** may signal capacity issues, scope creep, or blockers mid-sprint.
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#why-both-metrics-matter)

🧠 Why Both Metrics Matter

When used together, **Say-Do Ratio** and **Delivery Rate** provide a fuller picture of sprint health:

*   If both metrics are **high**, the team is likely performing well and adapting effectively.
    
*   If **Delivery Rate is high but Say-Do Ratio is low**, the team is completing work but not sticking to the original plan (possible unplanned work).
    
*   If **both are low**, the team may be overcommitting or facing blockers that need investigation.
    
*   If **Say-Do Ratio is high but Delivery Rate is low**, it might indicate too much ad-hoc work was started but not completed.
    

Use these insights to improve sprint planning, manage expectations, and identify areas where the team may need support or process adjustments.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment#h_01hzf0crtvgz5rkv4ha91qk0bk)

**Filters:**

In each of the sections, there are certain filters that can be applied to reflect only the relevant data:

*   **Boards/Sub boards** : Boards refer to Jira Projects and Sub boards refer to the boards inside a Jira project. You can select only one Board at a time, but you can select any number of Sub boards within that Board. All subsequent filters will apply on the selected Boards/Sub board filter.
    
*   **Sprints** _(only for Issue, Epic, and Delivery sections)_ : Use this filter to display data based on specific sprints. By default, the latest 5 sprints will be selected.
    
*   **Assignees** _(only for Issue, Epic, and Delivery sections)_ : To filter out data for the Assignees of Jira tickets.
    
*   **Tickets/Story Points** : Choose to view the data as either the count of tickets or the sum of story points.
    
*   **Date filter** (_only for Product and Allocation sections)_ : Filter the Product and Allocation data for a specified time period.
    

For more information or assistance, please contact our support team at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#97e4e2e7e7f8e5e3d7fffee1f2fbb9f6fe)
.

[PreviousMeetings Breakdownchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit/meetings-breakdown)
[NextIssue Agechevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/investment/issue-age)

# Comments Categorization | Hivel

**Explainer Video:**

The "Comments Category" column in the Pull Requests tab is an AI-powered feature that automatically analyzes and categorizes comments into specific labels based on their content.

This feature helps you quickly understand the overall sentiment and focus of the comments within each pull request, making it easier to address issues and manage code reviews.

**We categorize the Pull request in the below categories:**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/comments-categorization#type-1)

**Type 1:**

*   _**LGTM**__:_ PRs that are merged without significant issues or objections i.e. comments indicating approval, positive feedback on the implementation, or minor suggestions that are quickly addressed without major revisions.
    
    *   _For example, "Great job! This looks perfect and works as expected."_
        
    
*   _**Refactor**__:_ PRs that need significant changes to improve code quality or structure before they can be merged i.e. comments suggesting extensive changes, restructuring, or optimization of the code.
    
    *   _For example, "The algorithm here can be optimized for better performance."_
        
    
*   _**Buggy**__:_ PRs that introduce new bugs or issues into the codebase i.e. comments highlighting bugs, regressions, or issues that break existing functionality.
    
    *   _For example, "This change breaks the login functionality."_
        
    
*   _**Controversial**__:_ PRs that generate significant debate or disagreement among reviewers i.e. comments that show differing opinions or disputes on the implementation, approach, or necessity of the changes.
    
    *   _For example, "I don't think this approach is the best solution."_
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/comments-categorization#type-2)

**Type 2:**

*   _**Code Quality**__:_ Comments focused on the overall design, architecture, and cleanliness of the code i.e. feedback related to code organization, modularity, adherence to design patterns, and overall structural improvements.
    
    *   _For example, "This module should be broken down into smaller, more manageable components."_
        
    
*   _**Readability**__:_ Comments aimed at improving the readability of the code and the adequacy of its documentation i.e. feedback about code clarity, naming conventions, comments within the code, and the presence and quality of documentation.
    
    *   _For example, "Variable names should be more descriptive."_
        
    
*   _**Testing**__:_ Comments that address the sufficiency and quality of tests and error handling mechanisms. Suggestions or concerns regarding unit tests, integration tests, error handling, edge cases, and the robustness of the code against failures.
    
    *   _For example, "Error handling is not sufficient here; consider adding more checks."_
        
    
*   _**Compliance**__:_ Comments that ensure the code adheres to industry standards, coding guidelines, and best practices i.e. feedback on adherence to coding standards, security practices, regulatory compliance, and the use of recommended libraries or frameworks.
    
    *   _For example, "This code doesn't comply with our security guidelines."_
        
    
*   _**Maintainability:**_ Comments that focus on the long-term maintenance and scalability of the code. Suggestions for making the code easier to maintain, extending its functionality, or improving performance to handle larger scale or more complex operations.
    
    *   _For example, "This code will be hard to maintain; consider refactoring."_
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/comments-categorization#type-3-special-cases-for-categorization)

**Type 3: Special Cases for Categorization:**

*   When a comment consists of a single word, it is categorized as a _"__**One Word Comment**__"_.
    
*   If a pull request has no comments, it is categorized as _"__**No Comment**__"_.
    
*   When a pull request cannot be categorized based on its comments due to various reasons, it is categorised as _**"No Value"**_.
    

**Wherever applicable, each PR will be categorized into either one or two of the above types. For example -**

*   "Looks good to me. Well done on keeping the code clean and efficient!"
    
    *   Categories: _**LGTM, Code Quality**_
        
    
*   “Consider refactoring this function to reduce its complexity and improve readability.”
    
    *   Categories: _**Refactor, Readability**_
        
    
*   “There's a bug in the validation logic. Please fix it before merging”
    
    *   Categories: _**Buggy**_
        
    
*   "Looks good to me. Well done on keeping the code clean and efficient!" "Can you add more comments to this section for better understanding?"
    
    *   Categories: _**LGTM, Readability**_
        
    
*   "There's a bug in the validation logic. Please fix it before merging." "Make sure to add unit tests to cover this scenario."
    
    *   Categories: _**Buggy, Testing**_
        
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fyl69xDZplcuJ9FcR9y5S%252FScreenshot%25202024-09-10%2520at%25203.56.22%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D20953499-f9a9-4630-a4c5-94f653afba73&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9bca0986&sv=2)

_Examples_

**Please note:** For this feature to work, we process the metadata through AI.

If you cannot see this column in the Pull Request screen, please contact our support team at [\[email protected\]arrow-up-right](https://support@hivel.ai/)

[PreviousPull Requestchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request)
[NextReview Cycleschevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/review-cycles)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Coding | Hivel

As we all may agree that engineering productivity cannot be measured by lines of code, it’s important to gain visibility into the percentage of code spent across various categories - **New Work**, **Maintenance**, and **Rework**.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FVfUtnbzlcDWhhcfk8Nqf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65de74f0-a55f-4907-bd6b-d3145d97e85b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2484e49f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/coding#every-line-of-code-is-classified-into-3-categories-as-explained-below)

**Every line of code is classified into 3 categories, as explained below:**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/coding#new-work)

New Work

New Work is the amount of work newly created, or in other words launching new features. Every new line of code that’s written is called New Work and this measures the innovation percentage spent by the team.

**How to use this data on a regular basis?**

*   When the business is aiming to focus on innovation, watch out this space if the efforts are being put in the right direction
    
*   Do you have a complex legacy project and delivering new features is being delayed? This metric can show you to make your strategic move.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/coding#rework)

Rework

Rework as the name suggests is working on something, and then modifying or deleting it. But, there’s a catch. Anything we build ought to be modified/deleted, but doing so within 30 days of writing the code originally is what’s classified as rework.

Why 30 days? Most agile teams have a 2 - 3 week sprint cycle and a code rewritten within 30 days can cover all possible cases of rework listed here.

**What are the causes for rework?**

*   You write it first, and then polish it for performance or ease of maintenance
    
*   Fix features based on bugs reported in QA or Prod
    
*   Deliver the feature and then learn about changing scope or requirements
    
*   Or, something works on your local, but throws errors when integrated with systems
    

While a certain amount of rework is normal for any team, watching out for increased rework in a given time can help address issues earlier in the process.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/coding#maintenance)

Maintenance

Maintenance or refactoring or tech debt is required for any teams and is classified as code that’s modified/deleted which was originally written prior to 30 days.

While most teams take time to work on tech debt, it’s inevitable to modify some old code while building new features. It’s helpful to watch the repos/projects causing most maintenance, monitor ROI of such projects and take up corrective actions.

**What are the causes for maintenance?**

*   Complex architecture can make building new features harder without touching old code
    
*   Update applications to newer technologies or changing business requirements
    
*   Reduce code-bloat by removing unnecessary features/code that’s not in use anymore.
    

circle-info

For a more detailed explanation on how New Work, Rework, and Maintenance work, please refer to [**this article**](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/coding/understanding-rework-new-work-and-maintenance)
.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/coding#how-to-use-this-data-on-a-regular-basis)

**How to use this data on a regular basis?**

The first step is to baseline the numbers for each team to see the percentage of new work, rework, maintenance and collaboration. And then, monitor for trends to see if the team’s work is reflecting your initiatives and goals.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/coding#what-can-be-a-few-things-to-watch-out-for)

**What can be a few things to watch out for?**

High maintenance could be a signal for tech debt. High rework can be a signal to demand better requirements.

circle-info

Refer [here](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/pull-request/how-to-exclude-outlier-commits-and-prs)
 to know how to exclude certain PRs and commits from the calculation.

[PreviousGoalschevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/goals)
[NextUnderstanding Rework, New Work, and Maintenancechevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/coding/understanding-rework-new-work-and-maintenance)

Last updated 1 month ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# How are Active Days calculated | Hivel

For this calculation, we consider any GIT activity, such as regular commits, merge commits, and PRs opened, reviewed, merged, and declined. The **active day value** indicates, on average, how many days out of a seven-day week a person or team has been active. Weekends are included in the calculation to ensure any work that happens during that time is also accounted for.

circle-info

If the duration is >= 7 : **Active days** \=(CurrentActiveDays / (Selected time frame) / CurrentActiveAuthors) \* 7 If the duration is < 7 : **Active days** =(CurrentActiveDays / (Selected time frame) / CurrentActiveAuthors) \*1

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F0WY3zMmIY1kTpZJH0box%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2a35259-5bc0-4f32-9e39-9d4dd7b20e78&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=731cd435&sv=2)

Active days on Cockpit

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FV0BSWj831wdFlUcFv7El%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6582260-062a-4aa0-9a51-06c47cbcdd81&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2b50631f&sv=2)

Active days on Activity screen

**For example:** (Time frame: February 1st - 10th)

*   If the team worked for 10 days in February, and you have 3 active authors contributing to the work. Active days = (10/10/3) \* 7 = 2.3
    
*   If the team worked for only 5 days in February, and you have 2 active authors contributing. • Active days = (5/10/2) \* 1 = 0.25
    

[PreviousNew Work%chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/metrics-and-definitions/throughput/new-work)
[NextPRs Open, PRs Ready to Review or Mergechevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/metrics-and-definitions/throughput/prs-open-prs-ready-to-review-or-merge)

# Dev360 | Hivel

The Dev360 screen provides a comprehensive monthly view of a developer's activity in terms of GIT activities. This screen is particularly useful for gaining insights into the active days and throughput of a developer, which can be valuable during one-on-one discussions.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fr7FWV3kGCDuV1sNK0xYl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ffdc988-323e-4755-84a6-f6a8ccaddd64&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21cd7ca2&sv=2)

This screen shows the number of days a developer was involved in any GIT activity, such as commits, PRs (Pull Requests) opened, reviewed, merged, or declined. This visibility helps in understanding a developer's engagement and productivity over a given period.

**Filtering Activities:** You can filter the view based on specific activities like Commits, PRs Reviewed, etc.

**Detailed View:** Clicking on any bubble within the filtered view will provide basic details of that particular activity and a link to it.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/dev360#filters-available-in-dev360)

Filters Available in Dev360

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/dev360#general-filters)

General Filters

*   **Teams**: Select the relevant team to filter the developers accordingly.
    
*   **Users**: Choose the specific user to view their activities.
    
*   **Date**: Set the desired date period to see activities within that timeframe.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/dev360#activity-specific-filters)

Activity-Specific Filters

*   **Commits**: Shows all regular commits done by the user within the selected date period.
    
*   **Merge Commits**: Displays merge commits done by the user in the selected date period.
    
*   **PRs Open**: Filters out the PRs that were opened by the user within the selected date period.
    
*   **PRs Reviewed**: Lists the PRs reviewed by the user during the selected date period.
    
*   **PRs Merged**: Shows the PRs merged by the user within the selected date period.
    
*   **PRs Declined**: Filters out the PRs that were declined by the user in the selected date period.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/dev360#how-to-get-to-dev-360)

How to get to Dev 360

There are 2 ways in which you can access Dev360:

1.  Straight from the main Hivel left panel.
    
2.  By selecting one user in Activity or Cockpit.
    

[PreviousTeam Pulsechevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/team-pulse)
[NextWork Item Breakdownchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/work-item-breakdown)

Last updated 6 months ago

# Goals | Hivel

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/goals#using-goals-in-hivel)

🎯 Using Goals in Hivel


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Goals** feature in Hivel helps you set clear targets, track progress, and assess performance at both the **organization** and **team** levels. Whether you're aligning teams around strategic objectives or tracking key performance metrics, Goals provides the visibility and accountability to stay on track.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FDq4KgWMVM2Xddqep0Wi1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa1a23f9-9558-4764-a366-c6faa4f4fa71&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2362ec28&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/goals#where-to-find-goals)

📍 Where to Find Goals

You can access Goals Pro from the main navigation:

> **Overview → Goals (pro)**

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/goals#creating-an-organization-level-goal)

🏢 Creating an Organization-Level Goal

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F8Oz4dMD6FJ98L0RxRphm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4154de90-6d01-4428-8807-a081f06ae2b6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0828192&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to the **Goals (pro)** page.
    
2.  Click **Set Goals**.
    
3.  Select a **frequency**:
    
    *   Monthly
        
    *   Quarterly
        
    
4.  Select the metrics you want to track by clicking on them.
    
5.  Enter your **target value** for each metric.
    
    *   The initial value will also be available for reference - the initial value of a metric is calculated by taking into account the time period of last completed quarter or last completed month, based on the frequency selected.
        
    *   If industry benchmark data is available, it will appear here for comparison.
        
    
6.  Click **Save & Continue**.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/goals#creating-a-team-level-goal)

👥 Creating a Team-Level Goal

Follow the same steps as above, with one addition:

*   **Select the team** the goal applies to.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/goals#viewing-progress)

📊 Viewing Progress

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FDq4KgWMVM2Xddqep0Wi1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa1a23f9-9558-4764-a366-c6faa4f4fa71&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2362ec28&sv=2)

The Goals dashboard displays real-time progress for each metric:

*   **Metric Name**
    
*   **Initial Value** (at the start of the goal)
    
*   **Current Value**
    
*   **Target Value**
    
*   **Progress:**
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FkSbDWiqgV560ERveZK0t%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D846ea27d-315b-4e3a-a0f1-cfce5a6e8ad7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=53b2e675&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/goals#modifying-goals)

✏️ Modifying Goals

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F09nNcgwga8SU6s22Wy3l%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0d64072-3fa1-4f17-9c90-1cd4ec034d90&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ca39a522&sv=2)

You can update ongoing goals:

1.  Open the goal's dashboard.
    
2.  Click **Modify Goal**.
    
3.  Update existing metric values or add new metrics.
    
    > ⚠️ **Note:** You cannot change the goal’s duration.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/goals#deleting-goals)

🗑️ Deleting Goals

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FaWO7qLOfWvKP682k1lW7%252FScreenshot%25202025-09-03%2520at%25203.28.45%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0362cac-f199-4fe2-8586-367b7a0bd5fd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30ea5562&sv=2)

Only **ongoing goals** can be deleted:

1.  Open the goal dashboard.
    
2.  Click **Delete Goal**.
    
3.  Confirm deletion when prompted: _“The goal set will be completely deleted and cannot be retrieved. Are you sure you want to proceed?”_
    

> ⚠️ **Warning:** This action is permanent and will remove all associated metrics.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/goals#view-history-of-the-past-goals-and-performance)

⏳ View History of the past goals and performance

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FBwRJoYnghIYIJGjz2V4C%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01670234-5921-42cc-9f2c-7c3898233178&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=267871fd&sv=2)

Through this, you will be able to see what were the previous months/quarters goals and how much progress was made towards those goals.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FrUjuaCQ2ECnroiCyaBfr%252F03%2520-%2520Visiting%2520History%2520State.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a051195-91ac-4acd-be6d-8727e528dfdf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8991b7e2&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FTgrr2oDBYMAGj2WnJIWx%252F04%2520-%2520Visiting%2520History%2520State.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9467beb-0fe6-4a80-ab85-729dd1ab75d5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=82bb1b91&sv=2)

To download the goals and their progress into an excel, you can do that through the [Download Reports section](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/cockpit/how-to-download-reports)
 under Settings.

# Release Merge Frequency | Hivel

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/metrics-and-definitions/speed/release-merge-frequency#release-merge-frequency)

**Release Merge Frequency**

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FyHAsZUF4rPhNEqSqcS2R%252FScreenshot%25202025-11-27%2520at%25206.06.58%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0521d2a0-7ade-49cd-9d64-5bc8a12bb09f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=efc6111e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/metrics-and-definitions/speed/release-merge-frequency#formula)

Formula =

*   Release Merge frequency measures how often code is merged to the main/master branch. Elite Release Merge Frequency represents a stable and healthy delivery.
    
*   This metric would help you understand the number of PRs being pushed to production in a given time. This can work independently of your sprint cycle time. You can learn more about them [herearrow-up-right](https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/devops-sre/using-the-four-keys-to-measure-your-devops-performance)
    .
    
*   Too low Release Merge frequency indicates that there may be bottlenecks in review, or requirements, and teams are delivering features at a slower pace.
    
*   High Release Merge frequency shows that your team can quickly provide value and react to feedback or changes.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/metrics-and-definitions/speed/release-merge-frequency#industry-benchmarking)

Industry Benchmarking

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FP2DHq5C1WqoLuLsNIud9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db10d5e6a-9643-45c2-88fa-b1ec03747e61&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2517f145&sv=2)
