# How to build a data-driven culture of Engineering? | Hivel

Building a data-driven engineering culture is essential for making informed decisions, improving efficiency, and fostering innovation. Here are key points you can cover to guide organizations in fostering a culture where decisions are backed by data rather than intuition:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-1.-start-with-leadership-buy-in)

1\. **Start with Leadership Buy-In**

*   **Action**: Ensure that leadership supports and champions the use of data for decision-making across all levels.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Leadership sets the tone for the rest of the organization. When leaders prioritize data-driven approaches, it becomes part of the company’s values and practices.
    
*   **How to implement**: Encourage leadership to use engineering metrics and data during strategic meetings and planning sessions to demonstrate its value.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-2.-define-key-metrics-and-kpis)

2\. **Define Key Metrics and KPIs**

*   **Action**: Identify the key metrics that matter most for your engineering team, such as cycle time, deployment frequency, mean time to repair (MTTR), change failure rate (CFR), and more.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Without clear and relevant metrics, teams won’t know what data to focus on or how to measure success.
    
*   **How to implement**: Collaborate with product, design, and engineering leadership to establish the most important metrics that align with both business goals and team performance.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-3.-foster-a-culture-of-transparency-and-openness)

3\. **Foster a Culture of Transparency and Openness**

*   **Action**: Make engineering metrics visible and accessible to the entire team, from junior developers to executives.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Transparency encourages accountability and makes everyone feel responsible for improving metrics. It also helps team members understand how their work impacts overall goals.
    
*   **How to implement**: Use shared dashboards, regular team meetings, and retrospective discussions to review metrics and progress openly.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-4.-encourage-data-driven-decision-making-at-every-level)

4\. **Encourage Data-Driven Decision Making at Every Level**

*   **Action**: Empower developers, team leads, and managers to make decisions based on data rather than intuition or past practices.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Building a data-driven culture means that all levels of the organization rely on data for decision-making, not just leadership.
    
*   **How to implement**: Encourage team members to ask, "What does the data say?" before making technical or strategic decisions. Provide training on interpreting and acting on the data.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-5.-use-metrics-to-set-and-achieve-clear-goals)

5\. **Use Metrics to Set and Achieve Clear Goals**

*   **Action**: Align team and individual goals with specific, measurable metrics and KPIs to drive improvement.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Teams need measurable goals to work toward, and data-driven goals help clarify what success looks like.
    
*   **How to implement**: Implement OKRs (Objectives and Key Results) where each objective is tied to specific, data-driven key results (e.g., reduce cycle time by 20%, improve test coverage by 15%).
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-6.-incorporate-data-into-retrospectives)

6\. **Incorporate Data into Retrospectives**

*   **Action**: Use engineering metrics as a central part of sprint retrospectives to review performance, bottlenecks, and areas of improvement.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Retrospectives are an ideal time to reflect on past performance. Data gives teams concrete evidence of what went well and what needs to improve, rather than relying on anecdotal feedback.
    
*   **How to implement**: Regularly review key metrics at the end of each sprint and use them to identify improvement areas or process changes.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-7.-provide-continuous-education-and-training)

7\. **Provide Continuous Education and Training**

*   **Action**: Educate teams on the importance of data-driven decision-making and how to use data effectively.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Not everyone in the organization may be comfortable interpreting data, so providing the right training ensures teams can take advantage of analytics tools.
    
*   **How to implement**: Organize workshops, lunch-and-learns, or provide online resources for training team members on analytics tools, data interpretation, and best practices.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-8.-promote-accountability-and-ownership)

8\. **Promote Accountability and Ownership**

*   **Action**: Hold teams and individuals accountable for the data, encouraging ownership over both successes and areas needing improvement.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Accountability drives performance improvement. When teams own their metrics, they are more likely to focus on achieving results.
    
*   **How to implement**: Tie individual and team performance reviews to data-driven metrics. Regularly recognize teams that achieve goals based on data insights.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-9.-balance-data-with-context)

9\. **Balance Data with Context**

*   **Action**: Encourage teams to use data as a tool for decision-making while also understanding the context behind the data.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Data can sometimes lack the nuances of human judgment. Understanding the story behind the data ensures that decisions are both data-driven and contextually informed.
    
*   **How to implement**: Encourage teams to dig deeper when anomalies or surprising data points arise and combine qualitative insights with quantitative data for well-rounded decisions.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-10.-make-data-driven-improvements-incremental)

10\. **Make Data-Driven Improvements Incremental**

*   **Action**: Use data to drive continuous, incremental improvements rather than chasing perfection all at once.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Small, data-driven adjustments can lead to significant long-term improvements. Trying to change everything at once can overwhelm teams and dilute the effectiveness of data insights.
    
*   **How to implement**: Set small, achievable data-driven goals for each sprint and regularly evaluate progress.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-build-a-data-driven-culture-of-engineering#id-11.-celebrate-data-driven-wins)

11\. **Celebrate Data-Driven Wins**

*   **Action**: Recognize and reward teams when they achieve success through data-driven initiatives.
    
*   **Why it matters**: Celebrating wins helps reinforce the value of using data to drive decisions and motivates teams to continue using data to guide their work.
    
*   **How to implement**: Highlight metrics improvements during team meetings or company-wide updates and tie these successes to data-backed strategies.
    

By fostering a culture that relies on data for decision-making, organizations can reduce guesswork, improve efficiency, and drive performance improvements. Data-driven engineering ensures that every decision, from small technical choices to large strategic moves, is grounded in measurable, reliable information, leading to better outcomes.

[NextHow to balance speed and quality?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-balance-speed-and-quality)

# Marco - Code Review Agent | Hivel

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#product-overview-and-differentiation)

Product Overview & Differentiation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#what-is-marco-hivels-code-review-agent)

What is Marco - Hivel’s Code Review agent?

Marco uses machine learning and advanced foundational Large Language Models (LLMs) to automatically analyze code changes for bugs, security vulnerabilities, and performance issues. Unlike traditional static analysis, Marco understands the deep context of your codebase, learns your team’s patterns, and provides actionable feedback directly within your pull requests (PRs).

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#how-accurate-is-the-feedback-provided)

How accurate is the feedback provided?

By using built-in intelligence that analyzes codebase dependencies and learns from your specific coding style, Marco can provide highly relevant feedback that identifies over 95%+ of bugs in most cases, and catches critical issues that often slip past manual reviews. However, Marco is designed to complement human reviewers, not replace them, allowing humans to focus on high-level architecture and business logic after the first pass by AI code review.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#can-the-agent-catch-issues-that-humans-typically-miss)

Can the agent catch issues that humans typically miss?

Yes. Human reviewers often experience fatigue, which can lead to significant quality gaps, especially when reviews are rushed or when dealing with larger, more complex pull requests.

By automating the "repetitive task" of routine checks, Marco provides a consistent quality layer that doesn't get tired. This reduces reviewer fatigue by allowing your engineers to offload tedious syntax and standard checks to the AI, ensuring they can focus their mental energy on high-level architecture and business logic where human intuition is most valuable.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#how-does-the-complexity-score-help-clear-the-pr-backlog)

How does the Complexity Score help clear the PR backlog?

Marco assigns a 1-10 score to every pull request by scanning for review bottlenecks—such as intricate pointer logic, deep structural nesting, and complex dependencies. This score transforms your review process from a "repetitive task" into a prioritized, review-ready queue.

By identifying "big PR" blind spots at a glance, you can ensure logically dense changes receive the senior-level attention they require while allowing routine updates to move quickly. This data-driven approach reduces reviewer fatigue, prevents engineers from becoming bottlenecks, and allows your team to allocate their focus effectively—shortening review cycles without lowering the quality bar.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#technical-capabilities)

Technical Capabilities

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#which-programming-languages-are-supported)

Which programming languages are supported?

Marco is designed to support all major programming languages, including Python, JavaScript, Java, C++, Go, Ruby, and TypeScript. While proficiency may be highest in the most popular languages, advanced context engines allow Marco to work across entire stacks, including frontends, backends, and even Infrastructure-as-code like Terraform.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#how-does-marco-understand-my-entire-codebase)

How does Marco understand my entire codebase?

Marco analyzes your codebase by examining each file for dependencies and coding standards. It creates summaries at both the file and folder levels, capturing necessary context like dependencies, architectural standards, and functionality. Marco tracks bidirectional dependencies, identifying both the files that your code depends on and those that depend on it. Marco selectively provides only the most relevant context - avoiding information overload by focusing on key pieces of information rather than feeding in irrelevant data. This approach ensures high accuracy and avoids performance degradation. Marco uses advanced LLMs combined with custom algorithms to maintain efficient code organization and ensure optimal performance.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#security-and-data-privacy)

Security & Data Privacy

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#is-my-code-secure-and-private)

Is my code secure and private?

Security is a primary focus. Marco utilizes industry-standard encryption and adheres to compliance standards - ISO 27001, SOC 2 Type II and GDPR. Data isolation ensures that no unauthorized parties have access to your code during the review process.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#do-you-store-my-code)

Do you store my code?

No, we do not. Code collected for a review is typically disposed of as soon as the review is finished.By default, our tool automatically opts you out of data storage.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#workflow-and-integration)

Workflow & Integration

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#where-does-marco-fit-into-my-development-workflow)

Where does Marco fit into my development workflow?

The agent integrates seamlessly into existing workflows without requiring context switching. Key integration points include: Git Platforms: Automated reviews on GitHub & GitLab.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#can-marco-enforce-our-organizations-specific-coding-standards)

Can Marco enforce our organization’s specific coding standards?

Yes. You can define custom rulesets for architecture patterns, security policies, and style. Marco learns from your PR history and past comments to understand what "good code" looks like for your specific team, enforcing these standards consistently across all contributors.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#roi-measuring-success)

ROI : Measuring Success

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#what-kind-of-efficiency-gains-should-i-expect)

What kind of efficiency gains should I expect?

By pre-reviewing every pull request and surfacing high-signal issues, teams can significantly reduce review time. Automating routine checks frees up valuable time, allowing developers to focus on more complex tasks and high-level decision-making, leading to overall productivity improvements across the team.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/marco-code-review-agent#how-do-i-measure-the-success-of-hivels-marco)

How do I measure the success of Hivel’s Marco?

Success can be tracked through several key metrics:

*   Reduction in production bugs and "bug escape" rates.
    
*   Decreased review time and PR backlog.
    
*   Improved security, such as catching hardcoded credentials or SQL injection early.
    
*   Developer satisfaction and increased velocity.

# How to integrate Google Calendar in Hivel | Hivel

Integrating Google Calendar with Hivel involves a few key steps to ensure that all necessary calendars are accessible and synced properly. Below is a step-by-step guide to help you through the process:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/calendar/google-calendar/how-to-integrate-google-calendar-in-hivel#create-a-google-account)

Create a Google account

Create an account for Hivel which has at least "View" access to all the applicable developer's Google accounts.

*   You have the option to use either a normal user account with access to other calendars or a service account, but it is recommended to use a service account.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/calendar/google-calendar/how-to-integrate-google-calendar-in-hivel#integrate-google-calendar-with-hivel)

Integrate Google Calendar with Hivel

1\. Log in to the Hivel platform using the service account.

2\. Navigate to the Settings -> Integrations section from the dashboard.

3\. Find Google Calendar in the list of available integrations and click on Connect.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FAV7aUHCTqZ44VfRTyTxL%252FCapture-2025-02-28-145206.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daaa4fb58-6ef8-4d34-8dd4-f1eba8ec97cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91275c69&sv=2)

Follow the on-screen prompts to allow permissions for Hivel to access your Google Calendar data.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FoNlnkyvpMwgYOsJ98EB7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc51af7d-b023-4dce-b975-1469e4ea92a7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e80bcdb&sv=2)

This should help you seamlessly integrate Google Calendar with Hivel, allowing you to understand the schedule of your team effectively within the platform.

For further assistance or any issues encountered during the integration, please contact our support team at [\[email protected\].envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#7704020707180503371f1e01121b59161e59)

# How to change a team owner? | Hivel

To change the team owner of a team, follow the below steps:

1.  Go to Settings screen -> Teams -> Select the particular team
    
2.  Click on the three dots on top
    
3.  Change the team owner and save

All done!🙌

# What to do if my Review Time is high? | Hivel

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-review-time-is-high#identify-which-team-or-repo)

Identify which team or repo

As a first step we should understand which team or repo is facing high review times so that we can evaluate if that is expected or not given the business context and focus on them.

You can do this in the Cockpit, by switching to tabular view and sorting on review time column.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F99TAv4v2sUBVZ4jjblbL%252FGIF%2520Recording%2520Aug%252012%2520from%2520Jumpshare%2520%281%29.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D410ae94d-9bbe-455c-a922-a71adfb3fa9c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e873c4f6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-review-time-is-high#causes-for-high-review-time)

Causes for high review time

*   **Complex Code**: If the code submitted for review is overly complex or lacks proper documentation, it can take longer for reviewers to understand and evaluate it.
    
*   **Code Smells**: Issues like code duplication, lack of modularization, and poor naming conventions can slow down the review process.
    
*   **Limited Reviewer Availability**: If there are not enough qualified reviewers available, the review queue can become backlogged.
    
*   **Inconsistent Review Standards**: If the team does not have clear guidelines or standards for code reviews, different reviewers might have varying expectations, leading to longer discussions and revisions.
    
*   **Ambiguous Feedback**: If reviewers provide vague or unclear feedback, the author might need to go back and forth multiple times to understand and address the issues.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-review-time-is-high#how-to-reduce-review-time)

How to reduce review time

After identifying the teams, users, or repositories having high review times, it's essential to take proactive steps to reduce them. Below are some recommended strategies to help improve review time:

*   **Limit PR Size:** Smaller PRs are easier and faster to review. Encourage developers to break down large features or fixes into smaller, manageable pieces.
    
*   **Incremental Changes:** Adopt a workflow where changes are submitted and reviewed incrementally rather than in large, monolithic chunks.
    
*   **Define Review Scope:** Clearly define what reviewers should focus on (e.g., logic, performance, security, readability) to prevent them from getting bogged down in less critical issues.
    
*   **Feedback Loop:** Establish an efficient feedback loop between reviewers and developers to clarify any issues or concerns rapidly, reducing back-and-forth delays.
    
*   **Encourage Timely and Quality Reviews:** Foster a culture where timely reviews are a priority. Acknowledge and reward team members who consistently contribute to swift and thorough reviews.
    
*   **Rotating Reviewers:** Rotate reviewers to avoid bottlenecks caused by one person being unavailable.
    

[PreviousWhat to do if my Coding Time is high?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-coding-time-is-high)
[NextWhat to do if my Merge Time is high?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-merge-time-is-high)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Identify which team or repo](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-review-time-is-high#identify-which-team-or-repo)
    
*   [Causes for high review time](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-review-time-is-high#causes-for-high-review-time)
    
*   [How to reduce review time](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-review-time-is-high#how-to-reduce-review-time)

# Why do I see "No existing user found" message while login | Hivel

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FkNieRtMnWSf2zHBDzKVA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1f82960-206c-402c-9a30-808240635abe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89e9e95d&sv=2)

If this is your first time logging into Hivel, you may encounter a message prompting you to complete the setup. To proceed, follow these steps:

1.  **Check your email for an invitation**:
    
    *   Look for an invite email from your Hivel admin in your inbox.
        
    *   Accept the invitation to activate your account.
        
    
2.  **No invite? No problem**:
    
    *   Click on **"Get Started"** on the login screen.
        
    *   Sign up using your organization credentials.
        
    *   Once registered, you should be able to log in without issues.
        
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FartRTXX7TUHpWbODGxuO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34e0a214-2695-492a-b1d8-83b0dc94be40&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bc4855a7&sv=2)

If you run into any trouble, feel free to contact us at **[\[email protected\]](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
** for assistance.

# Azure Boards | Hivel

**Data Access by Hivel**

*   Hivel accesses the past 60-90 days of commits and pull requests from active repositories during the initial sync.
    

**Authorization Mechanism**

*   Hivel gets access using a Personal Access Token, which can be created using this [linkarrow-up-right](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/devops/organizations/accounts/use-personal-access-tokens-to-authenticate?view=azure-devops&tabs=Windows#create-a-pat)
    .
    
*   Users maintain full control and can withdraw access anytime by revoking the Personal Access Token.
    
*   Ensure '**All accessible organizations'** is selected while creating the Personal Access Token. ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FWQ23CAsvj8bRFQTgfyw0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc576014f-0e52-4f44-b6d0-48350b76afb0&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb68633c&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FDI3qRLMqzJogW2VKSQ51%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa7a48e4-3c2d-4c53-8b9f-23c237d98c46&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48e1c3c0&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F6QVTdt5mgSnX6FhKspRJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a55fa48-b093-40a4-84b5-03713683899d&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d105af3&sv=2)
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F0vccKgvrZradW7UZ5FWB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db930bc69-052a-4717-af63-c44e321cc522&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f376b9b0&sv=2)

**Requirements**

*   Ensure to create the Personal Access Token from an account that has "Project Administrator" permissions for all relevant projects and repositories.
    

**Best Practice**

*   Opt for a service account rather than an individual-linked account.
    
*   Service accounts are typically overseen by the company's admin.
    

**Personal Access Token Permissions**

*   Please ensure you select all the options below while creating a Personal Access Token.
    
    *   **Project And Team**: Read
        
    *   **User Profile**: Read
        
    *   **Code**: Read
        
    *   **Build**: Read
        
    *   **Graph:** Read
        
    *   **Work Items:** Read ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fbvzlj9oxA4zEMkKSLa6S%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6dfe77b0-8342-4692-be62-801df0224749&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57fef77b&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F05fLXq4XnHbDXgIB9rEN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1550c531-0a79-46cb-86bb-366b6ff12041&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e061d34&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FC1tDnhhlCe2nBzUwHPCF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75885a07-7f18-4598-8134-7d35b19bcf17&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffd76eea&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FPIqxw6g5fSl2dAtCLNoy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86a43ff4-44b4-4d0d-ba6c-2b9ee2febcb9&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=11a1ebbe&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FRkS5YqtDTaONUGEIiCy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da17f527d-4bca-4a02-86fe-2db9244191e9&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28352300&sv=2)
        
    

**You are almost done.**

*   Once a Personal Access Token is created, please copy it and share it with the Hivel team.
    
*   You will receive an email from the Hivel team once your data is all up and running.

# How to ensure Gitlab token has access to required groups/repositories | Hivel

Follow these steps to grant a service account access to required repositories:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/gitlab/how-to-ensure-gitlab-token-has-access-to-required-groups-repositories#navigate-to-the-gitlab-group)

**Navigate to the GitLab Group**

1.  Log in to GitLab.
    
2.  In the left sidebar, click **"Groups"** → **"Your Groups"**.
    
3.  Select the Group where you want to add the service account.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FRMsY4JlEmBXFZKupVN87%252Fimage%2520%2843%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11ff1b0d-f5ad-4a6d-b589-6316bc0f79b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf9e1cf6&sv=2)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/gitlab/how-to-ensure-gitlab-token-has-access-to-required-groups-repositories#open-the-groups-members-settings)

**Open the Group’s Members Settings**

1.  In the Group Dashboard, go to the left sidebar.
    
2.  Click **"Settings"** → **"Members"**.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fdh8rUvMjdaVmLeCfacjy%252Fimage%2520%2844%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D347bde98-47d3-47bc-acd2-99ee06b78f36&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b717155&sv=2)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/gitlab/how-to-ensure-gitlab-token-has-access-to-required-groups-repositories#invite-the-service-account)

**Invite the Service Account**

1.  Click **"Invite Member"** (top right corner).
    
2.  In the **"Select members or email address"** field, enter the service account username or email.
    
3.  Assign a "Reporter" or "Developer" role as required.
    
4.  Click **"Invite"**.
    

Repeat the steps for all required groups.

Once added, the service account will inherit access to all repositories within the groups.

[PreviousGitlab Cloudchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/gitlab/gitlab-cloud)
[NextBitBucketchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket)

# Microsoft Outlook | Hivel

Integrating Outlook with Hivel involves a few key steps to ensure that all necessary calendars are accessible and synced properly. Below is a step-by-step guide to help you through the process:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/calendar/microsoft-outlook#use-an-outlook-account-with-admin-access)

Use an Outlook account with Admin access

circle-info

**Use an Admin account which has at least "View" access to all the applicable developer's Outlook accounts.**

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/calendar/microsoft-outlook#integrate-outlook-with-hivel)

Integrate Outlook with Hivel

1\. Log into Hivel using the admin account.

2\. Navigate to the Settings -> Integrations section from the dashboard.

3\. Find Outlook in the list of available integrations and click on Connect.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FxEtHpAR0CE7yaZBznarW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9077b40c-1080-4799-992f-3a077e38da43&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=557da313&sv=2)

Follow the on-screen prompts to allow permissions for Hivel to access your Outlook data.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FpIlvpQcqXOpu9r8JrEq0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b0859ab-1a45-44bd-9ae1-b6d81e7b1bc4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=639cc8ce&sv=2)

This should help you seamlessly integrate Outlook with Hivel, allowing you to understand the schedule of your team effectively within the platform.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/calendar/microsoft-outlook#data-collected-from-calendars)

Data Collected from Calendars

Once authorization is complete, Hivel will read calendar data for all users under the admin account. The specific data points fetched from each calendar include:

*   **id:** Unique identifier of the calendar event.
    
*   **iCalUId:** Unique identifier for the event across calendar clients.
    
*   **start:** Start time of the event.
    
*   **end:** End time of the event.
    
*   **isCancelled:** Indicates if the event has been canceled.
    
*   **organizer:** The person who created or owns the event.
    
*   **attendees:** List of participants invited to the event.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/calendar/microsoft-outlook#sync-frequency)

Sync Frequency

*   **Initial Sync:** Fetches calendar data for the past 90 days.
    
*   **Incremental Sync:** Nightly updates to fetch events for the past 1 day.
    

For further assistance or any issues encountered during the integration, please contact our support team at [\[email protected\].envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#c1b2b4b1b1aeb3b581a9a8b7a4adefa0a8ef)

[PreviousHow to integrate Google Calendar in Hivelchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/calendar/google-calendar/how-to-integrate-google-calendar-in-hivel)
[NextCI/CDchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/ci-cd)

Last updated 9 months ago

# What happens if there are too many Flashy Reviews and how to prevent them? | Hivel

circle-info

A Pull Request larger than 200 Lines of Code merged with less than 5 minutes is considered as a Flashy Review PR.

This is [configurablearrow-up-right](https://hivel.gitbook.io/knowlegebase/setup/configurations-explained/branch-configurations#flashy-review)
 in the Settings screen.

To filter out on the PRs with Flashy Reviews, simply apply the filter in Pull Request screen.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FDmdcMW4RYWA2SK6MKRHt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59cf1263-892a-432f-8044-61821b16c757&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fdf44afc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-happens-if-there-are-too-many-flashy-reviews-and-how-to-prevent-them#when-there-are-too-many-flashy-reviews-some-issues-that-can-potentially-arise-are)

When there are too many flashy reviews, some issues that can potentially arise are

*   **Reduced Code Quality**: Quick approvals of large PRs may lead to overlooked bugs and security issues due to insufficient review.
    
*   **Increased Technical Debt**: Quick reviews can result in code that doesn’t meet best practices or project standards, increasing maintenance challenges.
    
*   **Decreased Team Accountability**: Minimal scrutiny of PRs can promote a culture where developers expect fast approvals, reducing overall discipline and accountability.
    
*   **Knowledge Silos**: Quick approvals might limit the opportunity for team members to fully understand the changes, creating knowledge gaps within the team.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-happens-if-there-are-too-many-flashy-reviews-and-how-to-prevent-them#to-prevent-an-excess-of-flashy-review-prs-and-encourage-more-thorough-code-reviews-consider-the-foll)

To prevent an excess of Flashy Review PRs and encourage more thorough code reviews, consider the following strategies

*   **Limit Size of PRs:** Encourage developers to keep PRs manageable by limiting the number of lines of code or changes included. Smaller, more focused PRs are easier to review thoroughly than large batches of changes.
    
*   **Set Clear Review Policies:** Establish and enforce a policy that requires sufficient time for code review, especially for larger PRs. This policy could include specific time frames based on the size of the PR.
    
*   **Use Code Review Checklists:** Develop checklists that reviewers can use to guide their review process, ensuring they cover all necessary aspects of the code.
    
*   **Mandatory Reviewer Assignments:** Require that PRs be reviewed by at least one senior developer. Assign reviews based on the areas of the codebase affected to ensure knowledgeable feedback.
    

[PreviousWhat to do if my Rework is high?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-to-do-if-my-rework-is-high)
[NextBest Practices for Ensuring Strong Pull Request Review Coveragechevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [When there are too many flashy reviews, some issues that can potentially arise are](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-happens-if-there-are-too-many-flashy-reviews-and-how-to-prevent-them#when-there-are-too-many-flashy-reviews-some-issues-that-can-potentially-arise-are)
    
*   [To prevent an excess of Flashy Review PRs and encourage more thorough code reviews, consider the following strategies](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-happens-if-there-are-too-many-flashy-reviews-and-how-to-prevent-them#to-prevent-an-excess-of-flashy-review-prs-and-encourage-more-thorough-code-reviews-consider-the-foll)

# Why Product and Allocation's previous data is not reflecting? | Hivel

After configuring the [**Product** and **Allocation**arrow-up-right](https://hivel.gitbook.io/knowlegebase/using-hivel/investment/how-to-set-up-products-and-allocation-tabs-in-the-investment-screen)
 fields in Hivel:

*   **Ongoing and Incremental Issues**: The data starts reflecting automatically for new and ongoing issues.
    
*   **Previous Issues**: Historical data does not appear automatically and requires a manual backend process to sync.
    

If you have historical data for the **Product** and **Allocation** fields and need it to reflect in Hivel:

1.  Reach out to us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#c3b0b6b3b3acb1b783abaab5a6afeda2aa)
    .
    
2.  We will manually run the backend process to sync the data.
    
3.  The updated data will be available in Hivel within 24 hours.
    

[PreviousHow do I exclude a PR from rework/maintenance/new work calculation?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs/how-do-i-exclude-a-pr-from-rework-maintenance-new-work-calculation)
[NextWhy don't I see delivery accuracy for Kanban boards?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs/why-dont-i-see-delivery-accuracy-for-kanban-boards)

# BitBucket Integration | Hivel

**What data does Hivel require access to?**

Hivel securely accesses the last 60-90 days of commits and pull requests from active repositories.

**Authorization Control**

We utilize Bitbucket's OAuth for secure login. You retain full control and can revoke access at any time via Bitbucket's authorized apps settings.

**Pre-requisites**

A service account with _write_ access to all applicable Bitbucket repositories.Write access is essential for publishing webhooks, enabling real-time data synchronization.

**Sign in to Hivel**

1.  Navigate to the Hivel [sign-up pagearrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/signup)
    
2.  Add your work email id (If you'd like to use your personal email id please contact [\[email protected\])envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#ef9c9a9f9f809d9baf8786998a83c18e86c6)
    
3.  Now, you can use your Google or Microsoft login with your work email id; or create a password.
    
4.  Create your Company Profile, and click '**Get Started**'.
    
5.  Once you've successfully created your Company Profile you will be redirected to the Integrations Page.
    
6.  Select Bitbucket, and log in to your company's Bitbucket account using a service account.
    
7.  Authorize Hivel on the ensuing Bitbucket redirect.
    
8.  Click "Grant" for desired workspaces.
    
9.  After authorization, you'll be redirected back to Hivel.
    
10.  Once your Bitbucket is successfully integrated, we will start to pull data. It will take between 2 - 48 hours for the complete sync, depending on the volume of the data.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/bitbucket-integration#below-are-step-by-step-screenshots-of-instructions-you-can-refer-to-if-needed)

# How to Re-authorize Jira with OAuth 2.0 | Hivel

**Here's a quick guide on how to re-authorize your Jira integration with Hivel:**

1.  Log in to your Hivel account.
    
2.  In the left panel, select **Settings** and go to the **Integrations** tab.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FiXFAYVLwayDew5VTMBGW%252Fimage%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26529b0f-d7e0-42d6-8665-9908182bd399&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30e65c92&sv=2)

1.  Find the Jira card and click the **'Reauthorize'** button.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F4GzFFMG8W9IDWb68SJYv%252Fimage%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D322fe9a2-74a9-4502-b810-10e043953068&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a467e55c&sv=2)

1.  Click on Accept
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FAbZywrtFogVq8kxz5uuC%252Fimage%2520%283%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7797dba-8a1d-4ad5-9035-efd9bed54fac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e15271de&sv=2)

**Once reauthorized, we’ll automatically resume fetching your latest Jira data.**

[PreviousHow to Integrate Jira with OAuth 2.0chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/jira/how-to-integrate-jira-with-oauth-2.0)
[NextHow to integrate Jira Server with Hivelchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/jira/how-to-integrate-jira-server-with-hivel)

# Azure DevOps | Hivel

**Data Access by Hivel**

*   Hivel accesses the past 60-90 days of commits and pull requests from active repositories during the initial sync.
    

**Authorization Mechanism**

*   Hivel gets access using a Personal Access Token, which can be created using this [linkarrow-up-right](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/devops/organizations/accounts/use-personal-access-tokens-to-authenticate?view=azure-devops&tabs=Windows#create-a-pat)
    .
    
*   Users maintain full control and can withdraw access anytime by revoking the Personal Access Token.
    
*   Ensure '**All accessible organizations'** is selected while creating the Personal Access Token. ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FWQ23CAsvj8bRFQTgfyw0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc576014f-0e52-4f44-b6d0-48350b76afb0&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb68633c&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FDI3qRLMqzJogW2VKSQ51%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa7a48e4-3c2d-4c53-8b9f-23c237d98c46&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48e1c3c0&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F6QVTdt5mgSnX6FhKspRJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a55fa48-b093-40a4-84b5-03713683899d&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d105af3&sv=2)
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F0vccKgvrZradW7UZ5FWB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db930bc69-052a-4717-af63-c44e321cc522&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f376b9b0&sv=2)

**Requirements**

*   Ensure to create the Personal Access Token from an account that has "Project Administrator" permissions for all relevant projects and repositories.
    

**Best Practice**

*   Opt for a service account rather than an individual-linked account.
    
*   Service accounts are typically overseen by the company's admin.
    

**Personal Access Token Permissions**

*   Please ensure you select all the options below while creating a Personal Access Token.
    
    *   **Project And Team**: Read
        
    *   **User Profile**: Read
        
    *   **Code**: Read
        
    *   **Build**: Read
        
    *   **Graph:** Read
        
    *   **Work Items:** Read ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fbvzlj9oxA4zEMkKSLa6S%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6dfe77b0-8342-4692-be62-801df0224749&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57fef77b&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F05fLXq4XnHbDXgIB9rEN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1550c531-0a79-46cb-86bb-366b6ff12041&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e061d34&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FC1tDnhhlCe2nBzUwHPCF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75885a07-7f18-4598-8134-7d35b19bcf17&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffd76eea&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FPIqxw6g5fSl2dAtCLNoy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86a43ff4-44b4-4d0d-ba6c-2b9ee2febcb9&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=11a1ebbe&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FRkS5YqtDTaONUGEIiCy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da17f527d-4bca-4a02-86fe-2db9244191e9&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28352300&sv=2)
        
    

**You are almost done.**

*   Once a Personal Access Token is created, please copy it and share it with the Hivel team.
    
*   You will receive an email from the Hivel team once your data is all up and running.

# How to identify root cases of high change failure rates? | Hivel

Identifying root causes of high change failure rates is crucial for improving the stability and reliability of software deployments. Here are effective strategies for determining the underlying issues that contribute to a high rate of change failures:

1.  **Conduct thorough postmortems for each failure**
    
    *   After every failure, organize a detailed review or postmortem that includes everyone involved in the deployment process. Analyze what went wrong and document the findings. The goal is to identify patterns or repeated mistakes that lead to failures.
        
    
2.  **Use monitoring and logging data effectively**
    
    *   Leverage logs and monitoring tools to trace back the failures to their origin. Look for anomalies in logs immediately before a failure occurred. This can provide clues about system behavior and help pinpoint the problematic changes.
        
    
3.  **Implement a blameless culture**
    
    *   Foster an environment where team members feel safe to report and discuss errors. A blameless culture encourages openness and can lead to more accurate identification of root causes without fear of retribution or criticism.
        
    
4.  **Enhance testing and quality assurance practices**
    
    *   Evaluate current testing methodologies to ensure they are robust enough to catch errors before deployment. This might include increasing code coverage with automated tests, integrating static code analysis tools, and conducting more rigorous peer reviews.
        
    
5.  **Review and refine deployment practices**
    
    *   Assess the deployment processes to identify any steps that may contribute to failures. This can involve reviewing the staging environment, deployment scripts, and rollback procedures to ensure they match the production environment as closely as possible.
        
    
6.  **Analyze configuration management**
    
    *   Misconfigurations can often lead to deployment failures. Ensure that all environment configurations are managed properly with automation tools to avoid human errors and inconsistencies between environments.
        
    
7.  **Investigate external dependencies**
    
    *   External services and libraries can also be sources of change failures. Verify that all external dependencies are stable, well-documented, and tested within the application context before they are integrated into the production environment.
        
    
8.  **Conduct regular skill and process training**
    
    *   Regular training sessions for the development and operations teams can help update and sharpen their skills in coding, testing, and deploying. This helps reduce errors due to outdated practices or lack of knowledge.
        
    
9.  **Seek feedback from all stakeholders**
    
    *   Regularly solicit feedback from developers, testers, operations staff, and even end-users to gather different perspectives on what might be causing the failures. This comprehensive feedback can provide a broader view of the issues at hand.
        
    

By systematically applying these strategies, teams can more effectively identify the root causes of high change failure rates and take corrective action to improve their deployment processes and reduce the likelihood of future failures.

[PreviousBest Practices for Team Ownership in Code Reviewchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review)
[NextBuilding a feedback loop for continuous code improvementchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/building-a-feedback-loop-for-continuous-code-improvement)

# Okta SSO | Hivel

To integrate Okta with Hivel, follow these steps:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/okta-sso#id-1.-create-an-application-in-okta)

1\. Create an Application in Okta

Follow these steps to set up an Okta application for Hivel authentication:

1.  **Log in** to your Okta Admin Console.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FanAaNDtes7RnlYfkw6zl%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%25207.14.58%25E2%2580%25AFPM%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7632eb2-7bf5-4818-a34a-3d266971fd3a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=85570f76&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to **Applications** → Click **Create App Integration**.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FhrNf2HhLcOJ6gtvCgeNM%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%25207.15.44%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D028ac564-d33b-4611-b560-7a5dca537167&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf1d63ce&sv=2)

1.  Select the **Sign-in method**: `OIDC - OpenID Connect`.
    
2.  Choose **Application Type**: `Web`.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FRmfehVF9EuUUoqli7UFo%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%25207.16.20%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D619a556b-e92c-43eb-b78e-64c8a77cbf13&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eef36078&sv=2)

1.  Enter the **Redirect URI**:
    

1.  Under **Assignments access**, configure permissions based on your organization's requirements.
    
2.  Add the required users to the Okta application to grant them access to Hivel.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FySxghUvU5ocpMhxrhMaN%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%25207.18.26%25E2%2580%25AFPM%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0f75871-aaed-438f-a7a7-6990cc09a03a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e02ba96&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FmIxPvsaMBvasBbLdEcqJ%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%25207.19.26%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38818db1-fb35-4f75-b7ea-099ce1eea447&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c672364&sv=2)

1.  Click **Save** to generate a `Client ID` and `Client Secret`.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/okta-sso#id-2.-fill-the-following-details-on-hivel-ui)

2\. Fill the following details on Hivel UI

After creating the application, fill the input fields on integration page on Hivel UI. Here is how:

*   **Log into Hivel -> Go to Settings -> Integrations -> SSO -> Okta**
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FISzDLo8VgtjJ0LG7zupc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9842c2c5-fe26-4b06-9404-40cbb234a116&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1fa013e9&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FMB0MrV6tN9gwXo3TZdnU%252FGemini%2520Generated%2520Image%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfed23c37-f849-40cf-8bb9-ba17bf1b9694&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8af1642&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/okta-sso#fill-the-following-details-on-the-popup)

**Fill the following details on the popup:**

*   **OKTA Domain URL** – Your Okta instance URL, e.g., `https://yourcompany.okta.com`.
    
*   **OKTA API URL** - We prepopulate based on your domain URL, but it can be changed in case that is not the correct API URL.
    
*   **Client ID** – The client identifier from your Okta application.
    
*   **Client Secret** – The client secret associated with the client ID.
    

Click on "Integrate OKTA" once done.

These details will enable a seamless authentication flow between Okta and Hivel. If you have any questions or need assistance, feel free to reach out.

# GitHub | Hivel

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github#integration-with-account-wide-access)

Integration with account-wide access

[How to integrate GitHub with account wide access?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-account-wide-access)
[How to re-authorize / re-initiate GitHub integration with account wide access?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-re-authorize-re-initiate-github-integration-with-account-wide-access)

###

# Setting up your own key for AI features | Hivel

Model required: Model: 4 Sonnet | 4.5 Sonnet | 4.6 Sonnet Minimum Thinking budget: 3000|5000|5000 {Respectively for the models} Max Thinking Budget: 5000| 10,000| 10,000 {Respectively for the models}

Steps to create the Claude API key:

1.  Navigate to the "API Keys" section in your account dashboard or settings.
    
2.  Click the "+Create Key" button.
    
3.  Give your API key a descriptive name (e.g., "My\_First\_Claude\_App") and click "Create".
    
4.  Immediately copy the generated key and store it in a secure location (like a password manager). For security reasons, the key will not be shown again after you leave this page.

# Building a feedback loop for continuous code improvement | Hivel

Building a feedback loop for continuous code improvement is essential for fostering a culture of learning and innovation in software development teams. Here’s how you can create an effective feedback loop that promotes ongoing code quality and improvement:

1.  **Integrate code reviews into development workflow**
    
    *   Implement mandatory code reviews using platforms like GitHub, GitLab, or Bitbucket, ensuring issues are caught early and fostering knowledge sharing across the team.
        
    
2.  **Automate code quality checks**
    
    *   Utilize static analysis tools such as SonarQube, ESLint, and StyleCop to automatically review code for errors and technical debt, maintaining high quality standards while allowing reviewers to focus on complex issues.
        
    
3.  **Implement pair programming**
    
    *   Schedule regular pair programming sessions where two developers collaborate in real-time, enhancing code quality and team collaboration simultaneously.
        
    
4.  **Use metrics to track progress**
    
    *   Analyze metrics related to code quality, like bug rates and technical debt, using integrated tools to quantitatively measure and visualize improvement over time.
        
    
5.  **Conduct regular refactoring sessions**
    
    *   Dedicate time during development cycles specifically for refactoring, ensuring the codebase remains clean and maintainable, which minimizes long-term technical debt.
        
    
6.  **Hold retrospective meetings**
    
    *   Conduct retrospective meetings after each development cycle to discuss successes and areas for improvement, embedding a proactive approach to enhancing code quality and team processes.
        
    
7.  **Encourage training and continuous learning**
    
    *   Provide opportunities for developers to attend workshops and training sessions, keeping the team updated with the latest coding techniques and industry standards, which they can apply to their work.
        
    
8.  **Implement feedback tools within the application**
    
    *   Utilize feature flags, A/B testing tools, and monitor application logs to gather direct user feedback and performance data, guiding developers on where improvements are most needed.
        
    
9.  **Promote a culture of open communication**
    
    *   Foster an environment where feedback is welcomed and viewed as essential for personal and professional growth, improving code quality through collaborative problem-solving and shared ownership.
        
    
10.  **Create a knowledge sharing platform**
    
    *   Develop a central repository or wiki for sharing insights, best practices, and lessons learned, preventing repeated mistakes and promoting best practices across all projects.
        
    

By establishing these practices, your team can create a robust feedback loop that not only improves code quality but also supports the ongoing development and growth of your team members. This loop fosters an environment where continuous improvement is part of the everyday process, leading to better software products and a more engaged team.

[PreviousHow to identify root cases of high change failure rates?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/how-to-identify-root-cases-of-high-change-failure-rates)
[NextHow to improve planning and throughputchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-planning-and-throughput)

# How to Integrate Jira with OAuth 2.0 | Hivel

**Here's a quick guide on how to re-authorize your Jira integration with Hivel:**

1.  Log in to your Hivel account.
    
2.  In the left panel, select **Settings** and go to the **Integrations** tab.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FiXFAYVLwayDew5VTMBGW%252Fimage%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26529b0f-d7e0-42d6-8665-9908182bd399&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30e65c92&sv=2)

1.  Find the Jira card and click the **'Connect'** button.
    
2.  Click on Accept
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FAbZywrtFogVq8kxz5uuC%252Fimage%2520%283%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7797dba-8a1d-4ad5-9035-efd9bed54fac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e15271de&sv=2)

**5\. Once connected, we’ll automatically start fetching your latest data.**

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FW7YthWVhXYn77IeLeGrr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c2b700f-c43d-49b3-bfb8-8b3fa66f4e30&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=592d77d2&sv=2)

1.  The next step is to **create a webhook** for ongoing data, and for that
    
2.  Open a new tab and log in to your Jira application using the same admin credentials
    
3.  Top Right corner-> **Settings** -> **System**
    
4.  On the Left panel -> **Webhooks**
    
5.  Top Right -> **Create webhook**
    
6.  Now use the below details in the form:
    
    1.  **Name:** Hivel
        
    2.  **URL**\- [https://app.hivel.ai/jiraapi/webhook/processarrow-up-right](https://app.insightly.ai/jiraapi/webhook/process)
        ​
        
    3.  **Events:**
        
        1.  _Issue-related events_
            
            1.  **JQL: All issues**
                
            2.  **Issue** (select checkboxes) : created, updated, deleted
                
            
        2.  _User-related events_
            
            1.  **User** (select checkboxes) : created, deleted, updated
                
            
        3.  _Jira Software-related events_
            
            1.  **Sprint** (select checkboxes)**:** deleted, updated, started, closed
                
            
        
    
7.  Ensure the Name, URL, and events are all checked. Click on **Create.**
    

Done! The data will be refreshed within 24 hours.

[PreviousJirachevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/jira)
[NextHow to Re-authorize Jira with OAuth 2.0chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/jira/how-to-re-authorize-jira-with-oauth-2.0)

# Azure GIT Server | Hivel

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/azure/azure-git-server#data-access-by-hivel)

Data Access by Hivel

*   Hivel accesses the past 60-90 days of commits and pull requests from active repositories during the initial sync.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/azure/azure-git-server#h_01j3f1mcmbfjzaqwgecz0qnyxy)

Whitelist Necessary IP Addresses

For a secure and uninterrupted connection, make sure to whitelist the following IP addresses:

*   **Mandatory IPs**:
    
    *   107.23.139.76
        
    *   3.219.89.23
        
    
*   **Recommended, but Optional IPs**:
    
    *   45.119.114.218
        
    *   183.82.116.218
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/azure/azure-git-server#authorization-mechanism)

Authorization Mechanism

*   Hivel gets access using a Personal Access Token, which can be created using this [linkarrow-up-right](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/devops/organizations/accounts/use-personal-access-tokens-to-authenticate?view=azure-devops&tabs=Windows#create-a-pat)
    .
    
*   Users maintain full control and can withdraw access anytime by revoking the Personal Access Token.
    
*   Ensure '**All accessible organizations'** is selected while creating the Personal Access Token. ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FWQ23CAsvj8bRFQTgfyw0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc576014f-0e52-4f44-b6d0-48350b76afb0&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb68633c&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FDI3qRLMqzJogW2VKSQ51%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa7a48e4-3c2d-4c53-8b9f-23c237d98c46&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48e1c3c0&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F6QVTdt5mgSnX6FhKspRJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a55fa48-b093-40a4-84b5-03713683899d&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d105af3&sv=2)
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F0vccKgvrZradW7UZ5FWB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db930bc69-052a-4717-af63-c44e321cc522&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f376b9b0&sv=2)

**Requirements**

*   Ensure to create the Personal Access Token from an account that has "Project Administrator" permissions for all relevant projects and repositories.
    

**Best Practice**

*   Opt for a service account rather than an individual-linked account.
    
*   Service accounts are typically overseen by the company's admin.
    

**Personal Access Token Permissions**

*   Please ensure you select all the options below while creating a Personal Access Token.
    
    *   **Project And Team**: Read
        
    *   **User Profile**: Read
        
    *   **Code**: Read
        
    *   **Build**: Read
        
    *   **Graph:** Read
        
    *   **Work Items:** Read ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fbvzlj9oxA4zEMkKSLa6S%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6dfe77b0-8342-4692-be62-801df0224749&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57fef77b&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F05fLXq4XnHbDXgIB9rEN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1550c531-0a79-46cb-86bb-366b6ff12041&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e061d34&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FC1tDnhhlCe2nBzUwHPCF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75885a07-7f18-4598-8134-7d35b19bcf17&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ffd76eea&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FPIqxw6g5fSl2dAtCLNoy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86a43ff4-44b4-4d0d-ba6c-2b9ee2febcb9&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=11a1ebbe&sv=2) ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FRkS5YqtDTaONUGEIiCy1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da17f527d-4bca-4a02-86fe-2db9244191e9&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28352300&sv=2)
        
    

**You are almost done.**

*   Once a Personal Access Token is created, please copy it and share it with the Hivel team.
    
*   You will receive an email from the Hivel team once your data is all up and running.

# Release Notes - July 2025 | Hivel

Staying safe out there in the monsoon? Whether you're cozied up with a warm drink or dodging puddles, we’ve got updates to brighten your experience on Hivel.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-july-2025#a-more-intuitive-way-to-see-your-metrics)

💡 A more intuitive way to see your metrics

We’ve given Dashboards a fresh boost - with more ways to group, view, and understand your data.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FlCqibag6lkrZ4jw02REj%252FScreen%2520Cast%25202025-08-05%2520at%25204.37.29%2520PM.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D194fb76b-6a2b-46db-9490-4556175a57f6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cc213e6f&sv=2)

**📊 Grouping Made Simpler**

*   **Release Cycles**: Group data by release cycles that _started_ within your selected date range.
    
*   **None**: View data without any time grouping - ideal for cross-period insights (Daily / Weekly / Monthly / Quarterly / Release Cycles).
    

**📈 Chart Options**

*   Choose from **Bar**, **Line**, or **Area** charts to match your data storytelling style.
    

**🧩 Smarter Toggles for Deeper Control**

*   **Teams Toggle**: Break down graphs by individual teams.
    
*   **Aggregate Toggle**: View the big picture with combined team data.
    

These upgrades mean less digging and more clarity. [_Try it out!_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/overview/cycle-time)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-july-2025#cascade-team-selection)

🌐 Cascade Team Selection

You asked for more flexibility in team selections - we delivered!

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FL1w1TBozheEDwZnvXPXO%252FScreen%2520Cast%25202025-08-05%2520at%25204.46.18%2520PM.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D676af324-ea1a-462b-9f1f-ed262ee4a21b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2e7039f&sv=2)

**Cascade Toggle Behavior:**

*   **ON (default)**: Select all sub-teams under a parent, and the parent gets auto-selected too.
    
*   **OFF**: Only the teams you explicitly pick (parent or sub) are included.
    

This gives you tighter control over how your data is sliced and diced across team structures.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-july-2025#a-fresh-look-for-integrations-and-configurations)

🛠️ A Fresh look for Integrations & Configurations

The Integrations and Configuration pages have been fully revamped.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F9GPh0hijfr5tYlG1E4Zp%252FScreen%2520Cast%25202025-08-05%2520at%25204.49.11%2520PM.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcff20887-d295-4df7-82b8-61e20b4a1af1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f0c63cc&sv=2)

You’ll find:

*   All key settings and details in one place
    
*   A cleaner experience for faster, smoother setups
    

This makes it easier to plug in and configure exactly how you need - no confusion, no fuss.

# How do I exclude a PR from rework/maintenance/new work calculation? | Hivel

**Excluding commits on the Coding Screen**:

*   On the **Coding** screen, you can exclude **commits** but not pull requests (PRs).
    
*   This approach provides a more granular view, allowing you to drill down into specific commits responsible for spikes in **rework**, **maintenance**, or **new work**.
    

**Excluding pull requests**:

*   To exclude an entire PR, use the **Process** screen or the **Pull Request** screen.
    
*   These sections are designed for managing PR-level exclusions, offering a broader view of work at the PR level.
    

This differentiation ensures that you can focus on the level of detail most relevant to your analysis i.e. commit-level insights on the Coding screen and PR-level actions on the Process or Pull Request screens.

[PreviousWhy do some Jira issues show as spillover in Hivel even though they were completed in Jira?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs/why-do-some-jira-issues-show-as-spillover-in-hivel-even-though-they-were-completed-in-jira)
[NextWhy Product and Allocation's previous data is not reflecting?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs/why-product-and-allocations-previous-data-is-not-reflecting)

# What to do if my Rework is high? | Hivel

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-to-do-if-my-rework-is-high#identify-which-team-or-repo)

Identify which team or repo

As a first step we should understand which team or repo is having high rework so that we can evaluate if that is expected or not given the business context and focus on them.

You can do this in the Cockpit, by switching to tabular view and sorting on rework column.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FVdS28QDgBREPY77uJx9n%252FGIF%2520Recording%2520Aug%252021%2520from%2520Jumpshare%2520%281%29.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7bf7a4c9-f868-461f-ad47-d2dbe487fa78&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc359931&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-to-do-if-my-rework-is-high#identify-which-team-or-repo-1)

Drilldown further to identify user or PR

You can drill down and identify which users or PRs had the most rework by applying filters on the Coding screen.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FhLVfKxTfuwlV6wZi5u27%252FGIF%2520Recording%2520Aug%252021%2520from%2520Jumpshare.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D891acb53-475d-4206-9744-09fa07b3d8e0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4cf2470e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-to-do-if-my-rework-is-high#causes-of-high-rework)

Causes of high rework

*   **Incomplete or Evolving Requirements:** If requirements are not fully defined or evolve after coding has started, developers may need to revisit and modify code to accommodate new or refined expectations.
    
*   **Poor Initial Design or Implementation:** If the code is not well-designed or optimally implemented from the start, it may need to be refactored or rewritten shortly after being introduced.
    
*   **Bug Fixes Post-Release:** Bugs that are discovered after the code has been deployed often need to be fixed quickly, leading to rework within a short timeframe.
    
*   **Technical Debt Payoff:** If the initial implementation was rushed or done with known technical debt, there may be a need to revisit and clean up the code shortly after it was written.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-to-do-if-my-rework-is-high#ways-to-address-high-rework)

Ways to address high rework

*   **Improve Requirement Gathering and Stakeholder Alignment:** Engage stakeholders early and frequently to ensure that all requirements are thoroughly understood and documented. Use user stories, acceptance criteria, and wireframes to clearly define expectations.
    
*   **Invest in Design and Code Reviews:** Allocate time for thorough design before implementation. Conduct design reviews with peers to identify potential issues early. Follow up with regular code reviews to ensure that the implementation aligns with the design and best practices.
    
*   **Improve Release and Monitoring Processes:** Implement a more rigorous testing and staging process before release to catch bugs earlier. Use continuous deployment practices with canary releases or blue-green deployments to minimize the impact of bugs.
    
*   **Allocate Time for Refactoring and Debt Reduction:** Regularly schedule time within sprints specifically for addressing technical debt. Encourage developers to refactor code as part of their daily work, rather than postponing it.
    

[PreviousHow to improve Qualitychevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality)
[NextWhat happens if there are too many Flashy Reviews and how to prevent them?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-happens-if-there-are-too-many-flashy-reviews-and-how-to-prevent-them)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Identify which team or repo](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-to-do-if-my-rework-is-high#identify-which-team-or-repo)
    
*   [Drilldown further to identify user or PR](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-to-do-if-my-rework-is-high#identify-which-team-or-repo-1)
    
*   [Causes of high rework](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-to-do-if-my-rework-is-high#causes-of-high-rework)

# Why don't I see delivery accuracy for Kanban boards? | Hivel

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs/why-dont-i-see-delivery-accuracy-for-kanban-boards#why-delivery-accuracy-isnt-shown-for-kanban-boards)

Why Delivery Accuracy isn’t shown for kanban boards:

1.  **Sprint-Based Metrics**:
    
    *   Delivery Accuracy calculates the planned vs. completed work based on a **sprint cycle**. This includes determining the percentage of tickets completed relative to those planned for the sprint.
        
    *   Since Kanban does not operate with defined time-boxed sprints, this metric is incompatible with its continuous delivery flow.
        
    
2.  **Kanban’s continuous nature**:
    
    *   Kanban focuses on **workflow optimization and throughput**, with no strict boundaries like sprint start or end dates.
        
    *   Without those boundaries, measuring planned vs. completed work over a set timeframe (as required for Delivery Accuracy) would yield incomplete or misleading results.
        
    

circle-info

You may notice sprints appearing in the sprint filter for Kanban boards; these are weekly dummy sprints generated from the backend to provide a trend representation in the Issue tab.

[PreviousWhy Product and Allocation's previous data is not reflecting?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs/why-product-and-allocations-previous-data-is-not-reflecting)
[NextWhy some of the repositories are not imported or synced?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs/why-some-of-the-repositories-are-not-imported-or-synced)
