# Slack Integration with Hivel | Hivel

No need to jump between 10 different dashboards to figure out your top priorities or spot potential problems. Whether it’s reminders about pending PRs, or a quick summary of what happened in the week, you can stay on top of things right where you work.

Hivel will send timely notifications to your preferred Slack channel(s), so you can act on issues before they turn into bigger problems.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/slack-integration-with-hivel#how-to-integrate-slack-with-hivel)

**How to Integrate Slack with Hivel**

*   Go to _**Settings →**_ [_**Integrations**_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/settings/integrations)
     _**→ Slack**_ and click on "Connect".
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F42x7kBgZhFk9K7BxtnIO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a65b626-c15e-4b9a-b567-45d0619f97ab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22c7ca9&sv=2)

*   A prompt will appear asking you to review the app’s access permissions. Click **Allow** to confirm.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FcBLsFgZlicliNRzkeRy5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D947e55a9-a3d3-4875-ae9a-9fd2f2874dff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f8ab8c8&sv=2)

circle-info

**Note:** You’ll need to be a **Slack Workspace Admin** to complete this integration.

**Ta-da! You’re all set. Hivel is now connected to Slack.**

For Hivel to start sending alerts to your preferred Slack channel, follow the steps outlined in [this guidearrow-up-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/using-hivel/alerts-in-hivel/setting-up-the-slack-channel-for-alerts)
.

Let us know if you need any help setting this up! Contact us at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
.

# Why do some Jira issues show as spillover in Hivel even though they were completed in Jira? | Hivel

In Hivel, we identify completed issues by the issue status category and resolution date of the issues i.e.

1.  If the resolution date is on of before the sprint end date, then they are considered as completed.
    
2.  If the resolution date is not set or is after the sprint end date, then it is considered as spillover.
    

As a result of certain Jira configurations, some completed issues may lack a resolution date. Hence even if their status falls under the "Closed" category, these issues are still classified as spillovers in Hivel.

circle-info

To configure the issues to have resolutions and resolution dates set while closing, please refer to this [documentationarrow-up-right](https://confluence.atlassian.com/jirakb/jira-issues-need-a-resolution-826873869.html)
 from Atlassian on the same.

[PreviousPR, Issues & Workflow FAQschevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs)
[NextHow do I exclude a PR from rework/maintenance/new work calculation?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs/how-do-i-exclude-a-pr-from-rework-maintenance-new-work-calculation)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Easing into Kanban: How to set your team up for success | Hivel

As a team begins to shift from Scrum to Kanban, it's important to remember that this is not just a process change - it's a mindset shift!

Kanban emphasizes continuous flow, transparency, and incremental improvement rather than sprint-based planning and velocity.

This transition doesn’t need to be abrupt. In fact, the most effective shifts happen gradually, building on what your team already knows and does well. In this guide, we’ve outlined practical, low-friction steps to help your team ease into Kanban.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#start-small-support-your-team-and-grow-together)

Start small, Support your team, and Grow together

Making the shift to Kanban works best when done gradually, with empathy for your team and clarity on the _why_. Here’s how to set a strong foundation:

**a) Begin with what’s familiar**

Instead of reinventing your workflow from day one, just visualize your current process on a Kanban board. No need to change how you work immediately - just observe and get a shared view of how work flows.

**b) Invest in readiness, not perfection**

Before diving deep, check how confident your team feels about Kanban. Share simple training, clarify common misconceptions, and create a safe space for questions. The goal isn’t perfection - it’s comfort and clarity.

**c) Encourage everyone to lead**

Empower team members to call out blockers, suggest process tweaks, and take ownership of improvements. Leadership isn’t a title here - it’s a behavior. Recognizing these efforts helps build trust and keeps momentum going.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#consider-a-hybrid-approach-scrumban-during-transition)

Consider a hybrid approach (Scrumban) during transition

**Why:** Combining elements of Scrum and Kanban can ease the transition and allow teams to retain beneficial practices from both methodologies.

**What to do:**

*   Implement a Scrumban approach by maintaining certain Scrum rituals (like daily stand-ups) while adopting Kanban's continuous flow.
    
*   Gradually shift towards a full Kanban system as the team becomes more comfortable.
    
*   An intro to Scrumban by [Asanaarrow-up-right](https://asana.com/resources/scrumban?utm_source=chatgpt.com)
    .
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#focus-on-how-long-work-takes-not-sprint-velocity)

Focus on how long work takes (Not Sprint Velocity)

**Why:** In Kanban, there are no sprints - so speed should be measured by how long each task or bug fix takes to complete.

**What to do:**

*   Track **Cycle Time** and identify if there are an bottlenecks in any stage.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#visualize-blocked-work-or-on-hold-items)

Visualize Blocked Work or On Hold items

**Why:** Making stalled tasks visible helps teams identify and address issues promptly.

**What to do:**

*   Use visual indicators (like color codes or tags) to mark tasks that are blocked or waiting.
    
*   Create specific columns or areas on the Kanban board for tasks that are on hold or awaiting input.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#limit-work-in-progress-to-avoid-overload)

Limit Work in Progress (to avoid overload)

**Why:** If teams take on too much at once, nothing gets done quickly.

**What to do:**

*   Set a limit on how many tasks or PRs are “in progress” at the same time.
    
*   Use Hivel to see how many things each developer is juggling.
    
*   A guide on [WIP limitsarrow-up-right](https://www.atlassian.com/agile/kanban/wip-limits)
     by Atlassian
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#separate-planned-and-unplanned-work)

Separate Planned and Unplanned work

**Why:** Without sprints, unexpected work can sneak in and cause delays.

**What to do:**

*   In Hivel, to represent the work item volume, we create auto 2-week sprints. And we categorize each work item into planned or unplanned depending on whether they were created before the sprint start date or after.
    
*   Another approach to identify planned and unplanned work is to maintain a separate field to capture the info.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#encourage-smaller-faster-code-changes)

Encourage smaller, faster code changes

**Why:** In a continuous flow model, large PRs slow everything down.

**What to do:**

*   Recommend smaller PRs that are easier to review.
    
*   Hivel shows PR size and how long reviews take.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#prevent-work-from-getting-stuck)

Prevent work from getting stuck

**Why:** In Kanban, there’s no sprint deadline to push things along.

**What to do:**

*   Use Hivel to:
    
    *   Identify work items with high issue age
        
    *   Tasks sitting without activity for a few days
        
    *   PRs not reviewed or merged
        
    
*   This keeps things moving.
    

`**The shift to Kanban is a journey and with the right mindset, your team will not only adapt but thrive.**`

[PreviousHow to measure impact of Copilots using Hivel?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/how-to-measure-impact-of-copilots-using-hivel)
[NextMetrics & Data FAQschevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/metrics-and-data-faqs)

Last updated 9 months ago

*   [Start small, Support your team, and Grow together](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#start-small-support-your-team-and-grow-together)
    
*   [Consider a hybrid approach (Scrumban) during transition](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#consider-a-hybrid-approach-scrumban-during-transition)
    
*   [Focus on how long work takes (Not Sprint Velocity)](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#focus-on-how-long-work-takes-not-sprint-velocity)

*   [Encourage smaller, faster code changes](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#encourage-smaller-faster-code-changes)
    
*   [Prevent work from getting stuck](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/reporting-and-goal-tracking-faqs/easing-into-kanban-how-to-set-your-team-up-for-success#prevent-work-from-getting-stuck)

# What to do if my Cycle Time is high? | Hivel

circle-check

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-cycle-time-is-high#cycle-time-is-the-time-it-takes-from-the-first-commit-to-pr-merged)

Cycle time is the time it takes from the first commit to PR merged.

High cycle time means that it takes a longer than desirable duration to complete tasks, such as features or bug fixes, from the start of development to delivery. This can indicate inefficiencies in the process, such as bottlenecks, poor resource allocation, or overly complex tasks. High cycle times often lead to slower delivery of value, reduced productivity, and a lack of responsiveness to changes, which can impact overall project success and stakeholder satisfaction.

Reducing the org's cycle time is crucial for maintaining agility and ensuring timely, cost-effective delivery of quality software.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-cycle-time-is-high#identify-which-team-or-repo)

Identify which team or repo

As a first step we should understand which team or repo is facing high cycle times so that we can evaluate if that is expected or not given the business context and focus on them.

You can do this in the Cockpit, by switiching to tabular view and sorting on cycle time column.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F99TAv4v2sUBVZ4jjblbL%252FGIF%2520Recording%2520Aug%252012%2520from%2520Jumpshare%2520%281%29.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D410ae94d-9bbe-455c-a922-a71adfb3fa9c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e873c4f6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-cycle-time-is-high#identify-the-bottlenecks-whether-coding-review-or-merge)

Identify the bottlenecks - whether coding, review, or merge

To understand what is causing the cycle time to be high, it is important to identify which phases of the development are taking the longest.

We can do this by going to the Process screen, filtering on any particular teams, and understanding from the trendline which phase is taking longer.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F4zfcHMdq0Ep18dnTfZTn%252FGIF%2520Recording%2520Aug%252012%2520from%2520Jumpshare.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac6ecacb-db21-436d-9c7c-6031382cf87b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ec5e894d&sv=2)

_In this case, the Cycle Time was mainly influenced by Coding Time_

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-cycle-time-is-high#causes-for-high-cycle-time)

Causes for high cycle time

*   **Review and testing bottlenecks:** Delays in specific stages like code reviews, testing, or approvals can create bottlenecks, slowing down the overall process.
    
*   **Lack of Automation:** Manual processes for testing, deployment, or integration can significantly increase cycle time. Lack of CI/CD pipelines can contribute to this.
    
*   **Overloaded Team Members:** If team members are juggling too many tasks or are overburdened, it can delay progress on their assigned tasks.
    
*   **Unclear Prioritization:** When tasks are not clearly prioritized, developers may focus on less critical work, delaying more important tasks.
    
*   **Scope Creep:** Continuously adding new requirements or features during the development process can extend the cycle time.
    

circle-info

To know more on understanding and addressing high [Coding times](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-coding-time-is-high)
, high [Merge times](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-merge-time-is-high)
, and high [Review times](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-review-time-is-high)
, please refer to the linked articles.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-cycle-time-is-high#how-to-reduce-cycle-time)

How to reduce Cycle Time?

*   **Optimize Code Reviews:** Streamline code review processes by setting clear guidelines, automating checks, and ensuring timely reviews. Consider implementing a review rotation to evenly distribute the workload.
    
*   **Automate Testing and Deployment:** Automate repetitive tasks such as unit testing, integration testing, and deployment to reduce manual effort and minimize errors.
    
*   **Prioritize Work Effectively:** Use tools like Kanban boards or sprint planning to prioritize tasks based on their importance and impact. Focus on high-value tasks that can be delivered quickly.
    
*   **Limit Work in Progress (WIP):** Avoid overloading developers with too many tasks at once. Limiting WIP helps maintain focus and reduces context switching, leading to faster completion of individual tasks.
    
*   **Refactor Code Regularly:** Dedicate time to refactoring and cleaning up code to reduce technical debt. Cleaner code is easier to work with, leading to faster development and fewer bugs.
    

If you need additional help, feel free to reach out to [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e794929797889593a78f8e91828bc9868e)
.

[PreviousHow to improve Speed?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed)
[NextWhat to do if my Coding Time is high?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-speed/what-to-do-if-my-coding-time-is-high)

# Claude Code | Hivel

1.  Log in to your Hivel account.
    
2.  In the left panel, select **Settings**, and go to the **Integrations** tab.
    
3.  Find the **Claude Code** card and click the **'Connect'** button.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FWpgCfqAydU9cRr3IIKZK%252Fimage%2520%28118%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D53250a61-579c-498a-b7d4-86ca6f5f05f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cbfb9007&sv=2)
    
4.  In the pop-up, paste the Claude Code API
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F0zNg29TUiWdoJqiGfqzh%252Fimage%2520%28119%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5d51b546-bb5a-4a18-b0ba-0b7b49ef079e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4de30692&sv=2)

*   To get the above Claude Code API key, use the following steps:
    
    *   Go to the Settings tab, click API keys on the left-side menu.
        
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FOqLz5rCFW8fKbDl9gnXW%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3c8f214-bb1f-4f60-84a6-9dae01b58c26&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b3a4d2e0&sv=2)
    
    *   Click Create Key.
        
        ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Ft3YmgUexgerjwKM72udu%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4bb9fd8-41aa-4b69-8583-cfcf6fd186b1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ead7c1a1&sv=2)
        
    *   **Name your key as Hivel, and click Create Key to finish the process.**
        
    

circle-exclamation

Please ensure that the API key is an Admin API key (done from an Admin account), which starts with `sk-ant-admin...` and differs from standard API keys.

# Gitlab Server | Hivel

**Data Access by Hivel**

*   Hivel accesses the past 60-90 days of commits and pull requests from active repositories during the initial sync.
    

**Authorization Mechanism**

*   Hivel employs GitLab Server's OAuth for authentication.
    
*   Users maintain full control and can withdraw access by revoking the Personal Access Token.
    

**Effortlessly Connect Your GitLab Server with Hivel**

This easy-to-follow guide will lead you through each step, ensuring a smooth and efficient integration process to unlock efficiency insights across your org.

**Step 1: Gather Your GitLab Server Details**

First things first, let's get some essential information from your GitLab Server:

*   **GitLab Server URL**: This is your gateway to accessing your GitLab Server. Look for an address in the format of `https://{your-git-domain}.com/`. Don't forget to replace `{your-git-domain}` with your actual domain.
    
*   **GitLab Server Version**: Compatibility is key, and knowing your GitLab Server version is crucial. Here's how to find it:
    
    *   Head over to your GitLab Server interface.
        
    *   Click on the 'Help' section. It’s usually at the end of your GitLab URL, like this: `/help`.
        
    *   You'll see your version info displayed, typically in the format of "GitLab Community Edition {x.x.x} / GitLab Enterprise Edition {x.x.x}".
        
    

**Step 2: Whitelist Necessary IP Addresses**

For a secure and uninterrupted connection, make sure to whitelist the following IP addresses:

*   **Mandatory IPs**:
    
    *   107.23.139.76
        
    *   3.219.89.23
        
    
*   **Recommended but Optional IPs**:
    
    *   45.119.114.218
        
    *   183.82.116.218
        
    

**Step 3: Creating a Personal Access Token (PAT):**

Let's create your PAT in GitLab:

*   Select 'Preferences'.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FwSRdR4516GeE2HUNRYqz%252Fimage%2520%287%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc57ebffc-c262-43ca-9250-42a6ef3b5dbd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b50bd3f2&sv=2)

*   Navigate to 'Access Tokens' in the left sidebar.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F3Hqyn7emceKVROnC67Nq%252Fimage%2520%288%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daaa7031a-f383-41e5-9b84-b023b7072aed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d0bb354d&sv=2)

*   Enter a token name and opt not to set an expiry date.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F1BqmBcgXqEzaFuW8vOML%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-19%2520at%25204.26.01%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db709f10d-9e86-467b-83bd-9069f4fe9c10&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ebdd528&sv=2)

*   Select the following scopes: `api, read_api, read_user, read_repository`.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FvdlQM7ApkHv730hIQJdx%252Fimage%2520%289%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a236f70-80b1-4005-be33-5edbbe566f14&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=76dbc3dc&sv=2)

*   Click 'Create personal access token'. **Note these scopes as they're crucial for integration**
    

**Step 4:** Navigate to the Hivel [sign-up pagearrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/signup)

**Step 5:** Add your work email id (If you'd like to use your personal email id please contact [\[email protected\])envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#2754525757485553674f4e51424b09464e0e)

**Step 6:** Now, you can use your Google or Microsoft login with your work email id; or create a password.

**Step 7:** Create your Company Profile, and click '**Get Started**'.

**Step 8:** Once you've successfully created your Company Profile, you will be redirected to the Integrations Page.

**Step 9:** Select Gitlab and log in to your company's Gitlab account using a service account.

**Step 10: Share Your Details**

You’ll need to provide the following:

*   Email, preferably a service account such as \[[\[email protected\]](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)\
    \]
    
*   Username
    
*   Personal Access Token (PAT) - return to the Hivel application, paste the personal access token, and hit **Submit.**
    

**Below are some screenshots of the steps you can refer to if needed:**

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F9Al1RETLnRQZ4jI3yVlL%252Fimage%2520%2820%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6497821d-9343-48c0-9151-01eb6a9ccb06&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1c39fb7&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FdejuQx5xvnK79sqk8SYq%252Fimage%2520%2821%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50e0fdff-46ea-40d1-ba37-f2869e69131b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3da3fb2&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FIfGHZJHIeObwoc1LdWPc%252Fimage%2520%2822%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D840f3ed7-cbef-476f-8dd0-9ac00d19a701&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=daf29f07&sv=2)

# Github Copilot Integration | Hivel

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/ai-tools/github-copilot-integration#log-in-to-hivel-through-a-copilot-admin-account)

Log in to Hivel through a Copilot admin account


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Ensure to use a Copilot admin account, which also has access to all the workspaces applicable for Copilot.
    
2.  Ensure the "Copilot Metrics API" in GitHub is enabled.
    
    1.  Settings >> Copilot >> Copilot Metrics API
        
    
3.  Navigate to the Integrations screen in the left panel.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F3JdSXZeJGYhiC0soSStJ%252Fimage%2520%2855%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f903e06-ad8f-4c49-88dd-5a72c8d1466f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64671346&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/ai-tools/github-copilot-integration#integrate-copilot)

Integrate Copilot


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Click on the Copilot integration card and follow the steps to redirect to your GitHub account.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F7i5e2MqTq2HgBWH9cbMJ%252Fimage%2520%2854%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe1ea0eb-059f-4ed0-8a26-437279cd336f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a3c1075&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F9SUOAxFK1NUCTpCZA9BW%252Fimage%2520%2853%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df71c2cb0-91b3-4044-a358-4cc5cc99a653&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49da9775&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/ai-tools/github-copilot-integration#grant-permissions-to-the-required-workspaces)

Grant permissions to the required workspaces


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once redirected to GitHub, authorize your organization's access by clicking on "Grant" against your organization.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F3L7eHybcEvUtPLJRlyQO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e939050-ce9f-4012-a062-6cae4448a710&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8cf7e691&sv=2)

All done! The data will be processed within 24 hours and you should be able to view the metrics in [Copilot Adoption screenarrow-up-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/copilot-adoption)
.

circle-info

In initial sync, we only have access to 28 days of historical data

# Why some of the repositories are not imported or synced? | Hivel

Sometimes, you might notice that certain repositories are listed as **not synced** in Hivel. This can happen due to the following reasons:

1.  **Lost Access**: Hivel no longer has access to the workspace or repository due to expired or revoked token permissions.
    
2.  **Inactivity**: The repository hasn’t had any recent activity, so no new data has been synced.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs/why-some-of-the-repositories-are-not-imported-or-synced#steps-to-fix-unsynced-repositories)

Steps to Fix Unsynced Repositories

To resolve this issue:

1.  **Reauthorize Hivel**: If access has been lost, reauthorize Hivel with the necessary permissions to the workspace or repository. This will restore synchronization and ensure data is up to date.
    
2.  **Check Repository Activity**: For inactive repositories, verify if they are expected to remain dormant or should have recent updates.
    

If you need further help, please contact our support team at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#33404643435c4147735b5a45565f1d525a)
.

[How to reauthorize Github with a classic token?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/alternate-methods/how-to-reauthorize-github-with-a-classic-token)
[How to re-authorize / re-initiate GitHub integration with account wide access?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-re-authorize-re-initiate-github-integration-with-account-wide-access)
[BitBucket Integrationchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/bitbucket-integration)
[Gitlabchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/gitlab)

# Release Notes - January 2025 | Hivel

We’re kicking off the year with a bang (well, a focused one)! January’s update brings a couple of exciting additions to start your 2025 on the right foot.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-january-2025#coding-hotspots-beta)

**Coding Hotspots (Beta)**

Our new _Coding Hotspots_ feature is here to help engineering teams identify the areas in the codebase that see the most bug activity. By analyzing JIRA issues, PRs, and commit history, it highlights the files most often modified due to bug fixes. This will help you focus on the right areas, improve code stability, and boost your team's efficiency.

_It’s currently available through a flag as we continue to iterate and enhance it. If you want to be an early adopter, please reach out to us🙌_

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FrgywFOJN5Vcy81HATPjm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f3baed2-5e36-4ca8-a933-ea182b7a4621&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e8300237&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FLb8uEYqU0tvmygObnvJD%252FScreen%2520Cast%25202025-04-01%2520at%25202.40.22%2520PM.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44b28733-399f-4fb0-9970-30b3cde0c39f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=53bdf745&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-january-2025#id-2024-wrapped)

**2024 Wrapped**:

Need a little end-of-year reflection? _2024 Wrapped_ brings you a summary of key metrics and highlights from last year - perfect for reflecting on accomplishments while you’re planning your 2025 goals. It’s like a year-in-review, but with more fun stats!

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FKOG1u12CpqKucZ0sSR9I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08e8da05-005f-4f44-942c-1cd385cc6245&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=382e1694&sv=2)

That's a wrap! Other than that, we’ve been hard at work planning the roadmap and making sure everything stays stable so you can hit the ground running in the new year. 🚀

**Time to debug your code and your caffeine levels for the new year** ☕️⚡️

# Release Notes - March 2025 | Hivel

Spring is here 🌱, and so is a fresh new set of updates! In March, we’ve been heads-down working on some major upgrades and a whole bunch of thoughtful enhancements to make your workflows smoother and smarter.

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-march-2025#introducing-cockpit-pro)

We’ve combined the best of _Cockpit_ and _Dashboards_ into a unified, intuitive experience called **Cockpit Pro**. It’s your go-to command center for metrics and insights. Here’s what’s new:

*   ✅ **Unified Boards & Templates** - All in one place with clear labels.
    
*   ⭐ **Favorites** - Pin your go-tos for quick access.

# How can I add a template in dashboards for my org to follow? | Hivel

**Custom Templates**:

*   The **Template** section in Dashboards does not currently support adding custom templates directly.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F1kP0uewI5VeYBsdGJ4Tz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28f91783-3959-488d-9aef-9d70e0469232&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=894b3367&sv=2)

*   However, you can reach out to our team, and we’ll configure the custom template for you. Contact us at **[\[email protected\]](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
    ** for assistance.
    

**Creating and Sharing Dashboards**:

*   Alternatively, you can create a **public dashboard**, which can be shared and accessed by other users.
    
*   **Note**: Only the **dashboard owner** has the ability to edit the dashboard, ensuring control over its content and structure.
    

For further questions or support, feel free to get in touch with our team!

[PreviousWhy some of the repositories are not imported or synced?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/pr-issues-and-workflow-faqs/why-some-of-the-repositories-are-not-imported-or-synced)
[NextSystem Behavior & Limitations FAQschevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/faqs/system-behavior-and-limitations-faqs)

# Gitlab Cloud | Hivel

**Data Access by Hivel**

*   Hivel accesses the past 60-90 days of commits and pull requests from active repositories during the initial sync.
    

**Authorization Mechanism**

*   Hivel employs GitLab's OAuth for authentication.
    
*   Users maintain full control and can withdraw access anytime via GitLab's authorized apps section.
    

**Requirements**

*   Ensure to log in with an account possessing write permissions to relevant GitLab repositories.
    
*   Write permissions are mandatory for webhook publication, facilitating real-time data sync.
    

**Best Practice**

*   Opt for a service account rather than an individual-linked account.
    
*   Service accounts are typically overseen by the company's admin.
    

**Create your Hivel Account**

1.  Navigate to the Hivel [sign-up pagearrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/signup)
    
2.  Add your work email id.
    
3.  Now, you can use your Google or Microsoft login with your work email id; or create a password.
    
4.  Create your Company Profile, and click '**Get Started**'.
    
5.  Once you've successfully created your Company Profile, you will be redirected to the Integrations Page.
    
6.  Select GitLab, and log in to your company's GitLab account using a service account.
    

**Connect GitLab**

1.  Next, you will be redirected to Hivel and prompted to add a **Personal Access Token.**
    
2.  To create a Personal Access Token, return to your GitLab account, and in the top-right corner, click your avatar.
    
3.  Select **Preferences**
    
4.  On the left sidebar, select **Access Tokens**.
    
5.  Enter a name, and do not set any expiry date for the token.
    
6.  Select the [desired scopesarrow-up-right](https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/user/profile/personal_access_tokens.html#personal-access-token-scopes)
     - api, read\_api, read\_user, read\_repository
    
7.  Select **Create personal access token**, and copy it.
    
8.  Return to the Hivel application, paste the personal access token, and hit **Submit**.
    

Once the token is validated, and your GitLab is successfully integrated, we will start to pull data. It will take between 2 - 48 hours for the complete sync, depending on the volume of the data.

**Below are some screenshots of the steps you can refer to if needed:**

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FEgtVdyFeQ6ZOHMXUsUdX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99e16bfc-989c-4161-99ae-1b351832b329&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d43d387&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F9Al1RETLnRQZ4jI3yVlL%252Fimage%2520%2820%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6497821d-9343-48c0-9151-01eb6a9ccb06&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1c39fb7&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FdejuQx5xvnK79sqk8SYq%252Fimage%2520%2821%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50e0fdff-46ea-40d1-ba37-f2869e69131b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3da3fb2&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FIfGHZJHIeObwoc1LdWPc%252Fimage%2520%2822%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D840f3ed7-cbef-476f-8dd0-9ac00d19a701&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=daf29f07&sv=2)

# DORA Metrics Powered by New APIs in Hivel | Hivel

We’ve launched two new APIs - Deployment API and Incident API - to improve how DORA metrics are calculated in Hivel. These updates make the metrics more accurate, reliable, and real-time, giving you better insights into your team’s delivery and reliability.

With these new APIs, you can now integrate Hivel with any tool in your workflow, and the DORA metrics will be calculated consistently based on real-time data.

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/dora-metrics-powered-by-new-apis-in-hivel#whats-changed)

What’s Changed?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/dora-metrics-powered-by-new-apis-in-hivel#new-api-powered-dora-metrics)

New API-Powered DORA Metrics

With the launch of the new APIs, we’ve introduced new API-powered DORA metrics for even greater accuracy. These metrics give you real-time visibility into your delivery pipeline:

Metric

What It Means

Data Source

Change Failure Rate (CFR)

The percentage of deployments that result in a failure.

Incident API

Mean Time to Restore (MTTR)

The time taken to restore a service from a production failure.

Incident API

Deployment Frequency (DF)

The number of times that code changes are successfully deployed to production.

Deployment API

Delivery Lead Time

The time from code commit to successful deployment in production.

Deployment API

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/dora-metrics-powered-by-new-apis-in-hivel#weve-also-renamed-some-of-the-older-dora-metrics-to-reflect-this-update.-heres-a-quick-look)

We’ve also renamed some of the older DORA metrics to reflect this update. Here’s a quick look:

Old Name

New Name

What It Means

CFR (Change Failure Rate)

Hotfix Rate

PRs merged to release branches with the hotfix pattern as configured.

MTTR (Mean Time to Restore)

Hotfix Resolution Time

Cycle time of all PRs merged to release branches with the hotfix pattern as configured.

Deployment Frequency

Release Merge Frequency

No. of PRs merged to release branches as per configuration.

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/dora-metrics-powered-by-new-apis-in-hivel#how-to-enable-these-metrics)

How to Enable These Metrics


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start viewing the new API-powered DORA metrics, make sure you’ve connected both the Deployment API and Incident API to your workspace.

1.  In Hivel application navigate to Integrations → **CI/CD Section**
    
2.  Connect the Deployment API for the following metrics:
    
    1.  Deployment Frequency
        
    2.  Delivery Lead Time
        
    
    👉 [View Integration Guidearrow-up-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/deployment-events-api)
    
3.  Connect the Incident API for the following metrics:
    
    1.  Hotfix Rate
        
    2.  Hotfix Resolution Time
        
    
    👉 [View Integration Guidearrow-up-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api)
    

Once the APIs are connected, your DORA metrics will automatically update with data from these integrations.

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/dora-metrics-powered-by-new-apis-in-hivel#where-youll-see-these-changes)

Where You’ll See These Changes


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The newly calculated DORA metrics will appear wherever DORA metrics are displayed. For areas that previously used the old calculation method, you’ll now see the renamed metrics.

Here’s where the changes apply:

1.  **Cockpit**
    
    1.  The DORA DASHBOARD - NEW board will include the metrics powered from Deployment and Incident API
        
    2.  The old metrics will appear in other boards renamed to Hotfix Rate, Hotfix Resolution Time, Release Merge Frequency.
        
    3.  These changes will be reflected in all the dashboards, graphical and tabular views
        
    
2.  **PR Screen**
    
    1.  In the Pull Request screen, the top-level metric cards have been renamed to match the updated terminology.
        
    2.  They now align with the same logic used in the Cockpit, providing consistency across views.
        
    

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/dora-metrics-powered-by-new-apis-in-hivel#why-this-change-matters)

Why This Change Matters


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By using the Deployment API and Incident API, DORA metrics in Hivel are now more accurate, real-time, and consistent across tools.

You can integrate any tool with Hivel, and your metrics will follow a standard calculation method every time.

The renamed old metrics remain available for those who prefer the earlier approach, while the new APIs ensure your DORA insights stay aligned with modern engineering practices.

[PreviousCreate Incident APIchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api)
[NextOn-Prem Setupchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup)

Last updated 4 months ago

*   [What’s Changed?](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/dora-metrics-powered-by-new-apis-in-hivel#whats-changed)
    
*   [New API-Powered DORA Metrics](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/dora-metrics-powered-by-new-apis-in-hivel#new-api-powered-dora-metrics)

# How to integrate GitHub with account wide access? | Hivel

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-account-wide-access#data-access-by-hivel)

Data Access by Hivel

*   Hivel accesses the past 60-90 days of commits and pull requests from active repositories during the initial sync.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-account-wide-access#authorization-mechanism)

Authorization Mechanism

*   Hivel employs GitHub's OAuth for authentication.
    
*   Users maintain full control and can withdraw access anytime via GitHub's authorized apps section.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-account-wide-access#requirements)

Requirements

*   Ensure to log in with an account possessing write permissions to relevant GitHub repositories.
    
*   Write permissions are mandatory for webhook publication, facilitating real-time data sync.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-account-wide-access#best-practice)

Best Practice

*   Opt for a service account rather than an individual-linked account.
    
*   Service accounts are typically overseen by the company's admin.
    

**Permissions Required**

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FfuGFYrIfn5oKmyDnw7jx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c265b13-9ca8-453d-aac0-66fa167d5b25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b6c22aa&sv=2)

circle-check

**You can either create a service account or use one with access to only the required workspaces.**

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-account-wide-access#how-to-create-a-service-account-and-give-access-to-the-required-workspaces)

How to create a service account and give access to the required workspaces

circle-info

Skip this section if you are using an existing account with required access.

1.  Sign up on [github.comarrow-up-right](https://github.com/)
     using a generic email ID which does not belong to any developer and can be accessed by the admin.
    
2.  Once created, open the required workspace using an admin account.
    
3.  Under **People** section, click on **Invite member** to invite the newly created service account.
    
4.  Do the same for **all the required workspaces**.
    
5.  Once invited, log into the account mail and **accept the invite**. This will give the service account permission for only the required workspaces.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FDmotpSsSvrB8r1MBb0T5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc92a0ff2-6213-4940-bce6-63d9ae5057d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ce3bf79&sv=2)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-account-wide-access#sign-in-to-hivel)

**Sign in to Hivel**

1.  Navigate to the Hivel [sign-up pagearrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/signup)
    
2.  Add your work email id (If you'd like to use your personal email id please contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#7a090f0a0a15080e3a12130c1f16541b13)
    
3.  Now, you can use your Google or Microsoft login with your work email id; or create a password.
    
4.  Create your Company Profile, and click '**Get Started**'.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FfVfy42xatexMl1W1PPI9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9f44662-e81f-4b21-b7cf-8704c7a24322&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71c8eb56&sv=2)
    
5.  Once you've successfully created your Company Profile you will be redirected to the Integrations Page under **Settings.**
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FnJ0BKgHQiKefu7VRE9lr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee8a5e0a-82a8-4cc0-9baa-5aa656b52b74&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e622d9fa&sv=2)
    
6.  Select GitHub, and use your company's GitHub account (**either service account or the account which has access to the required workspaces**).
    
7.  Click on **Connect.**
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FUQAoNSCeIcGUzlnNLtbP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ba1f406-10f8-4eaa-ac5f-5a91dbb7d506&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=535b945c&sv=2)
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FDxJ4nfVPl7dPBiS9zIor%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2527cee4-5417-47f8-b07f-cbf97f74ec00&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd151182&sv=2)
    
8.  Click '**Integrate Github**' .
    
9.  Make sure you click on '**Gran**t' all the organization you want to integrate with Hivel.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FhqkNBgy8OVtUGxOWy10H%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31cb29df-456e-4635-a852-fe8950a24d72&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86328a10&sv=2)
    
10.  After authorization, you'll be redirected back to Hivel.
    

Once your GitHub is successfully integrated, we will start to pull data. It will take between 2 - 48 hours for the complete sync, depending on the volume of the data.

# How to integrate GitHub with repository level access? | Hivel

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-repository-level-access#data-access-by-hivel)

Data Access by Hivel

*   Hivel accesses the past 60-90 days of commits and pull requests from active repositories during the initial sync.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-repository-level-access#authorization-mechanism)

Authorization Mechanism

*   In this method, Hivel uses the GitHub app flow for the integration
    
*   Users maintain full control and can withdraw access anytime via GitHub's authorized apps section.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-repository-level-access#requirements)

Requirements

*   Ensure to log in with an account possessing write permissions to relevant GitHub repositories.
    
*   Write permissions are mandatory for webhook publication, facilitating real-time data sync.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-repository-level-access#best-practice)

Best Practice

*   Opt for a service account rather than an individual-linked account.
    
*   Service accounts are typically overseen by the company's admin.
    

**Permissions Required**

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FABRVnlQnvDwT3ruSrAO8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D76b2eea4-8e43-4bc4-a2c1-c2306d331969&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1cc366b9&sv=2)

circle-check

**You can either create a service account or use one with access to only the required workspaces.**

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-repository-level-access#how-to-create-a-service-account-and-give-access-to-the-required-workspaces)

How to create a service account and give access to the required workspaces

circle-info

Skip this section if you are using an existing account with required access.

1.  Sign up on [github.comarrow-up-right](https://github.com/)
     using a generic email ID which does not belong to any developer and can be accessed by the admin.
    
2.  Once created, open the required workspace using an admin account.
    
3.  Under **People** section, click on **Invite member** to invite the newly created service account.
    
4.  Do the same for **all the required workspaces**.
    
5.  Once invited, log into the account mail and **accept the invite**. This will give the service account permission for only the required workspaces.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FDmotpSsSvrB8r1MBb0T5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc92a0ff2-6213-4940-bce6-63d9ae5057d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ce3bf79&sv=2)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-integrate-github-with-repository-level-access#sign-in-to-hivel)

**Sign in to Hivel**

1.  Navigate to the Hivel [sign-up pagearrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/signup)
    
2.  Add your work email id (If you'd like to use your personal email id please contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#afdcdadfdfc0dddbefc7c6d9cac381cec6)
    
3.  Now, you can use your Google or Microsoft login with your work email ID, or create a password.
    
4.  Create your Company Profile, and click '**Get Started**'.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FfVfy42xatexMl1W1PPI9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9f44662-e81f-4b21-b7cf-8704c7a24322&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71c8eb56&sv=2)
    
5.  Once you've successfully created your Company Profile you will be redirected to the Integrations Page under **Settings.**
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FnJ0BKgHQiKefu7VRE9lr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee8a5e0a-82a8-4cc0-9baa-5aa656b52b74&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e622d9fa&sv=2)
    
6.  Select GitHub, and use your company's GitHub account (**either service account or the account which has access to the required workspaces**).
    
7.  Click on **Connect.**
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FUQAoNSCeIcGUzlnNLtbP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ba1f406-10f8-4eaa-ac5f-5a91dbb7d506&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=535b945c&sv=2)
    
8.  Select **"Repository-level Access"**
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FXXgJEQ9Dot4A7BHWRdrW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a2a513f-8e46-42d6-ae24-c5fb07043a05&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=29d18fee&sv=2)
    
9.  You will be redirected to the Github app installation page where you have to click on **"Install"** for the Hivel app.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FCq09HXVFl6P3WsU4rl1V%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2b21731-5919-4164-89a8-e48135e7094b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=427a8699&sv=2)
    
10.  Select the org where you want to integrate Hivel
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FLP5apfvYnVDl5ueb9wmw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5924cae-b659-4814-a53d-ec70cbdd87c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcb38c30&sv=2)
    
11.  You can either select to give access to all repositories or a few select repositories as required.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fbojnf2r0vYiSxg9B2UkW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3fa83c2-f8fb-49e6-9210-80c06cebf92a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=970708b5&sv=2)
    
12.  Click '**Install & Authorize'**.
    
13.  After authorization, you'll be redirected back to Hivel.
    

Once your GitHub is successfully integrated, we will start to pull data. It will take between 2 - 48 hours for the complete sync, depending on the volume of the data.

# Release Notes - October 2025 | Hivel

October’s updates are all about **clarity and control**.

From knowing exactly how fresh your data is, to drilling into commits behind every sprint, to tracking rework vs new work goals - these changes help you make faster, data-backed decisions with full context.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-october-2025#know-exactly-when-your-data-was-last-synced)

**Know Exactly When Your Data Was Last Synced**

A new **“Last Date Refreshed”** label now appears on every integration card, so you can instantly see when your data last synced.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F3Fv2oxwOW4DJK2gAviTn%252FScreenshot%25202025-11-07%2520at%25202.48.07%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5af742ab-41a7-4894-a832-c6e08d23b41b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a388853&sv=2)

You don't need to guess anymore if your Git or PM tool is up to date. If it hasn’t refreshed in a week, you’ll see:

> _“Data refreshed more than a week ago. Please contact support.”_

This helps you catch stale data early and keep your dashboards reliable.

**Works with:** GitHub, GitLab, Bitbucket, Azure, Jira, Freshrelease, Cursor, Copilot, Sonar, Google Calendar, and Outlook Calendar.

👉 [**Check it out**arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/settings/integrations)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-october-2025#go-deeper-in-the-investment-screen)

**Go Deeper in the Investment Screen**

The **Investment** screen now lets you open up what’s behind the numbers.

Both **PR counts** and **commit counts** are clickable, so you can jump straight from a metric to the actual work that drove it.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FsRSNKJKOkYQcMVBXosGr%252FScreenshot%25202025-11-07%2520at%25202.52.21%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a8571d2-ffd7-4aef-b42f-5119256d5627&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4d4435fb&sv=2)

Perfect for sprint reviews or team retros when you want to connect outcomes to the effort that went into them.

**Available for:** Jira Cloud, Jira Server, Azure, and Freshrelease users.

👉 [**Try it out**arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/dashboard/investment-profile)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-october-2025#goals-pro-now-tracks-new-work-and-rework)

**Goals PRO Now Tracks New Work and Rework**

We’ve added **New Work** and **Rework** metrics to **Goals PRO**, to help you see how your teams balance building new features vs fixing or maintaining existing ones.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FhNfLTnY1w8d9lhRMJZkM%252FScreenshot%25202025-11-07%2520at%25202.56.17%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2afe6b45-477c-4538-81cf-7c1faa59f04c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c5337d&sv=2)

You can now set more meaningful targets, like reducing rework over time or increasing the share of new work in a sprint.

👉 [**Explore it now**arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/dashboard/goals)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-october-2025#wrapping-up-october)

☕ **Wrapping Up October**

Hope this month’s updates help you with sharper visibility, up-to-date data, and metrics that tell a fuller story.

As the year winds down, remember this: sustainable pace beats sprinting to burnout. So take a breather, review your wins, and let the data guide your next move.

Here’s to finishing 2025 strong 💪✨

[PreviousRelease Notes - November 2025chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-november-2025)
[NextRelease Notes - September 2025chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-september-2025)

# Strategies to Reduce Hotfix Resolution Time | Hivel

[Hotfix Resolution Time](https://docs.hivel.ai/metrics-and-definitions/quality/hotfix-resolution-time)
 is the average time taken to resolve any bugs or push hotfixes to production.

Here are some actionable strategies to reduce the average cycle time for hotfix PRs, ensuring quick resolution of production bugs and maintaining system reliability:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-1.-create-a-rapid-code-review-process-for-hotfix-prs)

**1\. Create a Rapid Code Review Process for Hotfix PRs**

*   **Why It's Important**: Code reviews can become bottlenecks. Streamlining this process for hotfixes ensures that fixes are approved and merged quickly.
    
*   **Impact**: Speeds up the transition from code completion to deployment, reducing waiting times in the pipeline.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-2.-automate-testing-and-deployment-pipelines-for-hotfixes)

**2\. Automate Testing and Deployment Pipelines for Hotfixes**

*   **Why It's Important**: Automation eliminates manual steps that can introduce delays and errors. Automated pipelines validate and deploy hotfixes swiftly.
    
*   **Impact**: Significantly cuts down the time between code submission and deployment to production.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-3.-enhance-logging-monitoring-and-alerting-systems)

**3\. Enhance Logging, Monitoring, and Alerting Systems**

*   **Why It's Important**: Quickly identifying and diagnosing issues is half the battle. Enhanced observability tools help teams pinpoint problems faster.
    
*   **Impact**: Reduces the time spent on root cause analysis, allowing fixes to be developed sooner.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-4.-establish-a-dedicated-hotfix-workflow)

**4\. Establish a Dedicated Hotfix Workflow**

*   **Why It's Important**: A separate workflow for hotfixes prevents interference with ongoing development and simplifies the process.
    
*   **Impact**: Streamlines the hotfix process, reducing complexity and potential delays.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-5.-implement-feature-flags-and-toggle-systems)

**5\. Implement Feature Flags and Toggle Systems**

*   **Why It's Important**: Feature flags allow you to disable problematic features immediately without a full deployment.
    
*   **Impact**: Provides an immediate mitigation strategy, reducing the urgency and pressure on the hotfix cycle.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-6.-maintain-an-up-to-date-knowledge-base-and-runbooks)

**6\. Maintain an Up-to-Date Knowledge Base and Runbooks**

*   **Why It's Important**: Documentation of previous issues and solutions aids in faster troubleshooting.
    
*   **Impact**: Decreases the time engineers spend figuring out fixes by leveraging existing knowledge.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-7.-conduct-regular-post-incident-reviews-and-implement-improvements)

**7\. Conduct Regular Post-Incident Reviews and Implement Improvements**

*   **Why It's Important**: Learning from past incidents helps identify process weaknesses.
    
*   **Impact**: Leads to continuous improvement, gradually reducing cycle times over the long term.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-8.-allocate-buffer-time-in-sprints-for-unplanned-work)

**8\. Allocate Buffer Time in Sprints for Unplanned Work**

*   **Why It's Important**: Recognizing that unplanned work will occur allows teams to handle it without derailing planned tasks.
    
*   **Impact**: Ensures that hotfixes can be addressed promptly without significant impact on other deliverables.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#summary-of-priorities)

**Summary of Priorities**:

*   **Immediate Response**: Start by ensuring that issues are addressed as soon as they occur.
    
*   **Process Efficiency**: Streamline the processes that get fixes from development to production quickly.
    
*   **Effective Communication**: Keep everyone informed and coordinated to prevent delays.
    
*   **Preventative Measures**: Use tools and practices that minimize the need for hotfixes or mitigate their impact.
    
*   **Continuous Improvement**: Learn from each incident to improve future responses.
    

By prioritizing and focusing on these strategies, you'll address the most critical factors that impact the cycle time of hotfix PRs. Implementing them will lead to faster resolution of production bugs and a more resilient system overall.

[PreviousBest Practices for Ensuring Strong Pull Request Review Coveragechevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage)
[NextBest Practices for Team Ownership in Code Reviewchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [2\. Automate Testing and Deployment Pipelines for Hotfixes](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-2.-automate-testing-and-deployment-pipelines-for-hotfixes)
    
*   [3\. Enhance Logging, Monitoring, and Alerting Systems](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-3.-enhance-logging-monitoring-and-alerting-systems)
    
*   [4\. Establish a Dedicated Hotfix Workflow](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-4.-establish-a-dedicated-hotfix-workflow)
    
*   [5\. Implement Feature Flags and Toggle Systems](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-5.-implement-feature-flags-and-toggle-systems)
    
*   [6\. Maintain an Up-to-Date Knowledge Base and Runbooks](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-6.-maintain-an-up-to-date-knowledge-base-and-runbooks)
    
*   [7\. Conduct Regular Post-Incident Reviews and Implement Improvements](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-7.-conduct-regular-post-incident-reviews-and-implement-improvements)
    
*   [8\. Allocate Buffer Time in Sprints for Unplanned Work](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time#id-8.-allocate-buffer-time-in-sprints-for-unplanned-work)

# How to re-authorize / re-initiate GitHub integration with repository level access? | Hivel

Hivel currently only supports GitHub accounts that are associated with an organization. Often, this step is missed when setting up a GitHub account, and you may have run into an error when creating an account on Hivel. When you encounter this error during the initial process, we recommend you follow the below steps to create an organization and link your current users to the organization.

To re-initiate/reauthorize GitHub integration with Hivel, follow these steps:

1.  Log in to your GitHub account.
    
2.  Revoke the Hivel app access from your GitHub account by going to **Settings** > **Account Settings** > **Third Party apps** > **GitHub apps** \> **Hivel**.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FcteoWfRBaqHlWm9Vdnyn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc9ee32c-2e1d-40dc-9508-d794927394c6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d8b0a53&sv=2)
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FUwzhvjlXRSzcMmYx3rk5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b1b3c19-04cc-4fe2-99a2-083b55865540&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=393d94ab&sv=2)
    
3.  Click on **Configure** -> Scroll down and **uninstall** the app.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FfmZrATleOdb5uBDuYPG5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7ee2f2c-fda4-48bd-a1d3-520c5ecaef89&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=14d88dda&sv=2)
    
4.  Return to your Hivel account. Go to **Settings > Integrations**. You will see a "**Reauthorize**" button on the GitHub card. (If you're not able to see it, please reach out to [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#87f4f2f7f7e8f5f3c7efeef1e2eba9e6ee)
    )
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fy5wce2u7JLmBK47b8ORs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f39c82b-ff80-4836-bc11-8ee4d4d4686a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cdba05a1&sv=2)

1.  Select **"Repository-level Access"**
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FXXgJEQ9Dot4A7BHWRdrW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a2a513f-8e46-42d6-ae24-c5fb07043a05&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=29d18fee&sv=2)
    
2.  You will be redirected to the Github app installation page where you have to click on **"Install"** for the Hivel app.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FCq09HXVFl6P3WsU4rl1V%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2b21731-5919-4164-89a8-e48135e7094b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=427a8699&sv=2)
    
3.  Select the org where you want to integrate Hivel
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FLP5apfvYnVDl5ueb9wmw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5924cae-b659-4814-a53d-ec70cbdd87c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcb38c30&sv=2)
    
4.  You can either select to give access to all repositories or a few select repositories as required.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fbojnf2r0vYiSxg9B2UkW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3fa83c2-f8fb-49e6-9210-80c06cebf92a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=970708b5&sv=2)
    
5.  Click '**Install & Authorize'**.
    
6.  After authorization, you'll be redirected back to Hivel.
    

[PreviousHow to re-authorize / re-initiate GitHub integration with account wide access?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/how-to-re-authorize-re-initiate-github-integration-with-account-wide-access)

# How to re-authorize / re-initiate GitHub integration with account wide access? | Hivel

Hivel currently only supports GitHub accounts that are associated with an organization. Often, this step is missed when setting up a GitHub account, and you may have run into an error when creating an account on Hivel. When you encounter this error during the initial process, we recommend you follow the below steps to create an organization and link your current users to the organization.

To re-initiate/reauthorize GitHub integration with Hivel, follow these steps:

1.  Log in to your GitHub account.
    
2.  Revoke the Hivel app access from your GitHub account by going to **Settings** > **Account Settings** > **Applications** > **Authorized OAuth Apps** \> **Hivel**. Then click "**Revoke"**.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FmdmKmvrBd42oy7MFJV3D%252Fimage%2520%28115%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b8b6811-455b-4a40-862b-fe0c34a214c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d0dc8d4&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdO0aQ1F_fo-mKURqlUU_hC6mYFRamiPBEEjh1M-84GVDUza2ZEyW5KF-JNp6VYEr3VcB7AcNl8MANHvHG6VKPqaU7ccqGpxxzgdsoDh9NNpa4Uuhsz9Mli6-wxbMZslfwTVgw5PXsaDudUVyQaAfCLzuA%3Fkey%3D7e-FYm3-NHwQUjNXOPEkIw&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45133139&sv=2)

1.  Return to your Hivel account. Go to **Settings > Integrations**. You will see a "**Reauthorize**" button on the GitHub card. (If you're not able to see it, please reach out to [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a2d1d7d2d2cdd0d6e2cacbd4c7ce8cc3cb)
    )
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fy5wce2u7JLmBK47b8ORs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f39c82b-ff80-4836-bc11-8ee4d4d4686a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cdba05a1&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FuZgq9AEy8MYSnDIflwh1%252Fimage%2520%2873%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6b575045-de0a-4859-936b-9fcc26dda88f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=440643ef&sv=2)

`Authorize your organization's access by clicking on "``**Grant**``" against your organization.`
