# How to integrate Jira Server with Hivel | Hivel

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/jira/how-to-integrate-jira-server-with-hivel#before-starting-integration-make-sure-to-whitelist-the-following-ip-addresses)

Before starting integration, make sure to whitelist the following IP addresses:

*   **Recommended, but Optional IPs**:
    
    *   45.119.114.218
        
    *   183.82.116.218
        
    
*   **Mandatory IPs**:
    
    *   107.23.139.76
        
    *   3.219.89.23
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/jira/how-to-integrate-jira-server-with-hivel#to-start-the-integration-follow-the-below-steps)

To start the integration, follow the below steps:

1.  Log in to your Hivel account.
    
2.  In the left panel, select **Settings**, and go to the **Integrations** tab.
    
3.  Find the Jira card and click the **'Connect'** button.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fzhy3HFBOwDRS8H4m0C0P%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deec1abce-ecf2-46e6-8c73-5b9d1c273c71&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a569975&sv=2)
    
4.  In the pop-up, paste the link of your Jira domain and press "Enter" key. A link to Jira application page will be generated. Click on the link.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F3pt2idXkj8V5tRXMo2Ph%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73b0e2a0-0cff-437c-a1a4-604fed42b8c9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=871e78c2&sv=2)
    
5.  You'll be redirected to your Jira account. Click on **Create Link.**
    
6.  Select **Direct Application Link** and paste our application's link - [https://app.hivel.aiarrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/dashboard/cto)
    . Click on continue.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FIchDsFQAUqPThzOScS5b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df63f0fa6-e496-4018-937d-30a0884fdda3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66635b20&sv=2)
    
7.  Copy the **Application Name** from Hivel's integration page and paste in the recent pop-up in Jira. Select **Application Type** as "Generic Application". Click on continue.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FKtQr7pDrojLvcSLd8ZNJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D426e32bf-6f97-49bb-9184-45859797ffa2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b73369c&sv=2)
    
    _From Hivel's integration page_
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F7w6tf9QHwfAJXPABnBe2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf768d90-4c3b-4527-84fc-2b34f1185d69&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c627dc55&sv=2)
    
    _Jira pop-up_
    
8.  A new entry will be added in the Jira Application Link page. Click on the 3 dots in the new entry and select Configure.
    
9.  Go to **Incoming Authentication.**
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fr5nxvIffcbujOeJ6hmF6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4df9488d-d269-44ff-9413-f6c32ed8f620&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e69e6963&sv=2)
    
10.  Copy the **Consumer Key**, **Consumer Name**, **Public Key**, and **Redirection Link** from Hivel integration page and paste in the Incoming Authentication tab in Jira. Then, hit “Save”.
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FrEIojpX1k7VAzrX7uFVk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D876b9329-166d-462c-8ed6-7bba936fea05&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28cc1694&sv=2)
    
11.  Go back to the Hivel's integration page and click on **Submit.** In case an error pops up, please repeat the above processes again. If everything is set up correctly, it will get connected.
    

Done! Data will be refreshed within 24 hours.

circle-info

_**Note:**_ Make sure to connect Jira with the **admin account**.

For any issues or assistance, feel free to reach us at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#ddaea8adadb2afa99db5b4abb8b1f3bcb4)
.

[PreviousHow to Re-authorize Jira with OAuth 2.0chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/jira/how-to-re-authorize-jira-with-oauth-2.0)
[NextAzure Boardschevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/azure-boards)

*   [To start the integration, follow the below steps:](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/jira/how-to-integrate-jira-server-with-hivel#to-start-the-integration-follow-the-below-steps)

# Release Notes - February 2025 | Hivel

February brought some exciting updates that we’re sure your teams will love!

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-february-2025#jenkins-pipeline-metrics-is-now-live)

**Jenkins - Pipeline Metrics is Now Live!**

We’re thrilled to introduce the **Jenkins Pipelines Metrics** feature, now live in production! You can track Jenkins success and failed builds directly from your Custom Dashboards page under _Pipeline Metrics_. Plus, you’ll also see the average build run duration. Not yet set up? No worries - follow the [_steps to integrate Jenkins_arrow-up-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/jenkins)
 and start tracking today.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FIfg9cAaYGZEvrbcwG9Ww%252FScreen%2520Cast%25202025-04-01%2520at%25202.51.50%2520PM.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72847cf9-862e-4770-ae17-9a345369ec09&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1abf4b96&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-february-2025#rbac-role-based-access-control)

**RBAC (Role-Based Access Control)**

Managing user permissions just became a breeze with our new **RBAC system**. You can now define roles and assign permissions effortlessly, including access to specific screens, editing configurations, excluding PRs, and more. If user access control is a priority for your team, this update is a must-check!

[_Link to RBAC configurations_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/settings/rbac)

And that’s it for February - two major updates to streamline your workflow.

**Time to refactor your permissions... and maybe your work-life balance too!** ⚙️🧘‍♂️

# Best Practices for Team Ownership in Code Review | Hivel

Effective code review practices are vital for maintaining high-quality code and fostering a culture of collaboration and learning within development teams. Here are some best practices for promoting team ownership in the code review process:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review#define-clear-ownership-and-responsibilities)

**Define clear ownership and responsibilities**

*   Establish clear ownership of different modules or features within the team. Each team member should know their responsibilities and the areas of the codebase they own.
    
*   This clarity helps ensure that the right individuals are reviewing changes to the code they are most familiar with, leading to more effective and efficient reviews.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review#implement-a-peer-review-system)

**Implement a peer review system**

*   Encourage a peer review system where every piece of code must be reviewed by one or more team members before merging.
    
*   Peer reviews not only improve code quality and catch errors early but also enhance team collaboration and knowledge sharing.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review#use-automated-tools)

**Use automated tools**

*   Leverage automated code review tools (like SonarQube, CodeClimate, or GitHub’s built-in tools) to handle basic code quality checks, style enforcement, and security scans.
    
*   Automation frees human reviewers to focus on more complex aspects of the code, such as architecture and design principles, rather than syntax errors or style inconsistencies.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review#establish-review-standards-and-checklists)

**Establish review standards and checklists**

*   Develop and maintain a code review checklist that includes both general and project-specific criteria to be checked during the review.
    
*   Checklists standardize the review process and help ensure completeness in the review, reducing the chance of missing key issues.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review#promote-constructive-feedback)

**Promote constructive feedback**

*   Encourage reviewers to provide constructive, specific, and respectful feedback. Comments should be clear and actionable.
    
*   Positive and constructive feedback enhances learning and keeps the review process from becoming adversarial, fostering a supportive team environment.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review#encourage-pair-programming)

**Encourage pair programming**

*   Implement pair programming sessions, especially for complex features or bug fixes, where two developers write code together at the same workstation.
    
*   Pair programming can reduce the need for extensive code reviews later as it incorporates continuous code review and mutual learning.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review#track-and-act-on-review-metrics)

**Track and act on review metrics**

*   Monitor metrics such as [review timearrow-up-right](https://hivel.gitbook.io/knowlegebase/metrics-and-definitions/speed/review-time)
    , [number of iterations per PRarrow-up-right](https://hivel.gitbook.io/knowlegebase/using-hivel/pull-request/review-cycles)
    , and [defect ratesarrow-up-right](https://hivel.gitbook.io/knowlegebase/metrics-and-definitions/quality/change-failure-rate)
    . Use this data to refine the review process.
    
*   Tracking these metrics helps identify bottlenecks and areas for improvement, allowing teams to adjust practices and workload distribution effectively.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review#regularly-rotate-review-roles)

**Regularly rotate review roles**

*   Rotate code review assignments among team members to ensure that everyone stays familiar with different parts of the codebase.
    
*   This rotation promotes a more comprehensive understanding of the project and prevents silos from forming within the team.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review#review-the-review-process)

**Review the review process**

*   Periodically review and refine the code review process itself based on team feedback and evolving project needs.
    
*   Continual improvement of the review process ensures that it remains effective and relevant as the team and project evolve.
    

By integrating these best practices, your team can foster a sense of ownership and pride in their work, leading to higher quality software and more engaged and knowledgeable team members.

[PreviousStrategies to Reduce Hotfix Resolution Timechevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time)
[NextHow to identify root cases of high change failure rates?chevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/how-to-identify-root-cases-of-high-change-failure-rates)

*   [Implement a peer review system](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-team-ownership-in-code-review#implement-a-peer-review-system)

# Create Incident API | Hivel

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Hivel Incident API enables submitting incident data to Hivel, allowing for precise calculation of metrics such as CFR (Change Failure Rate) and MTTR (Mean Time to Recovery).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api#base-url)

Base URL

The base URL for accessing Hivel may vary depending on your organization's configuration. Please make sure to select the appropriate base URL according to your setup.

The URL will be either of these:

`**https://app.hivel.ai**` OR `**https://app.hivel.in**`

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api#authentication)

🔑 Authentication

All requests require an organization API token. Pass this in the request header:

Copy

    Authorization: YOUR_ORGANIZATION_API_TOKEN

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api#retrieving-your-api-key)

Retrieving Your API Key


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Open Hivel and navigate to **Integrations** under the **Settings**.
    
2.  Click on **Connect** on **Hivel API Authorization card**
    
    ![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FpZ80VBIdJuv8BsrwZdOI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0869583b-b6f0-4cda-a6b1-bd1ffc53c640&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57e2ed7c&sv=2)
    
3.  Follow the given steps to start your integration
    
4.  By clicking on **Generate** your API Key will be generated.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FRj7txCE1jkzHG2J822yp%252Fimage%2520%2898%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2759fa06-84bf-4094-879e-8b10ee6d4281&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66417070&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FoXU4heOSD8LS7QSB9Ve5%252Fimage%2520%2899%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9958254-4dd1-4120-ba69-a1074ce45ddc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=20742e08&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api#incident-events-api)

Incident Events API


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api#endpoint)

Endpoint

`POST` `https://app.hivel.ai/api/hooks/v1/incident`

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api#request-parameters)

**Request Parameters**

Field Name

Type

Description

Example

`description`

string

A detailed description of the incident (max 255 chars).

Database connection timeout error

`severity`

Required

string

The severity level of the incident (e.g., low, medium, high, critical) (max 255 chars).

high

`affected_systems`

array

A list of systems affected by the incident.

\["database", "backend"\]

`reported_time`

Required

string

The date and time when the incident occurred (ISO 8601 format).

2024-08-01T12:34:56Z

`reported_by`

string

The username or identifier of the person who reported the incident (max 255 chars).

jdoe

`resolution_time`

Required

string

The date and time when the incident was resolved (ISO 8601 format).

2024-08-01T13:34:56Z

`provider_id`

string

The unique identifier of the incident in your incident management provider (max 255 chars).

incident-123456

`repo_url`

Required

string

The URL of the repository related to the deployment or incident (max 255 chars).

[https://github.com/your-repo/projectarrow-up-right](https://github.com/your-repo/project)

`pr_number`

Required

string

The Pull Request (PR) identifier associated with the deployment.

44

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api#request-example)

**Request Example**

Example

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/api-documentation/create-incident-api#response)

Response

200 - Successful

*   `400` - Bad Request
    
*   `401` - Unauthorized
    
*   `500` - Internal Server Error

    --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
    --data-raw '{
      "description": "Database connection timeout affecting API",
      "severity": "HIGH",
      "affected_systems": ["database", "api-gateway"],
      "reported_time": "2025-09-22T10:30:00Z",
      "reported_by": "[email protected]",
      "resolution_time": "2025-09-22T11:15:00Z",
      "provider_id": "inc-20250922-1030",
      "repo_url": "https://github.com/hivelai/webhook-logger",
      "pr_number": "71"
    }'

Copy

    {
      "message": "Success",
      "incident_id": "incident-2024-08-01-12345",
    }

# ClickUp | Hivel

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/clickup#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Clickup

1.  You must have a ClickUp user account that is part of the Workspace(s) you want Hivel to access.
    
2.  Scope of access: The PAT gives the same access as the ClickUp user who generated it, if that user is in multiple Workspaces, the PAT can access them. We recommend you to create a service account with all the permissions required to give hivel and use that account to integrate hivel
    
3.  The account used to create the PAT should be an admin for the Workspace(s) you want to integrate. This prevents permission issues when Hivel tries to access lists, tasks or other workspace resources.
    

Hivel

1.  The user whoever is integrating must have access to Hivel’s Integrations page and the permission to edit integration settings.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/clickup#step-by-step-generate-a-clickup-personal-access-token-pat)

Step-by-step: generate a ClickUp Personal Access Token (PAT)

These steps follow the ClickUp UI (versions 2.0 / 3.0 may differ slightly in avatar placement). If your ClickUp layout differs, look for Settings → Apps / ClickUp API.

1.  Log in to ClickUp with the account that will own the PAT.
    
2.  Click your avatar (top-right in ClickUp 3.0; lower-left in older versions).
    
3.  Choose Settings from the menu. In the left sidebar, click Apps (or ClickUp API in some UI versions).
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FxZki2YqZSmjpgCyHastY%252FScreenshot%25202026-01-20%2520at%25203.27.10%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28ca0ebc-7451-4a56-867e-dbb72d338025&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4334d996&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F4qkwrF4HrGWWdSyoDpvM%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8feb52d8-4079-487e-99d9-f48c55b54042&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b90b5d58&sv=2)

1.  Under API Token (or Personal API token), click Generate (or Generate / Create token).
    

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/clickup#undefined)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fz02D2DIHTaHKwyVdY2qr%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D940eebb3-5eca-40c1-a58a-b4b34ad86b39&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0c64d&sv=2)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  When the token appears, click Copy to copy the token to your clipboard. The token string typically starts with pk\_.
    
2.  Store the token securely, paste it into your password manager or Hivel immediately (see next section). ClickUp personal tokens never expire unless you regenerate or revoke them.
    

Note: If you cannot see the Apps/API Token section, confirm you are signed in with a non-guest account and that your ClickUp user has necessary permissions.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/clickup#how-to-insert-the-pat-into-hivel)

How to insert the PAT into Hivel

1.  Open Hivel and go to Settings → Integrations → ClickUp (or the project management area where ClickUp is listed).
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FNJU3LLL37n4lCfJD6Tkd%252FScreenshot%25202026-01-20%2520at%25203.32.21%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21adde02-d39e-4a97-9034-3a3366ab8bd5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17e7e072&sv=2)

1.  Copy paste the PAT into the ClickUp PAT input field.
    
2.  Click Integrate ClickUp. Hivel will validate the token by calling ClickUp APIs.
    
3.  After successful validation, Hivel will be able to authorize API calls on behalf of the ClickUp user who created the PAT (so ensure that user has access to all required Workspaces / Lists / Projects).
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Fjx5g5Z4k67PaBmPlk30N%252FScreenshot%25202026-01-20%2520at%25203.32.54%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De647e318-9f09-4ec6-af97-f7302352f5a1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5fbc2a3&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/project-management/clickup#how-to-reauthorize)

How to reauthorize


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Regenerate/revoke: If the token is compromised or you want to force re-authentication, regenerate or revoke it from ClickUp Settings → Apps → API Token and update Hivel with the new token.

# Best Practices for Ensuring Strong Pull Request Review Coverage | Hivel

Consistent, high-quality PR review coverage is one of the strongest leading indicators of engineering health. It reduces defect escape, improves knowledge sharing, and keeps delivery predictable as teams scale. This guide outlines proven strategies to ensure every Pull Request receives timely, meaningful review, followed by concrete steps teams can take using Hivel.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#improving-pr-review-coverage-actionable-strategies)

Improving PR Review Coverage: Actionable Strategies

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#id-1.-mandate-reviews-with-branch-protection)

1\. Mandate Reviews with Branch Protection

Make PR reviews a non-negotiable step in your delivery workflow by enforcing branch protection rules. This ensures no code reaches critical branches without at least one approved review.

Most modern SCMs support this natively:

*   **GitHub** Require pull request reviews before merging and define minimum approvers, dismissal rules, and status checks.
    
*   **Bitbucket** Enforce merge checks such as minimum reviewers, successful builds, and resolved tasks before merge.
    

Why this matters Branch protection removes ambiguity and social friction. Reviews are no longer optional or dependent on individual discipline. The system enforces the behavior consistently.

chevron-right**Links to branch protection rules and mandatory reviews across SCMs**[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#links-to-branch-protection-rules-and-mandatory-reviews-across-scms)

[_Approving a pull request with required reviews (GitHub Docs)_arrow-up-right](https://docs.github.com/articles/approving-a-pull-request-with-required-reviews)

[_About protected branches (GitHub Docs)_arrow-up-right](https://docs.github.com/repositories/configuring-branches-and-merges-in-your-repository/managing-protected-branches/about-protected-branches)

[_Merge request approval rules (GitLab Docs)_arrow-up-right](https://docs.gitlab.com/user/project/merge_requests/approvals/)

[_Protected branches (GitLab Docs)_arrow-up-right](https://docs.gitlab.com/user/project/repository/branches/protected/)

[_Code Owners (GitLab Docs)_arrow-up-right](https://docs.gitlab.com/user/project/codeowners/)

[_Branch Protection (Bitbucket)_arrow-up-right](https://support.atlassian.com/bitbucket-cloud/docs/use-branch-permissions/)

[_Branch Policies in Azure Repos_arrow-up-right](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/devops/repos/git/branch-policies?view=azure-devops)

[_About Pull Requests and Permissions (Azure DevOps)_arrow-up-right](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/azure/devops/repos/git/review-pull-requests?view=azure-devops)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#id-2.-encourage-optimal-pr-sizing)

2\. Encourage Optimal PR Sizing

Actively promote shipping smaller, focused Pull Requests. As a general guideline, aim to keep PRs under **400 lines of code** whenever possible.

**Why this matters** Smaller PRs are easier to reason about, faster to review, and less likely to accumulate review debt. Large PRs increase cognitive load, slow feedback loops, and often lead to superficial reviews or delays.

**Practical tactics:**

*   Break features into incremental, reviewable slices.
    
*   Separate refactors from functional changes.
    
*   Avoid bundling unrelated changes into a single PR.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#id-3.-implement-a-code-review-checklist)

3\. Implement a Code Review Checklist

Provide a standard checklist that both authors and reviewers follow for every PR. This creates consistency and reduces the chance of important items being missed.

**A strong checklist typically covers:**

*   Correctness and logic
    
*   Test coverage and test quality
    
*   Edge cases and error handling
    
*   Performance considerations
    
*   Security and access control
    
*   Documentation and comments
    

**Why this matters** Checklists reduce reliance on memory and reviewer experience alone. They help new reviewers contribute confidently and ensure quality standards are applied uniformly across teams.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#id-4.-formalise-review-responsibilities)

4\. Formalise Review Responsibilities

Make code review an explicit, scheduled responsibility rather than an ad-hoc activity.

**Effective approaches include:**

*   Reviewer rotations to distribute load fairly
    
*   Assigned primary reviewers per repository or code area
    
*   Clear ownership for critical paths and services
    

**Why this matters** When “everyone” is responsible for reviews, no one truly is. Clear accountability ensures PRs are picked up quickly and do not stall due to ambiguity.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#id-5.-foster-a-positive-review-culture)

5\. Foster a Positive Review Culture

Strong review coverage depends as much on culture as on process.

**Encourage:**

*   Constructive, respectful feedback
    
*   Recognition for high-quality reviews, not just code output
    
*   Lightweight gamification or shout-outs for consistent reviewers
    

**Why this matters** When reviews are seen as collaborative and valued, participation increases naturally. Teams move from defensive reviews to shared ownership of code quality.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#id-6.-integrate-ai-assisted-code-review)

6\. Integrate AI-Assisted Code Review

Where appropriate, introduce AI-powered code review tools to handle repetitive or low-level checks.

**Typical use cases:**

*   Identifying common anti-patterns
    
*   Flagging potential bugs or security issues
    
*   Suggesting refactors or style improvements
    

**Why this matters** AI tools free human reviewers to focus on higher-order concerns such as architecture, domain correctness, and long-term maintainability.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#steps-you-can-take-using-hivel)

Steps You Can Take Using Hivel

Hivel helps operationalize these best practices by making review coverage visible, measurable, and actionable.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#id-1.-surface-and-prioritise-open-prs)

1\. Surface and Prioritise Open PRs

Use Hivel to filter and surface PRs that are **Ready to Review**. This ensures reviewers focus on PRs that are unblocked and actively awaiting feedback, preventing important work from getting buried in long queues.

**Outcome** Reviewers spend less time searching and more time reviewing.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#id-2.-identify-review-bottlenecks-at-pr-and-team-level)

2\. Identify Review Bottlenecks at PR and Team Level

When reviews take longer than expected or PRs remain unreviewed, use Hivel’s metrics to diagnose the root cause. Key signals include:

*   Average PR size
    
*   Review cycle count
    
*   Number of review comments
    
*   Comment sentiment analysis
    

**Why this matters** Instead of guessing why reviews are slow, teams can pinpoint whether the issue is PR size, reviewer load, excessive back-and-forth, or unclear expectations, and take targeted corrective action.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#id-3.-track-review-coverage-with-dashboards)

3\. Track Review Coverage with Dashboards

Create shared or private dashboards in **Hivel** to track:

*   Review coverage
    
*   Review turnaround time
    
*   Team-level review participation
    

**Why this matters** Visibility drives behavior. When review metrics are visible, teams naturally course-correct and leadership can spot systemic issues early.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#id-4.-set-clear-review-goals)

4\. Set Clear Review Goals

**Define explicit goals for:**

*   Minimum PR review coverage
    
*   Target review turnaround time
    

Use Hivel to track progress against these goals over time and identify trends.

**Why this matters** Clear goals turn reviews from a vague expectation into a measurable practice, enabling continuous improvement rather than reactive fixes.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#closing-perspective)

Closing Perspective

Strong PR review coverage does not happen by accident. It emerges from a combination of enforced guardrails, clear ownership, healthy culture, and continuous visibility. By pairing SCM-level controls with Hivel’s insights, teams can move from reactive reviews to a predictable, scalable review system that improves both code quality and delivery velocity.

[PreviousWhat happens if there are too many Flashy Reviews and how to prevent them?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/what-happens-if-there-are-too-many-flashy-reviews-and-how-to-prevent-them)
[NextStrategies to Reduce Hotfix Resolution Timechevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/strategies-to-reduce-hotfix-resolution-time)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [Improving PR Review Coverage: Actionable Strategies](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#improving-pr-review-coverage-actionable-strategies)
    
*   [Steps You Can Take Using Hivel](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#steps-you-can-take-using-hivel)
    
*   [Closing Perspective](https://docs.hivel.ai/improve-performance/how-to-improve-quality/best-practices-for-ensuring-strong-pull-request-review-coverage#closing-perspective)

# Release Notes - October 2024 | Hivel

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-october-2024#whats-new-this-month)

What’s New This Month!

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-october-2024#introducing-private-dashboards)

Introducing private dashboards

Your dashboard, your rules! Now, private dashboards are fully visible only to their owners, while public dashboards remain viewable but locked down for other users. Plus, an 'Access' option lets owners toggle dashboard visibility between public and private as needed. Note: all current dashboards are set as public in production. [_Go ahead and give it a try!_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/dashboard/custom-dashboards)

Navigating just got easier with our organized side menu. All features are now conveniently grouped.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FERLQFvzA2nuXzzK1t8gh%252FGIF%2520Recording%25202024-10-30%2520at%252012.31.22%2520PM.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D119bf996-407a-46d7-a910-95d03fb1a0d3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=98f96ec7&sv=2)

See the big picture with updated parent-child team displays

For those working with hierarchical teams, we’ve updated how metrics reflect! Selecting a parent team now reveals all associated members—parent and sub-teams—across the app, and the metrics are aggregated across all the sub-teams. This ensures you have the full team picture wherever you need it. [_See it in action!_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/dashboard/cto)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-october-2024#team-owner-icons-and-new-permissions)

Team owner icons and new permissions

Spot your team owners at a glance! An icon now identifies team owners on the Teams page, ensuring transparency in team management. Note: team owners must transfer ownership before their team can be archived or deleted, keeping your team structure intact.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FiP75qi2lpS0t8UALFmnt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9046aab-2c0b-4d2f-bd75-a562d6eee6b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d9beb24&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-october-2024#user-merges-made-smarter)

User merges made smarter

We’ve made user merges smarter and more inclusive. Now, when multiple users are merged (e.g., User 1 into User 2, and then User 2 into User 3), the final user (User 3) will inherit team memberships and data from all prior merges across parent and sub-teams.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FT6CijPCjpbg9S2zgxYKl%252Fimage%2520%2829%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D23d18208-cc70-4e41-8264-61afaa25232e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bd44504&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-october-2024#phased-roll-out-fine-tune-your-pr-exclusions-with-new-one-to-one-option)

(Phased roll-out) Fine-tune your PR exclusions with new one-to-one option

We’ve introduced a new 'One to One' option in PR Exclusions, offering precise control over branch exclusions. Now, configure up to 10 unique source-destination branch pairs, which will exclude corresponding PRs from your metrics. Prefer the traditional setup? The existing 'Many to Many' feature remains unchanged, giving you flexibility to choose the best fit for your workflow. Configuration changes apply to data processed post-save.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FjCpSOR21XHvBQcVOAZue%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd036d1b-2d30-4c3a-93cb-f1c38e0e3967&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b93f70f&sv=2)

* * *

Take a moment to breathe🧘‍♀️! You’re all caught up, and it’s time for a well-earned coffee break ☕. See you next month!

# Jira On-Prem | Hivel

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/jira-on-prem#creating-a-personal-access-token-pat-in-jira)

Creating a Personal Access Token (PAT) in Jira

To integrate **Hivel** with **Jira**, you need to generate a **Personal Access Token (PAT)** for authentication. Below are the detailed steps for setting up the **service account** and generating the PAT in **Jira** for successful integration:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/jira-on-prem#prerequisites)

**Prerequisites**

*   **Jira Service Account**: Ensure you have a **service account** with **Site Admin** access to the Jira projects you want to analyze. This account will be used to fetch data from Jira for Hivel analysis.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/jira-on-prem#steps-for-integration)

**Steps for Integration**

**1\. Service Account Setup**

*   **Create a service account** in Jira if you don’t already have one.
    
*   Ensure this service account has **Site Admin access** to the required Jira projects you want Hivel to analyze.
    
*   The service account must have sufficient permissions to read data from the Jira projects, such as issue fields, access to all boards, and any other necessary information for analysis.
    

**2\. Generate Personal Access Token (PAT)**

To authenticate Hivel with Jira, you’ll need to generate a Personal Access Token (PAT). Follow these steps:

*   **Step 1**: Log in to your **Jira Service Account** and go to the following URL to manage your account settings: [Jira Account API Tokensarrow-up-right](https://id.atlassian.com/manage-profile/security/api-tokens)
    
*   **Step 2**: On the **API Tokens** page, click on **Create API token**.
    
*   **Step 3**: In the **Create API token** dialog:
    
    *   Enter a **label** for the token (e.g., "Hivel Integration").
        
    *   Click **Create** to generate the token.
        
    
*   **Step 4**: After the token is created, a new token will appear in the list. Click the **Copy** button to copy the token to your clipboard.
    
*   **Step 5**: Store this token securely, as it is the only time it will be shown. You will use this token to authenticate with Jira from Hivel.
    

Use the token to complete the next steps as shown on the Integration screen in Hivel.

[PreviousGitlab On-Premchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/gitlab-on-prem)
[NextSonarQube On-Premchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/sonarqube-on-prem)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Release Notes - September 2025 | Hivel

As we close Q3, Hivel’s been busy refining the details to make your day smoother. Say hello to faster integrations, cleaner data, and sharper visibility across teams!

This round of updates focuses on control, clarity, and helping you move into Q4 with momentum.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-september-2025#a-smarter-github-integration)

A Smarter GitHub Integration

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FXOW0PmSGfOzOnRZDHevb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ba7ee68-6816-46f9-84d9-0ec8a64211e8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a489a67&sv=2)

We’ve redesigned how Hivel connects with GitHub to give your org more flexibility and control. Admins can now choose between:

*   **OAuth**, for full workspace access.
    
*   **GitHub App**, for tighter control over selected repositories.
    

You can switch between the two anytime, and **new users will see OAuth as the default** setup, with the App mentioned under **Advanced Options**.

👉 [_Check it out_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/settings/integrations)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-september-2025#upgraded-teams-and-goals-pages)

Upgraded Teams & Goals Pages

We’ve officially moved to the upgraded Teams and Goals experience.

*   Teams and Users now have dedicated pages, giving you clearer visibility and the ability to drill down from team → sub-team.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252Frn5Rov7SARcWxDOqjOhg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8337b03d-f655-44d1-b433-19d85750dae3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e917ff40&sv=2)

*   Goals PRO is now the default for new users, offering a more focused view for setting objectives and tracking outcomes.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FpVO0jJ7hAlClEEepcVUd%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-08%2520at%25206.22.38%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa2a93de-f059-48ef-854a-46d475b254dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=709771b9&sv=2)

The older Goals view will be deprecated within this week.

👉 [_Explore it now_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/dashboard/goals)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-september-2025#labels-organize-beyond-teams)

Labels - Organize Beyond Teams

Introducing **Labels**, a new way to tag and organize users beyond just team structures.

Add labels like Location, Skill Proficiency, or Product Line, and use them to filter dashboards and reports for more flexible insights.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FVTU4le8lK6fb4FS13qFa%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-09%2520at%252010.15.29%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b38f7a0-c33a-4632-8275-285182f5df2b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af66a3b3&sv=2)

👉 [_Try it out_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/settings/labels)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-september-2025#repo-exclusion-focus-on-what-matters)

Repo Exclusion – Focus on What Matters

You can now **exclude repositories directly from Hivel** (up to ten per organization).

All related commits and PRs will automatically be excluded from your analytics, keeping your reports focused on active, relevant work.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FgnSgogKI69YGMv0XeLcj%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-09%2520at%252010.17.08%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6ae8ce8-f26c-4cd0-bd0c-72e792aa66b8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bbc77275&sv=2)

👉 [_Try it out_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/settings/repos)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-september-2025#smarter-pr-auto-exclusions)

Smarter PR Auto-Exclusions

You can now auto-exclude PRs based on **Cycle Time**, **PR Size**, or **Keyword Patterns**, in addition to the existing branch and commit filters.

All exclusion settings now live under _Configuration → Exclusions_, where you can manage them for both orgs and teams.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FYyJqWd1mvDESrXjUzAdI%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-09%2520at%252010.19.52%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2ab99ee-62de-4ec2-b33d-bcccbad3515b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c645531d&sv=2)

👉 [_Check it out_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/settings/configuration)

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-september-2025#minor-upgrades-to-make-navigation-easier)

🔎 Minor Upgrades to Make Navigation Easier


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-september-2025#easier-metric-exploration)

Easier Metric Exploration

**Click on any metric chart from your Cockpit board**, and you’ll land on a detailed view of that metric’s trends.

Now, you can:

*   **Quickly switch metrics:** From the top of the metric detail page, you can now search and switch to any other metric instantly - no need to head back to the dashboard.
    
*   **View deeper drill-downs:** From the trend chart, you can now open commits and PRs directly for weekly and monthly date ranges (previously only available for daily).
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FrH6361Tj0XI10icEw8NH%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-09%2520at%252010.23.17%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daea73d8c-0d96-47dc-810b-0c0da34e4a25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=afdc8e5b&sv=2)

👉 [_Explore it now_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/dashboard/custom-dashboards)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-september-2025#smoother-navigation-across-hivel)

Smoother Navigation Across Hivel

**Clicking on the Hivel logo** now takes you exactly where you expect — your personal default page, your admin’s org default, or your dashboards.

It’s a small update, but it makes getting around a little simpler every time.

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-september-2025#wrapping-up-september)

☕ Wrapping Up September

We’re ending Q3 with updates curated for better performance, flexibility, and visibility. Expect even more depth around AI-driven insights and engineering impact during the last leg of the year.

Stepping into the Q4 requires a mix of focus and balance. Take a breather, stretch, and gear up for the next chapter. The best results come when effort meets a little downtime! 😉

Here's to a productive and well-paced quarter! 🍻

# Release Notes - August 2025 | Hivel

"_And so it was foretold, that in the ninth month, features of immense power would arrive. But let us not forget the eighth - August - whose quiet strength laid the groundwork for what’s to come."_

Herein lies the tale of August’s contributions...

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-august-2025#commit-frequency-metric)

Commit Frequency Metric

Say hello to **Commit Frequency** – our newest Git metric that calculates the _average number of commits per developer per day_. It gives a sharper lens into engineering rhythm and behavior, derived from our core Commits metric. You’ll find it across **All Git Metrics**, **Throughput Board templates**, and **Dev360** views.

Heads up: Graph values will typically hover around 0 or 1 – it’s all about daily averages per developer.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FnGLMMVG6aZPU59PIBZws%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D608b801d-295e-45f2-b6a0-69cab7556682&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a7ab071&sv=2)

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FIlsMneiaxWYUc3XY3GAa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fcac296-414f-4d7b-aff9-1ecaf0b6de51&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1806f6fd&sv=2)

👉 [_Check it out_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/overview/commit-frequency)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-august-2025#persistent-filters-in-investment-screen)

Persistent Filters in Investment Screen

Boards, Sub-boards, and Sprints selections now **persist** across all 5 tabs of the Investment screen. No more reapplying filters on every visit - they stay put until you refresh or log out.

👀 Coming soon: Saved Filters to make your views even smarter.

👉 [Investment Screenarrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/dashboard/investment-profile)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-august-2025#enhanced-release-cycle-filters)

Enhanced Release Cycle Filters

We’ve revamped how Release Cycles behave across the platform:

*   Default cycles always appear first.
    
*   Others are sorted by their proximity to today.
    
*   Future-only cycles are now hidden (unless you're configuring).
    
*   If a cycle spans past/future dates, data shows _only up to today_.
    
*   In **Cockpit Dashboards**, your saved filters always take precedence.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FgBdE5kVGrdOPhN42kKjI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D718f72e4-07e8-41a0-a3a4-3f95595fc416&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f2a77f2&sv=2)

[_Also check out last month's notes to see how you can see trends over sprints/release cycles._](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-october-2024)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-august-2025#smarter-default-landing-pages)

Smarter Default Landing Pages

Admins and Execs can now set default landing pages for their teams via Configuration. This update respects user preferences while giving org-wide control. The priority works like this:

1.  **User session** setting (existing behavior)
    
2.  **Admin-configured** landing page
    
3.  Default fallback → **Dashboards (All Boards)**
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252F9qUbQblo1MiOCYk5AYoD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4d41cf0-727f-42c4-b540-1c06c8a82c74&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10398abd&sv=2)

👉 [_Here is where you can set it up_arrow-up-right](https://app.hivel.ai/settings/configuration)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/release-notes/release-notes-august-2025#downloadable-cockpit-graphs)

Downloadable Cockpit Graphs

You can now **download graphs** in .png format from the Cockpit screen, per metric - perfect for sharing insights outside the platform.

👤 Unmerge User via UI

The new **Unmerge** feature on the UI lets you isolate a user from their merged chain. You can select one or multiple merged users in the Teams page, and once the users are unmerged, all the accounts chained together will be separated.

# How to reauthorize Github with a classic token? | Hivel

To ensure that personal repositories are not integrated with Hivel, it’s important to use a dedicated service account. Follow the steps below to reauthorize GitHub with a service account:

**Step-by-Step Guide**

1.  Make sure you have a dedicated service account on GitHub with access to the necessary repositories.
    
2.  Use the credentials for the service account to log into GitHub.
    
3.  Click on the profile icon located at the top-right corner of the GitHub page.
    
4.  From the dropdown menu, select **Settings**.
    
5.  In the left-hand sidebar of the settings page, scroll down and click on **Developer settings**.
    
6.  Under Developer settings, select **Personal access tokens**.
    
7.  Choose **Tokens (classic)** to proceed.
    
8.  Click on **Generate new token**.
    
9.  For the token type, select **Classic**.
    
10.  Name: Add name as "Hivel".
    
11.  Expiration: Select No expiration date. (You can revoke the token once the integration is no longer needed).
    
12.  Ensure the following scopes are selected to provide necessary access:
    
    1.  **repo**: (all scopes)
        
    2.  **org:** (only "read:org")
        
    3.  **hooks:** (all scopes)
        
    4.  **user:** (only "read:user" and "user:email")
        
    
13.  Once the token is generated, copy it immediately. You will not be able to see it again once you leave the page. Share the following information with Hivel to complete the integration:
    
    *   Personal Access Token
        
    *   Username
        
    *   Email
        
    

By following these steps, you can reauthorize GitHub with a service account, ensuring a secure and efficient setup for Hivel integration. For further assistance, contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#afdcdadfdfc0dddbefc7c6d9cac381cec6)
.

[PreviousHow to create Github fine-grained token for Hivel Integration?chevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/github/alternate-methods/how-to-create-github-fine-grained-token-for-hivel-integration)
[NextGitlabchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/gitlab)

Last updated 7 months ago

# Creating a Bitbucket App Password | Hivel

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/creating-a-bitbucket-app-password#id-1.-access-the-app-password-creation-page)

1\. Access the App Password Creation Page

*   Log in to your Bitbucket account
    
*   Go to: [https://bitbucket.org/account/settings/app-passwords/newarrow-up-right](https://bitbucket.org/account/settings/app-passwords/new)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/creating-a-bitbucket-app-password#id-2.-enter-basic-details)

2\. Enter Basic Details

*   In the "Label" field, enter a descriptive name (e.g., "Hivel" or another name that describes the purpose)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/creating-a-bitbucket-app-password#id-3.-set-permissions)

3\. Set Permissions

Select the following permissions:

Account:

*   ✓ Email Read
    
*   ✓ Read
    

Workspace membership:

*   ✓ Read
    

Repositories:

*   ✓ Read
    

Pull requests:

*   ✓ Read
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/creating-a-bitbucket-app-password#id-4.-create-the-password)

4\. Create the Password

*   Click the blue "Create" button at the bottom left
    
*   Bitbucket will generate a secure password
    

circle-exclamation

**IMPORTANT:** Copy this password immediately and store it securely - it will only be shown once

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/creating-a-bitbucket-app-password#id-5.-using-your-app-password)

5\. Using Your App Password

*   Use this password along with your Bitbucket username when authenticating with the API
    
*   The app password will have only the permissions you've selected
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcYMXTH732mvQZJatEXptiw4bfzxZ7mwl6n8xGqWzgRgvvOQoynRcBzaNJ_dpQMoIbXsNGh7PKJRJH1lmpXNqzDArNuzyM3_nc-j5wpHcHcwO_JTtSA9sfFz9VZvF2AWncn0ZGseg%3Fkey%3DKDoRtP05NudNy6wIntOgxSbd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55c48ae3&sv=2)

[NextOn-Prem Outlook Integrationchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/on-prem-outlook-integration)

Last updated 10 months ago

*   [1\. Access the App Password Creation Page](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/creating-a-bitbucket-app-password#id-1.-access-the-app-password-creation-page)
    
*   [2\. Enter Basic Details](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/creating-a-bitbucket-app-password#id-2.-enter-basic-details)
    
*   [3\. Set Permissions](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/creating-a-bitbucket-app-password#id-3.-set-permissions)
    
*   [4\. Create the Password](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/creating-a-bitbucket-app-password#id-4.-create-the-password)
    
*   [5\. Using Your App Password](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/creating-a-bitbucket-app-password#id-5.-using-your-app-password)

# Gitlab On-Prem | Hivel

To integrate **Hivel** with **GitLab**, you'll need to create a **Personal Access Token (PAT)** for authentication. Below are the detailed steps to generate the token in GitLab:

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/gitlab-on-prem#steps-to-create-a-personal-access-token-pat-in-gitlab)

**Steps to Create a Personal Access Token (PAT) in GitLab**

**1\. Access User Settings**

*   **Log in** to your **GitLab** account.
    
*   In the top-right corner of the screen, click on your **profile icon**.
    
*   From the dropdown menu, select **"Preferences"** to access your account settings.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXemfL102epMWT8llITWbQhS7GSrDkt6cRkiF6IDUrgTgdQroCSuYYtGQ4a62KUe_ir_6iP_-iZOzGxKyLg3MOB7BW4KVSQpu3c7n5i99DCus3lNqRbNldbHZZTWYBgIAQJ6hskMEw%3Fkey%3D3hJ1ramI-10wlNgIdI5NQFuy&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=231932b0&sv=2)

**2\. Navigate to Access Tokens**

*   In the left sidebar, scroll down and find **"Access tokens"** under the **"Access"** section.
    
*   Click on **"Access tokens"** to open the token generation page.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdU8E_ZlES5KHJLx3jp8ATP9ZALqMXbEyFa14NdblRl2wrs2tAb73x0kV6LuoKSa0lI0JPvgDN2WYcvao6l2u1sJGwUgBEzaS5HZsurgs3uab9Lh_qTYgYaosFAVRZ3-_7PlaUtIw%3Fkey%3D3hJ1ramI-10wlNgIdI5NQFuy&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91ee6043&sv=2)

**3\. Enter Token Details**

*   **Name**: Enter a name for your token. It is recommended to use something descriptive, like **"Hivel"**, for easy identification.
    
*   **Description**: This is optional, but you can add a description to help identify the token's purpose.
    
*   **Expiration Date**: Set an expiration date for the token if desired, or leave it blank for **no expiration**.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcEdDs0conc10Qj52nF6J9eS0kUtvCGHWhnH6VWtdMJpW9NtmXLUAqrLW1o-KG03bVOOYl41X4_Lmaj_daxQD4L9r0L-0DsIIDWxbyhLSVxnfZyhN7rfp-SqC2IKbgAdAu08TN17w%3Fkey%3D3hJ1ramI-10wlNgIdI5NQFuy&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=940be711&sv=2)

**4\. Select Required Scopes**

*   To enable **Hivel** to interact with your GitLab instance, check the following required scopes:
    
    *   **read\_api**: To read data from the GitLab API.
        
    *   **read\_user**: To read user information.
        
    *   **read\_repository**: To access repository data.
        
    

**5\. Create the Token**

*   After entering the details and selecting the necessary scopes, click on the **"Create personal access token"** button.
    

**6\. Save the Token**

*   Once the token is created, **copy the generated token** immediately and store it in a secure location.
    
*   **IMPORTANT**: This is the **only time** the token will be displayed, so make sure to copy it before leaving the page.
    

Use the token to complete the next steps as shown on the Integration screen in Hivel.

[PreviousApplication Setup Guide: User Sign-up and Integrationchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/application-setup-guide-user-sign-up-and-integration)
[NextJira On-Premchevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/jira-on-prem)

Last updated 1 month ago

# SonarQube On-Prem | Hivel

Integrating SonarQube with Hivel enhances the quality and security of your codebase by enabling continuous code inspection and quality monitoring. SonarQube helps detect bugs, vulnerabilities, and code smells, ensuring that your software projects maintain high standards of code quality. By following the steps outlined below, you can seamlessly connect SonarQube to Hivel, allowing for efficient code quality management within your platform.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/sonarqube-on-prem#h_01j3f1mcmbfjzaqwgecz0qnyxy)

Step - 1: Whitelist Necessary IP Addresses

For a secure and uninterrupted connection, make sure to whitelist the following IP addresses:

*   **Mandatory IPs**:
    
    *   107.23.139.76
        
    *   3.219.89.23
        
    
*   **Recommended, but Optional IPs**:
    
    *   45.119.114.218
        
    *   183.82.116.218
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/sonarqube-on-prem#h_01j05wwnfdzyph27b08y79h4sp)

Step - 2: Generate an Access Token in SonarQube

1\. Log in to your SonarQube account.

2\. Click on the name icon located in the top right corner.

3\. Select "**My Account**" from the dropdown menu.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FqsiPxfaJ5nBD2p9ciXBc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21858d36-722f-4efb-a690-38777760f6a7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2b8d6d67&sv=2)

4\. Navigate to the "**Security**" tab.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FLLgNSaSrjUfnKjuzVC6s%252Fimage%2520%2850%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75fbae5e-2b2e-4091-bef2-6022836857c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=466c297&sv=2)

5\. Go to Generate a token.

6\. Enter a token name, preferably "Hivel".

7\. Click on the "**Generate**" button.

8\. Copy the generated token and save it securely.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FLiR1AYc9cVS3GN9pgp0y%252Fimage%2520%2852%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2616e8f-dcbb-42bd-829c-facfc9c446e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f123a92&sv=2)

9\. Copy the URL from the address bar of your SonarQube server and save it.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FkZuNGgsuSxm132LPrZl6%252Fimage%2520%2853%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6798198-154b-4711-9890-095828dddbfd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4baa71c6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/on-prem-setup/sonarqube-on-prem#h_01j05wwnfd5tgn2061q6h8yasv)

Step - 3: Connecting SonarQube to Hivel

1\. Log in to the Hivel Platform.

2\. Go to "**Settings**".

3\. Select "**Integrations**" from the settings menu.

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FCiJ93Z09qbJC4O6WqtZt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd06beb6-c9c7-44cf-a7b9-9ca60827ce25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=62794edb&sv=2)

4\. Find the SonarQube card and click on "**Connect**".

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FxqC8hz6rkTAJJLnxpQPY%252Fimage%2520%2858%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a8d50e3-fa4a-406c-a92e-5a73f08b00a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef3b64df&sv=2)

5\. **Fill in the required details:**

*   **SonarQube URL:** Enter the SonarQube server URL you copied earlier.
    
*   **Access Token:** Enter the access token you generated in SonarQube.
    

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FpdKCJPJtp0CjgCTkEZw0%252Fimage%2520%2857%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D122306cf-5403-4e7c-9152-fd1c83d52376&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a72e2b&sv=2)

6\. **Click on Submit.**

![](https://docs.hivel.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3057781534-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5KAIOUWph0JLSgQqbzyT%252Fuploads%252FmInY4BsqJTXqYRKqU7UL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db748cc6b-9b7e-4900-bbf7-9dce88afd754&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e85a164&sv=2)

By following these steps, you should successfully connect your SonarQube instance to Hivel. If you encounter any issues or need further assistance, please reach out to the Hivel support team at [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.hivel.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#394a4c4949564b4d7951504f5c55175850)
.

# Validation at a metric level for BitBucket | Hivel

**Purpose:** To validate the accuracy of key engineering productivity metrics shown in Hivel by manually cross-checking with raw data from Bitbucket for a selected developer.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

*   Access to the Bitbucket repository and Bitbucket UI with permission to view pull requests, commits, and reviews.
    
*   Access to the Hivel platform with permissions to view the developer's metrics.
    
*   Basic familiarity with Bitbucket's interface (Pull Requests, Commits, and Activity tabs).
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#metrics-definitions)

Metrics Definitions

Metric Name

Definition

**Cycle Time**

Time from first commit to PR merged.

**Coding Time**

Time from first commit until PR is opened.

**Review Time**

Time from PR opened until PR is reviewed.

**PR > 400 LoC**

Number of PRs with more than 400 lines of code changed.

**PRs merged without review**

PRs merged that have no recorded review state.

**MTTR (Mean Time to Repair)**

Average cycle time for production issue fixes identified by 'hotfix' label or title.

**Deployment Frequency**

How often code is released — number of PRs merged to main/master per time period.

**Active Days**

Average number of days with any activity per engineer.

**Flashy Reviews**

PRs that have a review time under 5 minutes.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#step-by-step-validation-process-for-one-developer)

Step-by-Step Validation Process for One Developer

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#identify-the-developer-and-time-period)

Identify the Developer and Time Period

*   In Bitbucket, locate the developer by username or email.
    
*   Filter PRs and commits to only those authored by this developer within the validation time period.
    
*   **Ensure to select a shorter time period e.g. a week or 3 days to get a limited amount of data to cross-check with BitBucket.**
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#id-1.-validate-cycle-time)

1\. Validate Cycle Time

**On Hivel:** Go to Pull Request screen and filter out the team, developer, and time frame for the list of merged PRs in that duration.

Go to Cockpit to look at the average Cycle time for the same filters, once validated for each PR on BitBucket.

(follow the same above steps to filter on Hivel for time related metrics)

**On Bitbucket:**

*   For each PR by the developer:
    
    *   Identify the timestamp of the **first commit** included in the PR.
        
    *   Identify the timestamp when the PR was **merged**.
        
    *   Calculate the difference (merge time - first commit time).
        
    
*   Calculate the average of these differences across all PRs in the period.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#id-2.-validate-coding-time)

2\. Validate Coding Time

**On Bitbucket:**

*   For each PR:
    
    *   Find the time of the first commit in the PR.
        
    *   Find the time when the PR was **opened**.
        
    *   Calculate the difference (PR opened time - first commit time).
        
    
*   Calculate the average coding time.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#id-3.-validate-review-time)

3\. Validate Review Time

**On Bitbucket:**

*   For each PR:
    
    *   Note the time when the PR was **opened**.
        
    *   Find the time of the **first approval**.
        
    *   Calculate the difference (first review time - PR opened time).
        
    
*   Average this across all PRs.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#id-4.-validate-prs-greater-than-400-lines-of-code)

4\. Validate PRs > 400 Lines of Code

**On Hivel:**

Go to Pull Request screen and filter out the team, developer, time frame, and PRs > 400 LoC - for the list of large merged PRs in that duration.

**On Bitbucket:**

*   Filter all PRs merged by the developer in that time period.
    
*   For each PR, check the number of lines changed.
    
    *   BitBucket recommends running this command line to fetch the PR size
        
        *   "git fetch origin pull/PR\_ID/head:pr-branch git diff --stat main...pr-branch"
            
        *   Replace `PR_ID` and `main` with the appropriate PR number and base branch.
            
        
    
*   Count how many PRs exceed 400 lines changed.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#id-5.-validate-prs-merged-without-review)

5\. Validate PRs Merged Without Review

**On Hivel:**

Go to Pull Request screen and filter out the team, developer, time frame, and click on Unreviewed PRs - for the list of PRs merged without review in that duration.

**On Bitbucket:**

*   Filter out a small time period.
    

1.  **List Merged PRs:**
    
    *   Go to the repository's _Pull Requests_ page.
        
    *   Set the filter to show only "Merged" PRs.
        
    
2.  **Check Approval Status:**
    
    *   Open each merged PR.
        
    *   In the PR details, look for the "Reviewers" section. If there are no approvals listed, the PR was merged without approval.
        
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#id-6.-validate-mttr-mean-time-to-repair)

6\. Validate MTTR (Mean Time to Repair)

**On Hivel:**

Go to Pull Request screen and filter out the team, developer, time frame, and click on MTTR tile - for the list of CFR PRs and their respective MTTR.

**On Bitbucket:**

*   Identify PRs labeled with “hotfix” or similar (e.g., title contains "hotfix", "bugfix", "urgent").
    
*   Calculate cycle time for each hotfix PR (first commit to merge).
    
*   Average these times.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#id-7.-validate-deployment-frequency)

7\. Validate Deployment Frequency

**On Hivel:**

Go to Pull Request screen and filter out the team, developer, time frame, and click on Deployment Frequency tile.

**On Bitbucket:**

*   Go to the repository's **Pull Requests** page.
    
*   Filter by:
    
    *   State: **Merged**
        
    *   Author: The developer's username
        
    *   Destination branch: master or main
        
    
*   The UI does **not** support filtering by date, so you must manually count PRs merged in your time window by checking their merge dates
    
*   Count the total number of PRs merged into the master or main branch during the selected time period.
    
*   Calculate deployment frequency as:
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#id-8.-validate-active-days)

8\. Validate Active Days

**On Hivel:**

Go to Dev360 screen and filter out on the time period and developer to get a summary of GIT activity done by the developer.

**On Bitbucket:**

*   Identify all days where the developer had any activity:
    
    *   Commits, Merge Commits, PR opened, PR reviewed, PR merged, PR declined.
        
    
*   **Repository Commits and PRs:** You can manually filter commits and pull requests by author in the repository view, then check the dates to see which actions occurred during the week.
    
*   **Local Git Logs:** By cloning the repository and using `git log` or `git shortlog` filtered by author and date, you can see a developer’s commit activity for the week.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#id-9.-validate-flashy-reviews)

9\. Validate Flashy Reviews

**On Bitbucket:**

*   For each PR, calculate review time (first review - PR opened).
    
*   Identify PRs with review time less than 5 minutes.
    
*   Count these PRs.
    

[PreviousBitBucket Integrationchevron-left](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/bitbucket-integration)
[NextAzurechevron-right](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/azure)

Last updated 8 months ago

*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#prerequisites)
    
*   [Metrics Definitions](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#metrics-definitions)
    
*   [Step-by-Step Validation Process for One Developer](https://docs.hivel.ai/integrations/scm/bitbucket/validation-at-a-metric-level-for-bitbucket#step-by-step-validation-process-for-one-developer)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    Deployment Frequency = Total PRs merged / Time period (in days)
